pīṭhamānam
atha pīṭhodayaṃ paścātthsānakasya viśeṣataḥ 
bhuvaṅgasya samaṃ vātha adhyarthaṃ triguṇaṃ tu vā  BhS 
paritaḥ pāvayorasya nītvāvai bhāgamaṅgulam

vakṣyāmi devyormānaṃ tatkaṇṭhāntaṃ nāsikāntakam 
hanvastaṃ bāhusīmāntaṃ nābhyantaṃ vādha kārayet  BhS 
caturdhaikāṃśakaṃ vāpi tṛtīyaikāṃśakaṃ tu vā

sadya āvirbhavedviṣṇuryatra bhaktānukaṃpayā

atha saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ

śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadharaṃ svarṇābhave va ca

uttamaṃ daśatālena mānonmānapramāṇataḥ  BhS

lakṣmīṃ sannyasya vāmorau mukhe harṣasamanvitām 
prasāritakarāṃ devīṃ pañcatālapramāṇataḥ  BhS 
prāñjalīkṛtahastāṃ tāṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitām 
vāmena tāṃ pariṣvajya dakṣiṇenābhayapradam  BhS 
anyābhyāṃ ca karābhyāṃ ca śaṅkhacakradharaṃ param

nāgabhoge samāsīnamevaṃ kuryāttu vā harim 
saptabhiḥ pañcabhirvāpi phaṇairvistāritairyutam  BhS 
śeṣaṃ samyakprakurvīta samuttuṅgaśarīriṇam 
mādhavaṃ cotpalanibhaṃ cakracāvagadāsibhiḥ  BhS 
caturbhujadharaṃ kuryāccitramālyāṃbaraṃ harim 
govindaṃ pāṇḍurābhaṃ ca caturbhujadharaṃ harim  BhS 
gadāśaṅkhāripadmāni bibhrantaṃ kārayedbudhaḥ 
viṣṇuṃ nīlotpalābhantu śaṅkhāryabjagadābhṛtam  BhS 
sarvābharaṇa saṃyuktaṃ pītavāsasamacyutam 
raktotpalābhaṃ kurvīta devaṃ tu madhusūdanam  BhS 
śaṅkhāryabjagadāpāṇiṃ caturbhujamanāmayam 
trivikramaṃ nīlavarṇaṃ śaṅkhāryabjagadābhṛtam  BhS 
caturbhujadharaṃ devaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam 
vāmanaṃ meghavarṇaṃ tu caturbāhuṃ mahābalam  BhS 
gadāśaṅkhāripadmāni bibhrantaṃ chalarūpiṇam 
atha vā kārayetkuṃbhaṃ dadhyannaṃ ca karadvaye  BhS 
dadhivāmanamāhustaṃ śvetābhaṃ dvibhujaṃ harim 
atha vā vaṭurūpaṃ tu dhṛtvā daṇḍakamaṇḍalū  BhS 
svarṇacchami bālarūpaṃ dvibhujaṃ kārayeddharim 
sitāsitābhaṃ kurvīta śrīdharaṃ tu caturbhujam  BhS 
kaumodakīśaṅkhacakrapadmadhāriṇamīśvaram 
hṛṣīkeśaṃ prakurvīta śyāmābhaṃ ca caturbhujam  BhS 
gadāśaṅkhāripadmāni bibhrantaṃ harimavyayam 
sitamecakavarṇantu padmanābhaṃ prakalpayet  BhS 
kaumodakīcakrapadmaśaṅkhapāṇiṃ ramādhavam 
dāmodaraṃ prakurvīta sitagaurābhamīśvaram  BhS 
padmaśaṅkhagadācakradharaṃ devaṃ caturbhujam 
saṃkarṣaṇaṃ tu kurvīta śvetavarṇaṃ caturbhujam  BhS 
śaṅkhāryabjagadāpāṇiṃ sarvādhāraṃ sanātanam 
vāsudevaṃ prakurvīta taruṇādityasannibham  BhS 
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadharaṃ sarvadharaṃ vibhum 
candrābhaṃ navakundābhamatha vā kālayeddharim  BhS 
pradyumnaṃ tu suvarṇābhaṃ kuryāddevaṃ caturbhujam 
cakraśaṅkhagadāpadmadharaṃ devaṃ mahābalam  BhS 
aniruddhaṃ hiraṇyābhaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam 
śaṅkhacakradhanuḥkhaḍgadharaṃ deveśvareśvaram  BhS 
sitāsitābhaṃ kurvīta deveśaṃ puruṣottamam 
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadharaṃ devaṃ caturbhujam  BhS 
athokṣajaṃ prakurvīta śaṅkhābhaṃ ca caturbhujam 
cakraśaṅkhagadāpadmadharaṃ bhūṣaṇabhūṣitam  BhS 
nārasiṃhaṃ tu meghābhaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam 
śaṅkhapadmagadācakradharaṃ bhaktābhayapradam  BhS 
sitamecakavarṇaṃ tu kurvīta vibhumacyutam 
gadābjacakraśaṅkhāṅkaṃ caturbhujavirājitam  BhS 
janārdanamudārāṅgaṃ nīlavarṇaṃ samācaret 
cakraśaṅkhagadāpadmadharaṃ devaṃ sanātanam  BhS 
atha vā kaṭivinyastavāmahastaṃ prakalpayet 
upendraṃ ghanakṛṣṇābhaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  BhS 
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadharaṃ devaṃ jagatprabhum 
hariṃ pāṇḍurakṛṣṇābhaṃ sarvālaṅkāraśobhitam  BhS 
śaṅkhapadmagadācakradharaṃ kuryānmanoharam 
kṛṣṇaṃ tu nīradaśyāmaṃ puṇḍarīkanibhekṣaṇam  BhS 
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadharaṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ 
sarveṣāṃ tu vimānāni viṣṇoruktavadācaret  BhS 
sabhyakuṇḍe pradhānāgnau hautraṃ tatra praśaṃsya ca 
keśavaṃ kleśasaṃhāraṃ viṣṇuṃ caiva parātparam'  BhS 
nārāyaṇaṃ naraṃ viṣṇuṃ narakāntaka' mityapi

govindaṃ paramānandaṃ viṣṇuṃ caiva sanātanam'

madhusūdanamudyogaṃ mahāntaṃ viṣṇu'mityapi 
trivikramaṃ trilokeśaṃ lokādhāraṃ sanātanam'  BhS 
vāmanaṃ varadaṃ caiva kāśyapiṃ cāditipriyam' 
śrīdharaṃ puruṣaṃ ceti viṣṇuṃ śrīvatsavakṣasam'  BhS 
hṛṣīkeśaṃ jagannāthaṃ viṣṇuṃ viśvamayaṃ' tathā 
padmanābhaṃ sureśaṃ ca viṣṇuṃ caiva jagatpatim'  BhS 
dāmodaraṃ sadādhāraṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇavarūpiṇam' 
saṃkarṣaṇaṃ yaduvaraṃ viṣṇuṃ haladhara'ntathā  BhS 
vāsudevaṃ puṇyamūrtiṃ bhadreśaṃ puṇyarūpiṇam' 
pradyumnaṃ jagadīśānaṃ viṣṇu puṇyātmakaṃ' tathā  BhS 
aniruddhaṃ mahāntaṃ ca vairāgyaṃ sarvatejasam' 
puruṣottamamānandaṃ viṣṇuṃ pañcātmakaṃ' tathā  BhS 
adhokṣajamanādiṃ ca viṣṇuṃ vyāpaka' mityapi 
nārasiṃhaṃ taponāthaṃ mahāviṣṇuṃ mahābalam'  BhS 
acyutaṃ cāparimitamaiśvaryaṃ śrīpatiṃ' tathā 
janārdanamanādyantaṃ viṣṇuṃ tejomayaṃ' tathā  BhS 
upendramindrāvarajaṃ viṣṇuṃ vaikuṇṭha'mityapi 
hariṃ pāpaharaṃ ceti viṣṇuṃ maṅgalavigraham  BhS 
kṛṣṇaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ puṇyaṃ tridaśādhipa'mityapi 
āvāhya tu krameṇaiva nirupyājyāhutīryajet  BhS 
viṣṇornukā'dabhiṣṣaḍbhiratodevā'dabhistathā 
keśavādidvādaśānāṃ mantrairdvādaśabhirhunet  BhS 
nārasiṃhasya kṛṣṇasya mantraḥ pūrvamudīritaḥ 
itareṣāṃ daśānāṃ tu daśamantrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  BhS 
viṣṇussarveṣā'mityādi yaṃ yajñai'rantamīritāḥ 
taṃ taṃ devaṃ samuddiśya tattanmantreṇa cātvaraḥ  BhS 
śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ hutvā śeṣaṃ pūrvavadācaret 
evaṃ sarvatra kurvīta devībhyāṃ sahitaṃ vibhum  BhS 
tadrūpaṃ kautukaṃ kuryātsarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam 
karṣaṇādikriyāssarvā viṣṇorina samācaret  BhS 
lakṣmīkalpaḥ
atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa lakṣmīsthāpanamuttamam 
aṣṭadhā procyate lakṣmīḥ prathamā tvanapāyinī  BhS 
viṣṇorvakṣasthsalekāryā sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutā 
dakṣastanasyordhvabhāge vahnyaśredivyamaṇḍale  BhS 
padmamadhye samāsīnāṃ padmadvayakarāñcitām 
varadābhayahastāṃ ca mandasmita mukhāṃbujām  BhS 
evaṃ rūpāṃ prakurvīta yogalakṣmīstusā matā 
yogalakṣmīṃ pratiṣṭhāpya śrīkāmassamyagarcayet  BhS 
deveśena samaṃ kuryādasyāsthcāpanamuttamam 
kālāntare prakuryāccheddhemarūpyādinā punaḥ  BhS 
kṛtvā śrīvatsarūpaṃ tu dhārayedviṣṇumavyayam 
tattadbiṃbānurūpaṃ ca kuryācchrīvatsalakṣaṇam  BhS 
bhogalakṣmyassamākhyātā śśrībhūnīlāḥ kramādimāḥ 
dhruvādiṣu tu bereṣu śrībhūmyau devapāśanvge  BhS 
vaikuṇṭhamārgasaṃcārā nīlā nityasamāśritā 
śrībhūmyosthsāpanaṃ pūrvaṃ deveśena sahoditam  BhS 
devībhyāṃ rahite deve kuryātkālāntare punaḥ 
pṛdhakpratiṣṭhāṃ śrībhūmyoḥ kuryādāṅgirasoktivat  BhS 
vīralakṣmīriti proktā pṛthagālayasaṃgatā 
alayāddakṣiṇe pārśvekuryāttu pṛthagālayam  BhS 
daśatālena mānena kuryāddevīna salakṣaṇām 
padmadvayakarāṃ caiva vandā bhayadhāriṇīm  BhS 
kirīṭamukucopetāṃ sarvālaṅkāraśobhitam 
padmāsane samāsīnāṃ hemābhāṃ sarvamaṅgalām  BhS 
godāmanyāṃ prakurvīta lakṣmīṃ tu vijayābhidhām 
navatāleṃ mānena kuryādanyālayāśritām  BhS 
dakṣiṇena tu hastena kalhāraṃ dadhatīṃ tathā 
prasāritetarakarāṃ baddhadhammillaśobhinīm  BhS 
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktāṃ tiṣṭhantīmeva kārayet 
godā bhūmyaṃśajā proktā tanmantreṇācaretkriyāḥ  BhS 
pākalakṣmīssamākhyātā pacanālayasaṃgatā 
aṣṭatālena mānena kuryāttāṃ pacanālaye  BhS 
padmadvayāñcitakarāṃ varadābhayadhāriṇīm 
āsīnāṃ vātha tiṣṭhantīṃ kuryādbhūṣaṇabhūṣitām  BhS 
dvitīya maṇḍapadvāre dvāralakṣmīṃ samācaret 
pataṅgapaṭṭikāmadhye sarvālaṅkāraśobhitām  BhS 
padmadvayāñcitakarāṃ varadābhayadhāriṇīm 
padmāsane samāsīnāṃ kirīṭādivibhūṣitām  BhS 
gajai tu pāśanvyoḥkuryāddhemakuṃbhakarau punaḥ 
siṃcantau tau mahālakṣmīṃ kuryātkuṃbhajalaistathā  BhS 
śrībhūmyorvīravijayalakṣmyoreva vidhīyate 
dhravaberānurūpeṇa berāntarasamarcanam  BhS 
tadrūpaṃ kautukaṃ kuryādutsavādi yathecchayā 
anyāsāṃnaiva kurvīta dhruvārcāmeva kārayet  BhS 
paiṇḍarīke pradhānāgnau hautraṃ tatra praśaṃsya ca 
śrībhūmyormūrtimantraiśca krameṇāvāhanādikam  BhS 
godāṃ kṛṣṇapriyāṃ lakṣmīṃ rukmiṇī'miti cāhvayet 
āvāhanakrameṇaiva tanmantrairjuhuyātkrarūt  BhS 
pratiṣṭhoktakrameṇaiva sarvaṃ pūrvavadācaret 
navaṣaṭpañcamūrtīnāṃ vimānasyālayasya ca  BhS 
dvimūrtisthāpanaṃ tadvatrimūrtasthāpanaṃ tathā 
anyeṣāṃ parivārāṇāṃ sthāpanaṃ vidhivaccaret  BhS 
yadyatsamarpyate vastu deveśasya tu mandire 
tattatsarvaṃ vidhānena pratiṣṭhāpya samarpayet  BhS 
asaṃskṛtaṃ tu na grāhyaṃ na taddevapriyaṃ bhavet 
bhūṣaṇāni ca vā sāṃsi pātrāṇyanyatparicchadam  BhS 
berālaṅkārayogyāni dhāmālaṅkaraṇāni ca 
yathāhaṃn saṃskṛtānyeva gṛhṇīyātsaphalaṃ bhavet  BhS

dravyādhidevatākalbassamyagukto mayākhile  BhS

saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
athāṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
bhagavadarcanam
atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa viṣṇorarcanamuttamam 
pravaḥ pāntama'ndhetyādi śrutibhirvihitaṃ tathā  BhS 
yaccoktaṃ guruṇā sūtre samāsena maharṣiṇā 
tenaiva vivṛtaṃ śāstre sārdhakoṭī pramāṇataḥ  BhS 
asmābhistu susaṃkṣiptaṃ cāturlakṣapramāṇataḥ 
tadarcanakramaṃ vakṣye śruṇudhvamṛṣisattamāḥ  BhS 
vaikhānasena sūtreṇa niṣekādi kriyānvitaḥ 
ṛtviguktaguṇopetassupuṣṭāṅgassamāhitaḥ  BhS 
gṛhastho brahmacārī vā bhaktyaivār'canamācaret 
dravyairanekaissaṃpādyaṃ tathānantopacārakaiḥ  BhS 
āśakyaṃ vidhivatkartuṃ brahmādyairapi pūjanam 
manuṣyaiḥkimuvaktavyaṃ daridrairadṛḍhātmabhiḥ  BhS 
yathāśakti tataḥ kuryāttasmādbahubhirarcakaiḥ 
bahubhiḥ paricāraiśca tathai vānyapadārthibhiḥ  BhS 
nirvartyaṃ pūjanaṃ viṣṇośśraddhābhaktisamanvitaiḥ 
tasmānnavavidhā grāhyā arcakāḥ paricārakāḥ  BhS 
uttame tūttamaṃ proktamarcakānāntu viṃśatiḥ 
aśītiḥ paricārāṇāmuttame madhyamaṃ tataḥ  BhS 
paricārāṇāṃ catuṣṣaṣṭidarcakāṣṣoḍaśa smṛtāḥ 
uttame tvadhamaṃ proktamarcakā dvādaśa smṛtāḥ  BhS 
pañcāśatparicārāśca madhyame cottamaṃ punaḥ 
catvāriṃśatparicarāḥ pūjakāścāṣṭakīrtitāḥ  BhS 
madhyame madhyamaṃ proktamacankāṣṣaḍudīritāḥ 
pañcaviṃśatparicarā madhyame tvadhamaṃ punaḥ  BhS 
catvāraḥ pūjakāstatra paricārāstu ṣoḍaśa 
trayor'cakāḥ paricarā nava syuradhamottame  BhS 
pūjakau dvauparicarāścatvāro 'dhamamadhyame 
ekor'cakaḥ paricarau dvauproktāvadhamādhame  BhS 
ācāryassyādupadraṣṭā devassānnidhyakārakaḥ 
arcanādyakhilaṃ kāryaṃ tanniyogena kārayet  BhS 
sa hi kāryasya nirṇetā goptādharmasyadeśikaḥ 
arcako devadevasya kuryānmantrāsanādiṣu  BhS 
upacārānanantāṃśca vidhinā śāstracoditān 
arcakasya sahāyantu kiṅkaraḥ paricārakaḥ  BhS 
bahukāryakarāścaite grāhyāstu paricārakāḥ 
sammājannakaraścaiva tathā syādupalepakaḥ  BhS 
dīpoddīpayitā cauva potraśodhanakārakaḥ 
pānīya vāhakaścaiva puṣpāpacayakārakaḥ  BhS 
dhūpadīpādikartā ca gandhapeṣaṇatatparaḥ 
tattatparicchadāhartā tathaiva balivāhakaḥ  BhS 
evamādīni kāryāṇi kurvanti paricārakāḥ 
pācakaḥ paricārassyātpacanālayasaṃgataḥ  BhS 
haviṣpākavidhānajñaśśaucācāraparāyaṇaḥ 
etānvaikhānasāneva vṛṇetsarvān padārthinaḥ  BhS 
alābhe tatra sarveṣāmācāryaṃ cārcakānpusaḥ 
vaikhānasāneva vṛṇannakyudaryādanyasūtriṇaḥ  BhS 
avaikhānasa viprastu pūjayedālaye harim 
sa vai devalako nāma sarva karmabahiṣkṛtaḥ  BhS 
paricārāṃntu vṛṇuyādalābhe tvanyasūtriṇaḥ 
dīkṣitānevasadvṛttānāgamoktavidhānataḥ  BhS 
yajamānassadādhyātmarato mokṣārthacintakaḥ 
dhanī sarvasamastyāgī bhaktiyuktaḥ prasannadhīḥ  BhS 
śāstroktena vidhānena viṣṇulāñchanalāñchitaḥ 
devasya nityapūjārthamutsavārthaṃ viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
tathānyavibhavārthaṃ ca dāpayeddhanasaṃcayam 
ācāryājñāpratīkṣassyātṝjake hitacintakaḥ  BhS 
paricāre prasannaśca kiṅkareṣu dayāparaḥ 
tīrthaprasādasevī ca nirmālyeṣu kṛtādaraḥ  BhS 
iti lakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ prabhavantyālayārcane 
athārcakaḥ pramannātmā pañcakālaparāyaṇaḥ  BhS 
brāhmemuhūrte codthāya nārāyaṇamanusmaret 
kṛtvā sūtroktavidhinā śaucādīni yathāvidhi  BhS 
snātvā snānavidhānena dhṛtvā dhautāṃbare punaḥ 
ūrdhvapuṇḍrāṇi saṃdhārya vidhinā keśavādibhiḥ  BhS 
dhṛtvā pavitrapadmākṣatulasīmaṇimālikāḥ 
dhṛtvobhayapavitre ca tathā sandhyāmupāsya ca  BhS 
uṣṇīṣeṇa ca pañcāgabhūṣaṇainsuvibhūṣitaḥ 
samāpya nityakarmāṇi mahāmantrādikaṃ japan  BhS 
aruṇaṃ tu japitvaiva nārāyaṇamataḥ param 
praṇamya yantrikāñcaiva karābhyāṃ parigṛhya ca  BhS 
bāhvośśirasi vā nyasya bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ 
saṃgataḥ paricāraiśca yajamānena sādaram  BhS 
sarvavādya samāyuktaḥ sarvamaṅgalaśobhitaḥ 
kramamāṇaśśanairvidvān devāgāraṃ prati vrajet  BhS 
pratadviṣṇu'riti procya cālayaṃ paritaḥkramāt 
yugmapradakṣiṇaṃ kuryāddeva devamanusmaran  BhS 
yugmapradakṣiṇaṃ kuryādayugmaṃ tvābhicārikam 
āyugmaṃ tu parītyāpi tathāyugmaṃ praṇamya ca  BhS 
prekṣetodyantamādityaṃ japeddvādaśasūktakam 
chāyālaṅghanadoṣantu na tatra syātpradakṣiṇe  BhS 
devāgāraṃ praviśyaiva tattanmantramanusmaran 
dvāradevān praṇamyātha nirastaṃ rakṣamastrataḥ  BhS 
gṛhītvā yantrikāṃ caiva hiraṇyapāṇi' muccaran 
kavāṭe tu susaṃyojya divaṃ' vīti samuccaran  BhS 
kavāṭodghāyanaṃ kṛtvā praviśedantaraṃ budhaḥ 
ato devā' itiprocya devaṃ vīkṣyapraṇamya ca  BhS 
paricārakamāhūya dīpānuddīpayetkramāt 
praṇavaṃ mantramuccārya tatra kāryaṃ samācaret  BhS 
trissaṃprahārya pāṇibhyāṃ śāmyantvi'tyādi coccaran 
ādarśaṃ gāśca kanyāśca hastyaśvādīn śubhodayān  BhS 
brāhmaṇānvedaviduṣo nartakāṃścaiva gāyakān 
devasya puratasthsāpya mukhamaṇḍapa evacā  BhS 
pracchanna paṭamudvāsya kṛtvā nīrājanaṃ tathā 
sarvavādyasamāyuktaṃ darśayeddharaye mudā  BhS 
dhāroṣṇaṃ caiva gokṣīraṃ navanītaṃ saśarkaram 
deveśāya nivedyātha kuryādyavanikāṃ punaḥ  BhS 
bhūḥ prapadye' samuccārya deveśaṃ praṇamenmuhuḥ 
paraṃ raṃ'hīti mantreṇa śayanasthaṃ śriyaḥpatim  BhS 
bhūrasī bhū'riti procya jīvasthāne niveśayet 
tasmin kāletu ye bhaktyā sevante puruṣottamam  BhS 
teṣāṃ puṇyaphalaṃ vaktuṃ na śakyaṃ tridaśairapi 
tataśśiṣyaṃ samāhūya vinayānvitamādarāt  BhS 
sammārjanādikarmāṇi gurustasmai samādiśet 
ava dhūti'miti procya garbhagehādi sarvataḥ  BhS 
mārjanyā mārjayecchiṣyaḥ prādakṣiṇyakrameṇa vai 
pāṃsvādīn parihṛtyāpi prākārāntaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ  BhS 
āśā'sviti samuccārya gomayenopalepayet 
pañcagavyaistu saṃprokṣya raṅgavallīssamācaret  BhS 
ā mā vājasya' mantreṇa yathoktena vidhānataḥ 
sarvaṇyapi ca pātrāṇi śodhayetsumanorame  BhS 
to yasaṃgrahaṇārthaṃ tu niyuktaḥ pūjakena tu 
ghaṭamādāya śiṣyastu duhatāṃ diva'muccaran  BhS

iti mantraṃ samuccārya bhaktyā paramāyā yutaḥ 
prātarāvāhitāṃ śaktiṃ dhruvabere 'varopayet  BhS

ato devā'dibhirmantrairmantrairanyaiśca vaiṣṇavaiḥ  BhS

atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa pūjanaṃ cautsavādiṣu

uttare kautukasyaiva baliberasya saṃsthitiḥ  BhS

tathaiva pākalakṣmyāśca dvāralakṣmyāśca kārayet  BhS

trivikramapratiṣṭhāyāṃ dhruvārcāmarcayettataḥ  BhS 
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre 'ṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ

bhagavadarcanam
ata ūrdhvaṃ dhruvārcāyām arcanaṃ saṃpravakṣyate 
mūrdhādi pīṭhātsannyastapuṣpādīnyapi śodhayet  BhS 
yogavīrārcanaṃ syāccettrikālaṃ snānamācaret 
prātarmadhyāhnayorvātha yogapīṭhedhruvār'canam  BhS 
bhogameva dhruvārcāyāṃ prātarmadhyāhna yorapi 
trikālaṃ vātha saṃsnāpya dhruvārcāyāṃ viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
vastrādīnyapi saṃśodhya puṣpanyāsaṃ ca pūrvavat 
śivādīnarcayitvātu pādapīṭhe samantataḥ  BhS 
tathāsanādyaissarvaiśca trisaṃdhyaṃ cārcayedbudhaḥ 
ardhayāme tu pūrvāntamarcayitvā ca pūrvavat  BhS 
havirni vedayeccaivānuktamasyacca pūrvavat 
āvāhanavisargau tuna kuryāditi śāsanam  BhS 
atha vakṣyer'canāntetu vidhānaṃ prati karmaṇām 
sauvarṇamuttamaṃ pātraṃ rājataṃ madhyame bhavet  BhS 
adhamaṃ tāmrapātraṃ tu trividhaṃ pātra mucyate 
tritālamuttamaṃ proktaṃ dvitālaṃ madhyamaṃ bhavet  BhS 
adhamaṃ tvekatālaṃ syāttrividhaṃ pātravistaram 
vistāreṇa samākhyātaṃ tayormadhyamamadhyamam  BhS 
tasya madhye tribhāgaikaṃ karṇikāṃgulamucchrayam 
pareto 'ṣṭadalaṃ kuryātkarṇikocchrayamānataḥ  BhS 
dvyaṅgulaṃ mūlanāhaṃ syāttadagraṃ tvardhanāhakam 
kiñcitphalāṃbujākāramagraṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ  BhS 
dviprasthataṇḍulaiḥ pakvamannaṃ tatraiva nikṣipet 
abhighārya ghṛtenaiva aṣṭāṃgulasamunnatam  BhS 
daśāṅgulaṃ vā utsedhaṃ dvādaśāṃgulamevavā 
tatpātrañca samādāya kautukāgre nidhāya ca  BhS 
kautukācchaktimādāya cārcayedaṣṭavigrahaiḥ 
parabrahmāṇa mityuktvā paramātmānamityapi  BhS 
bhaktavatsalaṃ yogeśaṃ' caturmūrtibhirarcayet 
prātaḥpuṣpabaliṃ kuryānmadhyāhnennabaliṃ tathā  BhS 
sāye tvarghyabaliṃ kuryātpūrvameva pracoditam 
taṇḍulaiḥ kuḍubaiścāpi yathālābhamathāpi vā  BhS 
śrutaṃ cārghyabaliṃ kuryātpuṣbaṃ tu caturaṅgulam 
śiṣyamāhūya tatkāle soṣṇīṣaṃ sottarīyakam  BhS 
śiṣyaṃ garuḍa vatsmṛtvā pātramuddhṛtyatatra vai 
udutya'miti mantreṇa śiṣyastacchirasi nyaset  BhS 
pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ kuryātkur yācchabdaravairyutam 
vitānachatrasaṃyuktaṃ piñchacāmarasaṃyutam  BhS 
dhūpadīpasamāyuktaṃ śanaiḥkuryātpradakṣiṇam 
pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā praviśedālayaṃ bhudhaḥ  BhS 
bhūtapīṭhāntare tiṣṭhedgṛhṇīyāttu tadarcakaḥ 
kautukāgretu sannyasya oṅkāreṇa niveśayet  BhS 
balyagraṃ khaṇḍayitvātu seneśāya nivedayet 
taccheṣaṃ sodakaṃ caiva bhūtapīṭhe tu nikṣipet  BhS 
utsavaṃ kartukāmaścettrisaṃdhiṣvevamuttamam 
sāyaṃ prātarmadhyamaṃ syātsāyaṃ caivādhamaṃ bhavet  BhS 
baliṃ ca baliberaṃ vā kārayediti ke ca na 
balyarthaṃ klaptadevasya cordhvamānamudāhṛtam  BhS 
mahāberasya hastena caikaviṃśatikāṃgulam 
saptadaśāṅgulaṃ vidyāddvādaśāṃgulameva vā  BhS 
śreṣṭhamadhyakaniṣṭhāni trividhaṃ mānamācaret 
arcāberatribhāgai kamuttamapratimābhavet  BhS 
tanmānasya daśāṃśena tvekonaṃ madhyamaṃ bhavet 
madhyamasya daśāṃśena tvekonamadhamaṃ bhavet  BhS 
mahato mūlaberasya mukhāyāmaṃ praśasyate 
balyarthaṃ pratimāṃ kuryātsarveṣāṃ sthāpanaṃ bhavet  BhS 
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ śreṣṭhamadhyamagauṇataḥ 
ratnajapratimāṃ kuryānmānonmānaṃ na vidyate  BhS 
uṣṇīṣaṃ golakaṃ jñeyaṃ śiromānaṃ trimātrakam 
keśāntārcā samaṃ bhāgaṃ saṃgamātpuṭasūtrakam  BhS 
puṭasūtrāddhanuparyantamekamekantu bhāgaśaḥ 
galamardhāṅgulaṃ vindyānmātrārdhaṃ grīvamucyate  BhS 
hikkāhṛdayaparyantaṃ mukhaṃ mātrādhikaṃ bhavet 
hṛdayaṃ nābhi tathaivoktaṃ tadadhastāttu tatsamam  BhS 
ūrū ca dvimukhāyāmaṃ golakotsedhamiṣyate 
caraṇaṃ jānumānaṃ ca kālāyapurato param  BhS 
hikkāsūtrādadhastāttu bāhudvimukhanetrakam 
prakoṣṭhaṃ mukhabandhaṃ ca mukhamardhādhikaṃ bhavet  BhS 
maṇibandhāṅgulasyāgre mukhayāmaṃ praśasyate 
caturbhujaṃ ca kṛtvā tu mānamevamudāhṛtam  BhS 
vakuryātpadmākāraṃ tu golakam 
atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa haviṣpākaṃ vidhānataḥ  BhS 
paktvā vittānusāreṇa havīṃṣyapi ca kalpayet 
alpe mahati vā tulyaṃ phalamāḍhyadaridrayoḥ  BhS 
nivedayitvā deveśaṃ kalyāṇaṃ kārayedbudhaḥ 
avadatvā ghṛtaṃ yattu kalyāṇamaśubhāyavai  BhS 
alābhe caiva sarveṣāṃ vrīhīṇāṃ taṇḍulāṃ ḥs tathā 
śatadvayaṃ pañcaviṃśadvrīhibhiḥ pūritaṃ tu yat 
śuktimātramiti khyātaṃ mānaṃ tenaiva kārayet  BhS 
taddvayaṃ tilamityuktaṃ prakuñcaṃ syāttiladvayam

yajamānecchayātattanmaṇḍapena sahaiva tu 
ṣoḍaśastaṃbhasaṃyuktaṃ dvādaśastaṃbhamevavā  BhS 
bhaktiyuktaṃ prakalpyaiva prapāṃ yuktyaiva kārayet 
apare dvārasaṃyuktaṃ pūrvavat staṃbhameva vā  BhS 
kavāṭaṃ tatra vā kuryāccheṣaṃ yaktyaiva kārayet 
śilpaśāstroktamārgeṇa śilpibhiḥ kārayedbudhaḥ  BhS 
maṇḍapasya samāptautu aṅkurānarpayetkramāt 
śuddhyarthaṃ vāstuhomaṃ ca puṇyāhaṃ caiva kārayet  BhS 
brāhmaṇān bhojayetpaścāttaddeśamupalakṣayet 
carodaye ca nakṣatre sthirarāśiṃ pragṛhya ca  BhS 
maṇḍapasya tu madhye vai dhānyapīṭhāni kalpayet 
pratiṣṭhoktakrameṇaiva kuṃbhanyāsāti kārayet  BhS 
paścime gārhapatyāgnāvāghāraṃ juhuyātkramāt 
hotā hautrakrameṇaiva hautraṃ tatra praśaṃsayet  BhS 
tattaddevasya cāvāhya juṣṭākāraṃ hutaṃ caret 
śrīsūktaṃ vaiṣṇapaṃ caiva vaiṣṇavaṃ caikaviṃśatiḥ  BhS 
indrādilokapālānāṃ pratyekaṃ juhuyātkramāt 
tattatsthānetu kūrce vā sthaṇḍile vā samarcayet  BhS 
prabhūtaṃ tu nivedyaiva droṇandroṇārchameva vā 
ācāryasyārcakādīnāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ ca dadetkramāt  BhS 
sauvarṇairutpalaiḥ puṣpairalaṅkuryātprapāṃ tataḥ 
padmairvākumudairvātha puṣpairanyaissvaśaktitaḥ  BhS 
devadevamalaṅkṛtya vastramālyādibhiḥ punaḥ 
prapāṃ saṃyojya deveśaṃ dhyānenaiva tu sannayet  BhS 
deveśaṃ sthāpayettatra pādyādyairarcayetkramāt 
mahāhaviḥ prabhūtaṃ vā yathāśakti nivedayet  BhS 
evaṃ yaḥ kurute bhaktyā viṣṇuloke mahīyate
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre
bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre
viṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
anthaikaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
viśeṣārcanam
athātassaṃpravakṣyāmi viṣṇupañcadināni ca 
śravaṇaṃ dvādaśī śukle kṛṣṇe cārdhe ca dvādaśī  BhS 
pūrṇimā cāpyamāvāsyā pañcaitāni dināni vai 
pūrvoktena vidhānena aṅkurānarbayetkramāt  BhS 
baddhvā pratisaraṃ tatra pūrvarātrautu śāyayet 
prātassandhyārcanāntetu snāpanoktakrameṇavai  BhS 
samabhyarcya nivedyaiva pūrvasthāne niveśayet 
mārgaśīrṣākhyamāse tu pūrvapakṣe viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
prātassandhyāvasānetu pūrvamāsthānamaṇḍape 
saṃsthāpya caturo vedān krameṇādhyāpayetsadā  BhS 
pūjayeddevadeveśaṃ saptaviṃśativigrahaiḥ 
ekādaśīmupopyaiva mahāpātakanāśinīm  BhS 
tataḥprabhāte dvādaśyāṃ snātvāsnānavidhānataḥ 
mṛṇmayāni tu bhāṇḍāni purāṇāni parityajet  BhS 
mṛṣṭasiktopalepādyaiśśodhayitvā yathārhakam 
snāpanoktakrameṇaiva snāpayitvā yathāvidhi  BhS 
āsanādibhirabhyarcya pāyasaṃ ca nivedayet 
pānīyācamanaṃ datvā mukhavāsaṃ tataḥparam  BhS 
puruṣasūktena saṃstūya gkāmaṃ caiva pradakṣiṇam 
dhāmapradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā jīvasthāne niveśayet  BhS 
saṃvatsarer'cane hīne nityanaimittikādiṣu 
tatsarvaṃ pūrṇamityāhurdvāśīpūjane kṛte  BhS 
pauṣe tu pūrṇimāyāṃ vai viṣṇupañcadinoktavat 
arcayitvātu deveśaṃ gavyaṃ kṣīraṃ nivedayet  BhS 
so 'pi saṃvatsaraphalaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
māghamāse punarvasvo rāghavo 'jāyata svayam  BhS 
tattastasyāmapoṣyaiva rāmaṃ vā viṣṇumeva vā 
grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā snāpayitvā nivedayet  BhS 
tilapadmavidhiṃ vakṣye śruṇudhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ 
māghamāse tu pañcamyāṃ pūrvapakṣe viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
pūrvarātrai tu deveśamarcayitvā yathāvidhi 
havīṃṣyapi nivedyaiva baddhvā pratisaraṃ punaḥ  BhS 
pūrvavacchāyayitvaiva rātriśeṣaṃ nayetkramāt 
prabhāte devamuddhāpya kalaśaissnāpayetpunaḥ  BhS 
maṇḍapaṃ vātha kūṭaṃ vā prapāṃ vātha yathocitam 
gomayenopalipyaiva pañcavarṇairalaṅkṛtam  BhS 
tasmin saṃsthāpya deveśaṃ praṇamyaivānumāsya ca 
pramukhe dhānyarāśau tu dvihastāyatavistṛte  BhS 
kṛṣṇājinaṃ samāstīrya navavastressamāstaret 
tadūrdhvetu vikīryaivaṣaḍdroṇaṃ tilameva hi  BhS 
droṇatrayaṃ dvaye vāpi maṇḍalākālavattathā 
aṣṭabhiścadalairyuktaṃ tilapadmaṃ samālikhet  BhS 
triṇiṣkena tadardhena niṣkamātreṇa vā punaḥ 
svarṇapadmaṃ ca kṛtvātu tilapadme tu vinyaset  BhS 
āḍhakaiśśālidhānyaiśca pūrṇapātrāṇi ṣoḍaśa 
indrādīśānaparyantaṃ śālirāśyupari nyaset  BhS 
aḍhakaṃ tailamāhṛtya tadardhañca ghṛtaṃ tathā 
paścime dadhimannyasya devadevaṃ praṇamya ca  BhS 
ātmasūktaṃ ca japtvātu pūjayedaṣṭavigrahaiḥ 
praṇamya devadevāya padmamadhyetu pūrvavat  BhS 
prācyādi puruṣādīṃśca caturmūrtibhirāhvayet 
ekādaśopacāraiśca pūjayitvā yathārhakam  BhS 
indrādyaiśāntamāvāhya degdevānarcayettata 
atodevā'disaṃyuktaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ japetpunaḥ  BhS 
biṃbe devaṃ samāropya cānyānudvāsayetkramāt 
yajamāno 'tha tatkāle dadyādācāryadakṣiṇām  BhS 
viṣṇubhaktiyutaṃ śāstaṃ dayādyātmaguṇairyutam 
vedapārāyaṇaparaṃ sarvāvayavasaṃyutam  BhS 
vipramāhūya tatkāle devasya niyato 'grataḥ 
dhyātvā deveśamācāryo devadevasya sannidhau  BhS 
tilapadmaṃ dadettasmai sarvalokahitāya vai 
stotrairgeyaiśca vādaiśca stutvā devaṃ samarcayet  BhS 
devaṃ yāne samāropya sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam 
devālayaṃ parītyaiva jīvasthāne niveśayet  BhS 
eve yaḥkurute bhaktyā viṣṇave paramātmane 
sarvān kāmānavāpnoti vaiṣṇavaṃ lokamaśnute  BhS 
phālgune māsi phalgunyāṃ śriyā sārthaṃ janārdanam 
snāpayitvotsavaṃ kṛtvā samabhyarchya nivedayet  BhS 
caitremāsi tathā caitṣāṃ kuryāddamanakotsavam 
pūrvasminneva divase rātripūjāvasānake  BhS 
bhaddhvā pratisaraṃ tatra deveśāya nivedayet 
vasastaṃ kāmamabhyarcya pāyasānnaṃ nivedayet  BhS 
desasya dakṣiṇe pārśve mālāṃ damanakīṃnyaset 
prabhāte devamuddhāpya snāpayitvār'cayettathā  BhS 
devasya puṣpamantrābhyāṃ dadyādbhakti samanvitam 
sarveṣāṃ parivārāṇāṃ dadyāttanmantramūrtibhiḥ  BhS 
grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃsthāpyāsthānamaṇḍape 
samabhyarcya nivedyaiva mukhavāsaṃ dadettataḥ  BhS 
vaiśākhyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vai snāpayitvā samarcayet 
jyeṣṭhe tu snāpayeddevaṃ navavastraṃ pradāpayet  BhS 
so 'pi saṃvatsaraphalaṃ prāpnuyādeva mānavaḥ 
arghyadānaṃ praśastaṃ syāddevasyāṣāḍhamāsake  BhS 
śrāvaṇe māsi sakṣatre śravaṇe tu viśeṣataḥ 
utsavasnapanādīni pūrvavatkārayedbudhaḥ  BhS 
ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi jayantyutsavalakṣaṇam 
jayantī śrāvaṇe māsi kṛṣṇapakṣe 'ṣṭamī śubhā  BhS 
rohiṇīsahitā jñeyā sarvapāpaharā tithiḥ 
tasyāṃ jāto jacagannātho jagatpālana kāṅkṣayā  BhS 
candrasyodayakāletu madhyarātre svalīlayā 
tasmin vai divase kṛṣṇamarcayitvā prayatnataḥ  BhS 
utsavaṃ kārayedyastu viṣṇossālokyatāṃ vrajet 
aṣṭamī rohiṇīyuktā rahitāvā vicakṣaṇaiḥ  BhS 
aviddhaiva sadā grāhyāsaptamyā sarvadā tidhiḥ 
ādityodayavelāyāṃ kalāmātrāṣṭamī yadi  BhS 
sātithissakalā jñeyā niśīthavyāpinī bhavet 
nāgaviddhā yathā nandā varjitā śravaṇānvitā  BhS 
tathāṣṭamīṃ pūrvaviddhāṃ sarkṣāṃ vāpi parityajet 
aviddhaivāṣṭamī grāhyā tāṃ supuṇyāmupāvaset  BhS 
rohiṇīsahitā kṛṣṇā māsi bhādrapade 'ṣṭamī 
ardharātrādadhaścordhvaṃ galayā vāpi pūrvavat  BhS 
jayantī nāma sā proktā sarvapāpapraṇāśinī 
tasmāttu divasātpūrvaṃ navame vātha saptame  BhS 
pañcame vā tṣahe 'vāpi vidhivā cāṅkurārpaṇam 
pūrvedyureva śarvaryāṃ rātripūjāvasānake  BhS 
baddhvā pratisaraṃ tatra śayane śāyayeddharim 
tasyāṃ tithāvardharātre kṛṣṇamevaṃ viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
puṣpāñjaliṃ tataḥ kuryācchriyā yukto janārdanaḥ 
bhūmibhārāpahārāya lokejāto jagatpatiḥ  BhS 
iti saṃcintayeddevaṃ vaiṣmavaṃ mantramuccaran 
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ maṇḍapaṃ ca pradakṣiṇam  BhS 
purastānmadhyame vāpi cāsthāne vāpyalaṅkṛte 
tanmadhye viṣṭare sthāpya devadevaṃ praṇamya ca  BhS 
tailaṃ haridracūrṇaṃ ca kalaśān saṃprapūrya ca 
sthaṇḍile vinyasettatra devadevaṃ samarcayet  BhS 
tailenābhyañjanaṃ kṛtvā cūrṇenodyartanaṃ caret 
nādeyaṃ gandhatoyaṃ ca puṣpodaṃ cākṣatodakam  BhS 
kuśodakaṃ tu saṃbhṛtya kalaśān pañca vinyaset 
ato devā'dibhirmantraissnāpayetpuruṣottamam  BhS 
pādyādyarṅyāntamabhyarcya devadevaṃ praṇamya ca 
hiraṇyagarbha' ityuktvāgavāṃ kṣīraṃ nivedayet  BhS 
mukhavāsaṃ ca datvaiva praṇāmaṃ ca tataścaret 
niveditaṃ tu tat kṣīraṃ vandhyāputrapradaṃ bhavet  BhS 
pītvāprasūte putraṃ ca āyuṣmantaṃ balānvitam 
nītvā ghṛtaṃ ca tailaṃ ca mukhavāsayutaṃ tathā  BhS 
devasya darśayitvā tu brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradīyatām 
devadevamalaṅkṛtya bhaktānāmāttacetasām  BhS 
yathā vai yajamānasya tathā priyakaraṃ bhudhaiḥ 
sarvavādyasamāyuktaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam  BhS 
grāmaṃ vāpyālayaṃ vāpi pradakṣiṇamathācaret 
ālayaṃ saṃpraviśyaiva kalaśaissnāvayedbudhaḥ  BhS 
ācāryadakṣiṇāṃ datvā sodakaṃ devasannidhau 
prabhūtaṃ tu nivedyaiva mukhavāsaṃ dadetpunaḥ  BhS 
evamevaṃ tathā kuryādutsavaṃ prativatsaram 
bhuktimuktipradamidamṛṣibhiḥ parīkīrtitam  BhS 
apare 'tha dine vāpi kārayedutsavaṃ bhudhaḥ 
yadyanmantrakriyālopo vaiṣṇavair hūyate tathā  BhS 
ekasmin vatsare hīne devadevaṃ praṇamya ca 
snapanaṃ pañcaviṃśadbhiḥ kalaśaiśśuddhamānasaiḥ  BhS 
śāntihomaṃ ca hutvātu puṇyāhamapi vācayet 
utsavaṃ dviguṇaṃ kuryāddakṣiṇāṃ ca svaśaktitaḥ  BhS 
śrāvaṇe dvādaśīyoge māpi bhādrapade tathā 
saṃvatsarārcādoṣasya śāntyarthaṃ keśavasya tu  BhS 
asmin māse viśeṣeṇa pavitrāropaṇaṃ hareḥ 
sarvadoṣopaśamanaṃ sarvakāmābhivṛddhidam  BhS 
māse 'smīnnārabhetaiva śravaṇavratamuttamam 
tribhirvarṣaistribhirmāsairupoṣya ca mahatpalam  BhS 
āśvayujamāse cāśvyarkṣe deveśaṃ snāpayettataḥ 
arghyadānaṃ praśastaṃ syāddevadevasya śārjiṇaḥ  BhS 
athātaḥ kṛttikādīpadānalakṣaṇamucyate 
kārtikyāṃ pūrṇimāyāntu yadṛkṣantu pravartate  BhS 
tadṛkṣaṃ dīpaṛkṣaṃ syātkālāpekṣā na vidyate ravyastamayavelāyāṃ 
dīpāropaṇamācaret  BhS 
devasya sannidhau staṃbhe devālayasamocchraye 
adhike vā mahādīpaṃ mahāsnehaṃ prakalpayet  BhS 
tripādaṃ vā tadhardhaṃ vā dīpadaṇḍaṃ samāharet 
veṇuṃ vā kramukaṃ vāpi tālaṃ vā nālikerakam  BhS 
madhūkaṃ tintriṇīkaṃ cetyanyaissāradrumaistathā 
śatāṣṭadīpasaṃyuktaṃmuttamottamamucyate  BhS 
utme madhyamaṃ dīpaṃ 
śatasaṃkhyākramaṃ viduḥ 
uttamādhamadīpaṃ syānnavatirdvyadhikā tathā  BhS 
madhyamottamamuktaṃ syādaśītiścaturastathā 
madhyame madhyamaṃ caiva ṣaṭsaptatirathocyate  BhS 
madhyamādhamadīpantu aṣṭaṣaṣṭiriti smṛtam 
adhamottamadīpantu ṣaṣṭisaṃkhyāṃ vadantihi  BhS 
dvipañcāśatpradīpāṃśca kuryādadhamamadhyame 
adhamādhamamevedaṃ catvāriṃśatpradīpakam  BhS 
aśaktānāṃ yathāśakti dīpaṃ tatraiva yojayet 
daṇḍetu suṣire yojyaṃ caturdikṣu krameṇa vai  BhS 
bhūtapīṭhasya pūrvetu dīpasthānaṃ vidhīyate 
padmakośapratīkāśa' iti śrutyāmudāhṛtam  BhS 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena padmaṃ kuryātsalakṣaṇam 
vistārāyāmatulyaṃ syāccatustālapramāṇataḥ  BhS 
golakāṅgulamutsedhaṃ caturaśraṃ prakalpayet 
tatraiva śālibhi stiryakpadmamaṣṭadalānvitam  BhS 
tanmadhye tālamātreṇa samavṛttaṃ sakarṇikam 
ekāṅgulasamutsedhaṃ tatraivopari taṇḍulaiḥ  BhS 
sati padmaṃ samutphullaṃ navavastraṃ samāstaret 
puṣpaṃ tasyopari nyasya kalbayetpadmamaṇḍalam  BhS 
daleṣvabhyarcya ca vasūn madhye dharmaṃ samarcayet 
ālayābhimukhe kuryātprapāṃ caivātisundaram  BhS 
āsthānamaṇḍape vāpi kalpayetpadmamaṇḍalam 
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ mṛṇmayaṃ vāsvaśaktitaḥ  BhS 
śarāvaṃ prasthasaṃpūrṇaṃ samāhṛtya vicakṣaṇaḥ 
kiñcitkarpūrasaṃyuktaṃ picuvartisamanvitam  BhS 
gavyaṃ ghṛtaṃ samādāya sthāpayetpadmamadhyame 
ācāryassuprasannātmā navavastrottarīyakaḥ  BhS 
śriyaijā'teti mantreṇa dīpasyoddīpanaṃ caret 
pratīcyāṃ padmamadhyetu śriyaṃ dhyātvā samāhvayet  BhS 
ekādaśopacāraiśca pūjayitvā samāhitaḥ 
śrīdevīṃ manasā dhyātvā śrīsūktaṃ ca samuccaran  BhS 
dīpamādāya hastābhyāmapsarobhirviśeṣataḥ 
dīpānanyāntsamādāya to yadhārāsamanvitam  BhS 
geyadhvanisamāyuktaṃ nṛttavādyasamanvitam 
pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā garbhāgāraṃ praveśayet  BhS 
depasya dakṣiṇe pārśvesthāpayenmantravittamaḥ 
devadevaṃ samānīya maṇḍale sthāpya cātvaraḥ  BhS 
kuryāddaśopacārāṃśca samabhyarcyedvidhānataḥ 
śrīye jā'teti mantreṇa dīpānuddīpayedbudhaḥ  BhS 
garbhageheca sopāne prāsāde mukhamaṇḍape 
prāsādaśikhare vāpigrīvāyāṃ caraṇe 'pi ca  BhS 
prākāreṣu ca sarvatra tathaiva snapanālaye 
puṣpasaṃcayadeśe ca dvāre cāsthānamaṇḍape  BhS 
anyeṣvapi ca sarvatra dīpānuddīpayetkramāt 
kārpāsatūlaṃ saṃbaddhya śarāveṣughṛtena vai  BhS 
pūrvoktenaiva mantreṇa coddīpanamathācaret 
nṛttageyādivādyaiśca ghoṣayitvā prayatnataḥ  BhS 
taccharāvasthadīpaṃ ca balipīṭhasya paścime 
adhidevaṃ samārādhya nikṣipeddīpamaṇḍape  BhS 
śubhrājyoti'riti procya daṇḍrāgre 'nyāṃśca nikṣipet 
nivedya bahūdhā devaṃ pṛthukādīnviśeṣataḥ  BhS 
bhakṣyāṇi guḍamiśrāṇiprabhūtaṃ ca mahāhaviḥ

grahaṇārādhanam
athātassaṃpravakṣyāmi sūryasomoparāgayoḥ 
arcanādividhiṃ samyak devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ  BhS 
sūryagrahe caturyāmaṃ triyāmaṃ tu vidhugrahe 
nāśnanti havyakavyāni devatāḥ pitarastathā  BhS 
ālaye tu hareḥ pūjāṃ na tyajanti maharṣayaḥ 
havirnivedanaṃ hitvāpūjāṃ sarvāṃ samācaret  BhS 
grahaṇe vartamānetu snāpayetpuruṣottamam 
koṭiyajñaphalaṃ prāpya brahmaloke mahīyate  BhS 
grastāstagrahaṇe kuryātsnapanaṃ tu pare 'hani 
tathā grastodaye kuryāditi śātātapo 'bravīt  BhS 
sarvadhā varamāne tu grahaṇesnapanaṃ caret 
grahaṇaṃ saṃkramo hasticchāyā ca viṣuvādikam  BhS 
yugādi va mādyāstu puṇyakālāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
niṣethaḥ kathitaḥ prājñairhavirdāsavadutsave  BhS 
nityārcanaṃ cotsavaṃ ca snapanātpūrvamācaret 
snāpayitvā hṛṣīkeśaṃ havirdānaṃ praśasyate  BhS 
vāstuśuddhiṃ sadā kuryādgrahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ 
purāṇāni ca bhāṇḍāni tyaktvānyāni samāharet  BhS 
kuśāgrāṇāṃ samutkṣepādvāsasāṃ śuddhiriṣyate 
apakvānāṃ ca vastūnāṃ na pakvaṃ parigṛhṇate  BhS 
adṛśyamuparāgantu noparāgaṃ pracakṣate 
dīkṣitasya tathānyasya snānaṃ syātsparśamokṣayoḥ  BhS 
yāvānādyantakālassyāttāvatākīrtayeddharim 
maunī japādikaṃ kuryādūrdhvapuṇḍradharaśśuciḥ  BhS 
saptavātāhataṃ vastramārdraṃ dhṛtvā na doṣabhāk

utsavacakram
ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi pūrvoddiṣṭaṃ sudarśanam 
sudarśanasya coddiṣṭaṃ pramāṇaṃ ca viśeṣuḥ  BhS 
mahāberasya mānena navāṅgulamiti smṛtam 
tasya vṛttaṃ samuddiṣṭamarāścaiva tu tṣaṅgulam  BhS 
vṛttaṃ paṭṭasya vistāramekāṅgulamudāhṛtam 
tanmadhye cārakūṭaṃ syādekāṃgulamudāhṛtam  BhS 
arā dvādaśa uddiṣṭā etaccakrasya vai tathā 
adhamaṃ mārgamālokya proktametatpramāṇakam  BhS 
tatra madhyaṃ pramāṇantu vakṣyāmi śruṇutādarāt 
mahāberasya hastena dvādaśāṃgulamucyate  BhS 
tadvṛttaṃ tasya hastena dvādaśāṃgulamucyate 
vṛttaṃ tasya samuddiṣṭamārakūṭaṃ dviyaṅgulam  BhS 
vṛttapaṭṭasya vistāramekāṃgulamudāhṛtam 
aṣṭau ca caturaṅgulyā
duddiṣṭāśca samāsataḥ  BhS 
arāṣṣoḍaśa uddiṣṭāścakrasyaiva tu madhyame 
kūrmaṃ vāpyatha siṃhaṃ vā padmaṃ vāpyatha kālayet  BhS 
adhastādyogadaṇḍaṃ ca ekāṅgulamudāhṛtam 
ubhayoḥ pādayoścaiva siṃhenaiva tu kārayet  BhS 
āyasenaiva vā kuryāddāruṇā vā tathaiva ca 
sarvatra suṃdaraṃ kuryātsajānana
vidhīyate  BhS 
etallakṣaṇamudgiṣṭaṃ cakrasyaiva pramāṇataḥ 
madhūcchiṣṭena vidhinā kuryādvai tatra tatra tu  BhS 
vidadhyāddeva devasya heti pravaramuttamam 
pramāṇaṃ ca tu sarvatra tattribhāgaṃ viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
sthāpanāṃ mūrtimantraṃ ca cakrasya śruṇutarṣayaḥ 
athātassaṃpravakṣyāmi vaiṣṇavaṃ cakramuttamam  BhS 
trividhaṃ cakramuddiṣṭaṃ brahmaṇā parameṣinā 
kālacakraṃ vīracakraṃ sahasravikacaṃ kramāt  BhS 
karoddhṛtaṃ vīracakraṃ devasya mukhamānataḥ 
sarvājināṃ samūhanta bajaṃ khatrayamantataḥ  BhS 
devasya mukhamānaṃ syāddvādaśāṣṭāracihnitam 
jvālāpañcakasaṃyuktaṃ karāgre dakṣiṇe caret  BhS 
mayaṃ mahīmayaṃ divyamaṣṭāraṃ dvādaśārakam 
ebhirmantraissamabhyarcya rakṣārthaṃ mokṣaśāntaye  BhS 
kālacakraṃ pravakṣyāmi autsavaṃ sarvaśāntidam 
dhruvaberamukhāyāmaṃ dviguṇāyāmavistṛtam  BhS 
vṛttaṃ ca ṣaḍguṇaṃ proktaṃ kṣatāntaṃ tatsuvṛttakam 
vṛttasya paṭṭavistāraṃ triyaṅgulamiti smṛtam  BhS 
ṣaḍaṅgulasamāyāmamārakūṭaṃ tu tṣaṅgulam 
yavā kārakarā jñeyā ubhayatra praveśatā  BhS 
arakūṭe 'tha siṃhaṃ vā makaraṃ vātha padmakam 
jvālātrikaṃ vā kartavyaṃ jvālāpañjakameva vā  BhS 
śatāṣṭāraṃ niṃśatiṃ vā uttame samyagācaret 
catuṣpañcadvipañcāśanmadhyame samudāhṛtam  BhS 
dvātriṃśadvā caturviṃśadadhame saṃprayojayet 
evaṃ syātkālacakrantu utsavārthaṃ prakalpayet  BhS 
cakrādhastāttathā nālaṃ dvādaśāṃgulamācaret 
cakradviguṇadaṇḍantu khadiraṃ cāsanaṃ bhavet  BhS 
yājñikairatha vā vṛkṣaiḥ kārayedatra śāsanam 
ṣaḍaṅgulāyatavistārāṃ phalakāṃ saṃprakalpayet  BhS 
vṛttaṃ vā caturaśraṃ vā laṃbadāmasamāyutam 
triyaṅgulasamutsedhaṃ saṃdhayettarikopari  BhS 
tadadhastāttu tāṭiṃ ca kuṃbhalaṃbakasaṃyutam 
aṣṭāṃgulasamutsethaṃ kārayediti śāsanam  BhS 
antassuṣirasaṃ kṛtvā
daṇḍāgre cādha eva vā 
kūradaṇḍena saṃyojya phalakophalapadmakam  BhS 
latā prasthataraṃ vāpi kārayediti śāsanam 
padmaṃ tu tṣaṅgunāyāmaṃ vistāramadhikāṃgulam  BhS 
pālikopari siṃhau dvāvubhayoḥ pārśvayoścaret 
cakraṃ saṃvahamānau tau yāvattatra ca kālayet  BhS 
tayormānaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ pañcāṃgulamiti smṛtam 
daṇḍamadhyena kuryāttaddaṇḍamūle ṣaḍaṅgulam  BhS 
pīṭhaṃ ṣaḍaṅgulotsedhaṃ caturaṅgulameva vā 
vṛttaṃ vā caturaśraṃ vā sarojadalakarṇayuk  BhS 
ṣāḍhaśāṃgulamāyāmaṃ vistāraṃ saṃprakīrtitam 
karṇikāmadhyame nālamaṣṭāṃgula samāyutam  BhS 
nāladaṇḍena saṃyojya bandhayedaṣṭabandhanaiḥ 
hāravatsudṛḍhaṃ kuryādavakramṛjusaṃyutam  BhS 
evaṃ kṛtvā yathāmārgaṃ sthāpanaṃ samyagācaret 
sahasravikacaṃ cakraṃ puruṣākāramācaret  BhS 
raktābhaṃ nīlavarṇaṃ ca navatālena mānataḥ 
dvibhujaṃ mukuṭodbandhaṃ cakracūlinamācaret  BhS

anapāyinamityevaṃ mūrtimantraissamarcayet  BhS 
śatadhāraṃ kālacakraṃ sarvāsuravimardanam 
sarvavighnaharaṃ ceti kālacakraṃ samarcayet  BhS 
kālacakraṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvāsuravināśanam

vistārāyāmatomānamuttamādhamamadhyamam 
mānāṃgulena tadgrāhyaṃ takṣakaṃ vartulaṃ bhavet  BhS 
sahasrārā aṣṭaśataṃ triśataṃ ṣaṣṭimeva vā 
arāḥkrameṇa saṃyuktā uttamādhamamadhyamāḥ  BhS 
caturviṃśattathā jvālāṣṣoḍaśa dvādaśātha vā 
daśasaptāṅgulaṃ pañca vṛttaṃ paṭṭasya saṃyutam  BhS 
cakraprabhehakaṃ bhāgaṃ pīṭhaṃ padmakamācaret 
daṇḍādīni vinā tasya padmaṃ pīṭhasyayojayet  BhS 
etaduktaṃ mahaccakraṃ sarvāriṣṭavināśanam 
cakrasya sthāpanaṃ mārgaṃ pravakṣyāmi tapodhanāḥ  BhS 
aṅkurānarpayitvātu kārayedakṣimocanam 
tathādhivāsanaṃ kṛtvā gavyānāmadhivāsanam  BhS 
yāgaśālāṃ tathā kṛtvā bhūṣayettoraṇānvitam 
śayyāvediṃ ca tanmadhye cādhyardhāyāmavistṛtam  BhS 
tatturyāṃśodayāṃ vediṃ kṛtvā tāṃ caturaśrakam 
prācyāmāhavanīyaṃ ca kuṇḍamaupāsanāgnivat  BhS 
prācyāṃ tu snānavediṃ ca kṛtvācaiva vicakṣaṇaḥ 
athādhivāsitaṃ cakramādāyevābhiṣicya ca  BhS 
agniṃ saṃsādhya pūrvoktaṃ kuṃbhaṃ saṃsāthayetpunaḥ 
cakrasyābhimukhe kuṃbhaṃ dhānyapīṭhoparikramāt  BhS 
sannyasya tu gururdhīmān yaditaṃ bhāvayettathā 
grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā śālāyāṃ sthāpayettathā  BhS 
hṛtpadmamadhye cakreśaṃ dvibhujaṃ prāṃjalīkṛtam

tasmātkuṃbhe samāvāhya pūrvoktamabhipūjya ca 
vedyāṃ saṃsnāpya taccakraṃ kalaśaisnāpayettadā  BhS 
samala kṛtya vaktrādyairdhānyapīṭhoparikramāt 
sannyasya kuṃbhaṃ saṃyuktaṃ baddhvā pratisaraṃ tataḥ  BhS 
śāyayitvā tathā cakraṃ hautraṃ samyak praśaṃsya ca

paścādagniṃ paristīrya vaiṣṇavairmantra saṃyutaiḥ 
bhūmānano 'gre vandyāna'hutvā gāyatrisaṃyutam  BhS 
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ hutvā rātriśeṣaṃ vyapohya ca

grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā kuṃbhenāsādayettathā 
maṇḍape dakṣiṇe pārśve kṛtapīṭhe viśeṣataḥ  BhS

kuṃbhācchaktiṃ tathāvāhya pūjayedāsanādibhiḥ

iti śrīvaikhānase

utsavaḥ
ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi deveśasyotsavakramam 
varṣadaṃ sarvalokasya śāntidaṃ sarvapuṣṭidam  BhS 
rājñāṃ vijayadānāya śatrūṇāṃ nāśahetave 
vyādhidurbhikṣaśā ntyarthamutsavaṃ kārayedbudhaḥ  BhS 
kālaśraddhānimittārthākhyā
utsavāstrividhāssmṛtāḥ 
māsetu yasmin kasmiṃśchitpratisaṃvatsaraṃ caret  BhS 
ekasmin samayecaiva sa tu kālotsavo bhavet 
iṣṭamāse dine ceṣṭe śraddhayā kriyate tu yaḥ  BhS 
sa tu śraddhotsavojñeya stasmātkālotsavo guruḥ 
bhayapradanimitteṣu tathānāvṛṣṭikādiṣu  BhS 
kriyate tatra śāntyarthaṃ sa nimittotsavassmṛtaḥ 
pratiṣṭhādivase tīrthaṃ prati saṃvatkaraṃ caret  BhS 
kālotsava itijñeyaśśāntyarthaṃ saprakīrtitaḥ 
rājarāṣṭrābhivṛddhyarthaṃ rājñāṃ caivābhivṛddhaye  BhS 
atmanaścaiva putrāṇāṃ kuryādukteṣu maṅgalam 
rājño janmadine caiva yassa śraddhotsavo bhavet  BhS 
adbhutādyudbhaveśāntissatu naimittikotsavaḥ

darśanadravyarūpāṇāṃ yathālābhaṃ pragṛhya ca 
tattaddravyādhidaivatyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ juhuyātkramāt  BhS 
tattaddravyaṃ ca saṃpādya vidhivaddarśayetpunaḥ

yajñālaye mahāvedyāṃ kṛtāyāmapramāṇataḥ

tattaddeśādhidaivatyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam

puruṣasūktaṃ raudramārṣaṃ vāruṇaṃ ca punaścaret 
agnikuṇḍānyavidhinā kṛtānyālakṣya satvaram  BhS

apramāṇeṣu kūrcādiṣvājyapātra sruvādiṣu  BhS

pañcāgniṣu yathāsthānaṃ prokṣaṇollekhane kṛte  BhS

nagacchedyadi gacchettu tattaddikpāladaivatam 
vaiṣṇavaṃ pāvakaṃ ceti prāyaścittaṃ hunaitkramāt  BhS

ādau praṇayanādarvāgathavāgniṣu sarvaśaḥ śāntiṃ yathoditāṃ kuryādagni sūktaṃ sahasraśaḥ

tadvyapohyānyadādāya prājāpatyaṃ ca pāvakam

āgneyaṃ mindāhutī ca vaiṣṇavaṃ ca hunedbudhaḥ  BhS

puṇyāhahīne puṇyāhamantrān dvādaśaśo japet  BhS 
vāstuhomavihīne tu tanmantrān daśaśo hunet

viṣṇusūktaṃ pauruṣaṃ ca sūktaṃ hutvā samācaret

aṇḍajādidvalabdheṣu vastraṃ pratyekamāharet  BhS 
vaiṣṇavaṃ śrībhūdaivatyaṃ hutvā kāryaṃ samācaret 
pramāṇahīneṣu punastoraṇādiṣu cātvaraḥ  BhS 
pṛthagdvārādhidaivatyaṃ juhuyādviṃśatiṃ budhaḥ

yatnena tāni nikṣipya vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam 
puruṣasūktaṃ brāhmaṃ ca munimantrāṃśca pāvakam  BhS 
juhuyāddaśakṛtvantu viprāṇāṃ bhojanaṃ caret

hutvā viṃśatikṛtvantu dadyādācāryadakṣiṇām 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvaiva saṃpūjyaiva ca vaiṣmavān  BhS 
anyatkuṃbhaṃ samāhṛtya pūrvavatsādhayedbudhaḥ 
spṛṣṭe tu sāthite kuṃbhe patitaiḥ kukkuṭādibhiḥ  BhS 
tadvyapohyāryadādāya pūrvavatsādhayettathā

brāhmaṃ sauramathāgneyamaṣṭādhikaśataṃ yajet 
ācāryadakṣiṇāṃ dadyādvaiṣṇavān pūjayedvidhiḥ  BhS 
sparśaduṣṭe tathā bere snapanaṃ śāstrataścaret 
pūrvoktāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ kṛtvā paścātkāryaṃ samācaret  BhS 
nruvādīnāmalābhetu sruveṇaiva huneddhaviḥ 
śvakukkuṭādyaissaṃspṛṣṭe kuṇḍe taṃ taṃ vyapohya ca  BhS 
kuṇḍaṃ tu pūrvavatkṛtvā kṛtvāghāraṃ yathāvidhi 
āgneyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ pañcavāruṇaṃ mūlahomakam  BhS 
śataśo juhuyātkuryādbrāhmaṇānāṃ ca bhojanam

āgneyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmaṃ hutvākāryaṃ samācaret 
darbhān kuśānvā samidho māsātītān pragṛhya ca  BhS 
vāruṇaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmaṃ saumyamāgneyameva ca

dadhi kṣīraṃ gṛhītaṃ cedājaṃ māhiṣameva vā

saṃsnāpya devadeveśaṃ punasthsāpana mācaret  BhS 
akṣyunneṣādhivāsau tu punasthsāpanakarmaṇi 
hitvānyatsakalaṃ karma pūrvavattu samācaret  BhS 
havirhīne janāssarvetadgrāmasthāssamīpagāḥ 
pīḍitāḥ kṣutpipāsādyairbhaveyurvyādhitā api  BhS 
tasmādatiprayatnena havissamya ṅnivedayet 
hīne haviṣyeka kāle dvitīye dviguṇaṃ bhavet  BhS 
tṛtīye triguṇaṃ kuryādekasmin divase gate 
vaiṣṇavaṃ śrīmahīmantrān mūrti homaṃ tathā hunet  BhS 
devaṃ śuddhodakaissnāpya prabhūtaṃ tu nivedayet 
sopadaṃśamapakvaṃ ca śītaṃ paryuṣitaṃ tathā  BhS 
pātrāntareṣvanikṣiptaṃ sāvaśeṣaṃ ca laṅghitam

havirnivedayeccettu vaiṣṇavaṃ śrīmahīmanūn  BhS 
āgneyaṃ vāruṇaṃ caiva vāyavyaṃ daśaśo hunet 
dviguṇaṃ tu punaḥkṛtvā prabhūtaṃ tu nivedayet  BhS 
nivedya cāśumispṛṣṭaṃ devaṃ saṃsnāpya mantrataḥ 
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇugāyatrīṃ trayastriṃśatkramāddhunet  BhS

vrīhyaṅgāratuṣairyukteśarkarādivimiśrite 
nivedite tu haviṣi mantreṇāṣṭākṣareṇa tu  BhS

kṣama'svetyanumānyaiva praṇamayaiva ca yācayet  BhS

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca śrībhūdaivatyameva ca 
aṣṭottaraśataṃ hutvā dviguṇaṃ tu nivedayet  BhS 
mahāhaviṣi caitaintu saṃyukte tatra dūṣitam 
puruṣāśanamātraṃ tu vyapohya tadanantaram  BhS 
bhasmāṃbhasākuśai rāpo hiraṇya pavamāna'kaiḥ 
prokṣya devaṃ susaṃprārdhya tadgṛhītvā nivedayet  BhS 
pūrvamarkodayātpakva mupadaṃśamatho haviḥ 
koṣṇaṃ cedarpayet prātararcanāntena doṣabhāk  BhS 
pūrva mastamayātpakvaṃ tathā sāyaṃ nivedayet 
asaṃskṛtaṃ tu tāṃbūlaṃ lepakeśānvitaṃ tathā  BhS 
jantuspṛṣṭaṃ nivedyaiva vaiṣṇavaṃśrīmahīmanun 
hutvā saṃskṛtya tāṃbūlaṃ punaranyannivedayet  BhS 
arcanāṃgeṣu cānyeṣu padārtheṣvevameva hi 
dūṣiteṣvadha hīneṣu tasya tasyādhidaivatam  BhS 
mantraṃ sa vaiṣṇavaṃ hutvā punaranyaissamarcayet 
alābhe caiva sarveṣāṃ puṣpaṃ toyaṃ pragṛhyaca  BhS 
saṃkalpyaiva pratinidhiṃ tattatsmṛtvā samarcayet 
nityahome vihīnetu vaiṣṇavaṃ daśaśo hunet  BhS 
yathoktahomaṃ dviguṇamācarettadanantaram 
agnisaṃrakṣaṇe 'śaktā vayante yo'nimuccaran  BhS

nyasya copāvaro'hetipratyahaṃ juhuyātkramāt  BhS 
surarṣimanujānāṃ tu balaṃ yasmātpṛvardhate

uktadravyeṣu cāvāhya triṣu kāleṣu deśikaḥ 
abhyarcya bhrāmayedevamaśaktaḥ kartumuttamam  BhS

tasyopari yathoktaṃ tu baliberaṃ ca vinyaset  BhS 
śirasā dhārayan pātraṃ trirdvirvā sakṛdeva vā 
dene tataḥ parīyācca devāgāraṃ pradakṣiṇam  BhS 
atha hitvā balidravyaṃ śibikādau gaje 'thavā 
aropya yāne vidhivatkārayecca pradakṣiṇam  BhS 
prātarbhramaṇahīne tu vaiṣmavaṃ saurasaumyakam 
prājāpatyaṃ ca juhuyāddhīne coktapradakṣiṇe  BhS 
vaiṣṇavaṃ gāruḍaṃ hutvā balibhramaṇamācaret 
hīne prātarbalau kuryānmadhyāhne dviguṇaṃ balim  BhS 
tathā hīne ca madhyāhne rātrau triguṇamācaret 
ekāhe tu balau hīne nityāgnau vā mahānane  BhS 
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca puruṣasūktaṃ tathaiva ca 
digdaivatyaṃ ca hutvā tu pradakṣiṇanuthācaret  BhS 
devālaṅkārahīne tu śrīdaivatyaṃ yajedbudhaḥ 
chatrapiñchādyalābhe tu vāruṇaṃ juhuyāttathā  BhS 
alābhe cāmarādīnāṃ vāyavyaṃ caiva hūyate

dvādaśāhāntamevaṃ syāddvādaśāhe gate tataḥ  BhS 
aupāsanāgnimādhāya vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam

raudraṃ digdevatāmantraṃ hutvaiva bhramaṇaṃ caret

dvimāse dviguṇaṃ kuryāttrimāse triguṇaṃ caret 
vardhaye dvatsarāntaṃ cāpyatīte vatsare punaḥ  BhS 
sabhyaṃ saṃsādhya devābhimukhe vā dakṣiṇe nalam 
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca sūktaṃ pauruṣameva ca  BhS 
śrībhūmyoścaiva daivatyaṃ sarvadaivatyameva ca 
hutvā cāryaṃ ca saṃpūjya balyuddharaṇamācaret  BhS 
patite 'nnabalau bhūmyāṃ bhinne jīrṇe ca pūrvavat

prājāpatyaṃ tu vidhinā tataḥ kuryātpradakṣiṇam 
balyuddharaṇakāle tu vighnaścedāpatettadā  BhS 
sauraṃ saumyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca hutvā punarathācaret 
pātrālābhe haviḥpātraṃ hunaidādāya vaiṣṇavam  BhS 
pramāṇahīne 'nnabalau vaiṣṇavaṃ ca prajāpatim 
juhuyāddoṣaduṣṭe tu havirniṣkṛtimācaret  BhS 
āvāhanaṃ vinā cānnabalau tu bhramaṇekṛte 
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca puruṣasūktaṃ tathaiva ca  BhS 
hutvā śrībhūmidaivatyaṃ vidhinā bhramaṇaṃ caret 
balyagrakhaṇḍe vidhinā śāntāya tvanivedite  BhS 
vaiṣṇavaṃ mūrtimantraṃ ca hutvaiva daśaśaḥ kramāt 
nivedya viṣvakcenāya pradāya mukhavāsanam  BhS 
punaśca balyuddharaṇaṃ vidhinā kārayettataḥ 
akṛte balidāne tu prāśya pādodakaṃ hareḥ  BhS 
prasādaṃ cāpi saṃprāśya punardviguṇamarcayet 
pravṛttāyāṃ tu pūjāyāṃ havirdānāntameva ca  BhS

sarvāṇvapi havīṃṣyatra nāgavallīdalānyapi

nitye karmaṇi sarvatra pūjakaṃ pūrvamarcayet  BhS

dviguṇaṃ tu samabhyarcya cānyaddviguṇa mācaret  BhS 
aśucirvāpyanācāraḥ sadāvaikhānasa śśuciḥ 
pitā mṛṣyati putrāṇāṃ viśaṅkaṃ doṣasaṃcayam  BhS 
pitā hi bhagavān viṣṇuputrāssyuḥ pūjakā hareḥ 
tasmātteṣu na kupyeta dīrghamāyurjijīviṣuḥ  BhS 
ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi niṣkṛtiṃ snapanāśritām

śeṣeṣu snapanaṃ yattatkāmyaṃ tu parikīrtitam 
nityasnāpanahīne tu vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam  BhS 
puruṣasūktaṃ vāruṇaṃ ca daśakṛtvo hunetpunaḥ 
snapanaṃ vidhivatkuryānni tyasnapana niṣkṛtiḥ  BhS

anyathā cenmahādoṣo yajamāno vinaśyati

saṃdhyākāletu saṃprāpte nimittasnapane tathā  BhS 
naimittikaṃ samāpyaiva nityapūjaṃ samācaret 
anyathā vaiṣṇavaṃ mantraṃ śatavāraṃ japetsudhīḥ  BhS

parvateṣyapramāṇeṣu vaiṣṇavaṃ pāvakaṃ hunet 
dhānyeṣu vaiṣṇavaṃ caiva vāyavyaṃ ca hunedbudhaḥ  BhS 
aṅkureṣu vihīneṣu vaiṣṇavaṃ gāruḍaṃ tathā

varṇahīneṣvamāneṣu maṅgaleṣu tu vaiṣṇavam 
aindraṃ ca juhuyātkuryādyathārhaṃ saṃbharedapi  BhS 
pañcagavye mantrahīne vihīne yogakarmaṇi

uktapramāṇahīneṣu pañcagavyādiṣu kramāt

prāśanaṃ prokṣaṃ vāpi śāstre 'smin yatra codyate  BhS

kalaśānāṃ viparyāme taddhṛtenaiva cāplute  BhS

śuddhodaissnāpayec caiva yathāvacca punarnyaset  BhS

kṛmikīṭādipatane tattaddravyaṃ parityajet  BhS 
anyadādāya juhuyādvaiṣṇavaṃ dravyadaivatam

vastrālābhe vaiṣṇavaṃ ca śrīdaivatyaṃ ca hāvayet 
yathoktasnapane hīne kathaṃ citsnapanaṃ caret  BhS 
atha vā kārayec chuddhasnapanaṃ vā vidhānataḥ

vijñāpya devadeveśaṃ tataḥ kālotsavaṃ caret 
anyathā tu kṛtaṃ kāryamakṛtaṃ syādasaṃśayam  BhS

eṣa eva vidhiḥ proktaḥ parasminvatsare kṛte  BhS

yatra devālaye viṣṇusthsāpyate prathamaṃ tataḥ

tanniyuktais tadīyairvāpūrvābhāve paraiścaret  BhS 
anyathā kriyate cettu yajamāno vinaśyati 
utsavāhassu hīneṣu prāyaścittaṃ samācaret  BhS 
vardhayedvaiṣṇavaṃ kāryaṃ hrāsayenna kadā cana

sarve padārthinaḥ proktā gurupūrvāḥpadārthinaḥ

vatsarāśaucamitaraccāśaucaṃ na pravartate

nakuryācceddvitīye tu māse kartā vinaśyati

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca nṛsūktaṃ caiva gāruḍam 
dhvājaṃ śāntaṃ ca cakraṃ ca tathaivotsavadaivatam  BhS 
vyāhṛtyantaṃ ca hutvā tu vaiṣṇavān pūjya cācaret 
dhvajasya lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye yena mānena kārayet  BhS 
vimānena samaṃ vātha pādenār'dhena vādhikam

jayaśrīkīrtivijayamaṅgalākhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
ardhahīnaṃ na kurvīta tadevāgatikaṃ bhavet  BhS

avakramṛjumanyenāsaṃbaddhaṃ kīlitādibhiḥ  BhS 
ślakṣṇaṃ manoharaṃ dāru gṛhītvākhaṇḍamuttamam

bhāgamekaṃ vihāyāgre tatra kuryāttrimekhalāḥ 
mekhalānāmathāyāmastadbhāgena samo bhavet  BhS 
tritālavistṛtaṃ kuryāddaṇḍavistṛtameva vā

yaṣṭī dve purataḥ kuryātpaścādekā vidhīyate 
sarvatra kiṅkiṇīnāṃ tu kuryācchatama śeṣataḥ  BhS 
paścāccheṣaṃ tridhā kuryāccaturdhā vā dhvajaṃ budhaḥ 
aṣṭāśraṃ ca ṣaḍaśraṃ ca caturaśraṃ ca vṛttakam  BhS 
mūlādārabhya kurvīta caturdhā vihitaṃ dhvajam 
tridhā kṛte na kuryāttu ṣaḍaśraṃ śeṣamācaret  BhS 
ādyaṃ bhāgaṃ tridhā kṛtvā kecidevaṃ prakurvate 
śikharaṃ śira ityāhurardhena śikharaṃ bhavet  BhS 
pramādātpatitaṃ gṛhya śikharaṃ sthāpayedvidhiḥ 
spuṭitevātha bhinne vā biṃbasyoktavadācaret  BhS 
adhiṣṭite tu śikhare dvijairgṛdhrādibhissakṛt 
viṣṭhādikaraṇe vāpi uṣite vā nirantaram  BhS 
vāstuhomaṃ ca hutvaiva paryagnikaraṇaṃ caret 
eṣa eva vidhiḥ prokto vimānaśikharādiṣu  BhS 
adhiṣṭhānena pādena prastareṇa ca saṃyutam 
dhvajamūle tviṣṭakābhirvediṃ kuryānmanoharām  BhS 
na tāmapyadhitiṣṭheta naro dīrghaṃ jijīviṣuḥ 
kiṃ punastatra vaktavyamālayādyavarohaṇe  BhS 
vimānaṃ viṣṇurūpaṃ syānna tatpādādivā kramet 
dhāmapradakṣiṇe pūrvaṃ kuryāttatra namastriyāḥ  BhS 
na laṅghayeddhvajachāyāṃ pradakṣiṇavidhiṃ vinā 
gopurasya vimānasya prākārasyālayasya ca  BhS 
pramādādatilaṅghyaiva prāṇāyāmaśataṃ caret 
śivadṛṣṭiṃ viṣṇuvṛṣṭhaṃ durgāyāḥ pārśvato dṛśam  BhS 
vighneśasyordhvadṛṣṭiṃ ca tīkṣṇamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ 
yāvacchāvatarec chāyā tāvatī doṣabhūmikā  BhS 
doṣabhūmiṃ parityajya nivāsaṃ parikalpayet 
tyāge saṃpatsamṛddhissyādanyathā viparītakṛt  BhS 
radhyādibhiryathā bhūyādantaraṃ tanna doṣakṛt 
atha vā śatadaṇḍāntaṃ tyaktvānve vasatiṃ jaguḥ  BhS 
yāvaddhāmāyataṃ dāvatpṛṣṭhaṃ vā mughameva vā 
tatodhikaṃ tacca tacca kecidāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ  BhS 
dhvajaṃ nityamuśantyeke yatraiko hyanavāyiṣu 
tatrārohaṇakarmādi necchanti paramarṣayaḥ  BhS 
autsavaṃ dhvajamāsthāpya tatra kāryaṃ prakurvate 
dhvajamekaṃ tu sarvatra kecidāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ  BhS 
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dhvajadaṇḍe tu niṣkṛtim 
pramādātpatite bhūmyāṃ dhvaje vātādinā dṛḍhe  BhS 
abhagne vātha bhagne vā dhvajaṃ tatra pūnaḥ kṣipet 
abhagne taṃ dhvajaṃ gṛhya kṛtvā mantreṇa takṣaṇam  BhS 
adhivāsādikaṃ kṛtvā tatthsāne sthāpayedbudhaḥ 
bhagne dhvaje na sagrāhyastamapsu vidhinā tyajet  BhS 
tato 'nyaṃ dhvajamādāya sthāpayedavilaṃbitam 
corādyairbuddhipūrvaṃ vā pātite pūrvavadvidhiḥ  BhS 
tatrādhikaṃ prakurvīta śilpibhistakṣaṇaṃ punaḥ 
abhagnadhvajavatkuryādanyatpūrvavadatvaraḥ  BhS 
bhāgenānupayuktasya dhvajasya tyājyataiva hi 
duṣṭabhāgasya dānena na kadācitparigrahaḥ  BhS 
atha vā sudṛḍaṃ gṛhya pratiṣṭhāṃ mahatīṃ caret 
duṣṭaṃ bhāgaṃ vyapohyaiva pramāṇaṃ lakṣayetpunaḥ  BhS 
pramāṇamapramāṇaṃ vā dhvajaṃ nānyena dāruṇā 
saṃyutāṃ vardhitāṃ kuryādeṣa sārvatriko vidhiḥ  BhS 
yantu tāmrādinā kuryāllohena kavacādikam 
bālālayaṃ prakalpyaiva tatrakāryaṃ samācaret  BhS 
sthitameva dhvajaṃ kuryānna tu taṃ cālayetkvacit 
dagdhaṃ dhvajaṃ parityajya punaranyaṃ samāharet  BhS 
dhvaje 'ntyajātibhisspṛṣṭe mahāśāntimathācaret 
taissamīpamupetaintu sahasrāhutimācaret  BhS 
patite vātyayā caivaṃ dhvajasya śikhare tathā 
mekhalāsu ca tatsarvaṃ navīkṛtya yathāvidhi  BhS 
dhvajadaṇḍe tu saṃyojya pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret 
dhvajasya calane cāpi pramādādvraścane tathā  BhS 
bhagnābhagna dhvajasyoktaniṣkṛtiṃ tu samācaret 
eṣa eva vidhiḥ prokto daṇḍeṣvanveṣu sarvataḥ  BhS 
aśanyādinipātena dhāmanyantarite yadi 
deve naṣṭe dhvaje susthe dhvajasyārādhanaṃ bhavet  BhS 
ālayaṃ ca punaḥkṛtvā tamevārādhayeddhvajam 
nirīkṣyatrīṇi varṣāṇi devāgāre tvanirmite  BhS 
tatra devo na ramate taddhvajaṃ tu tyajetsudhīḥ 
atha vā yatra kutrāpi pratiṣṭhāpya samarcayet  BhS 
atha vakṣye dhvajasthānaṃ yathāśāstraviniścitam 
piṭhagopurayormadhye pañcabhāgaṃ prakalpya ca  BhS 
pīṭhāttyaktyā caturbhāgaṃ pañcame dhvajasaṃsthitiḥ 
tatsaṃdhau tu praśastaṃ syādyathā saṃphavamācaret  BhS 
yadi prākārabāhye syāddhvajaśśāstravadācaret 
anuktasthānanihitaṃ taṃ ca śāstravadācaret  BhS 
aśaktau punaranyaṃ ca prākāraṃ kārayetkramāt 
devadṛgviṣayaṃ kuryāddhvajaṃ laivāparokṣayet  BhS 
yadā cānyālayairvāpi gopurādibhireva vā 
abhyantaraṃ bhaveccettu chidraṃ kuryāttu dṛkpathe  BhS 
vṛkṣādyaiḥpatitairnaṣṭe cālite 'vanate 'pi ca 
taddhyajaṃ pūrvavatkuryāttrimāsābhyantare 'tvaraḥ  BhS 
kṛmyādibhirvihaṅgairvākoṭarādau kṛte dhvaje 
kṛtvā bālālayaṃ paścātsamīkṛtyārcayetpunaḥ  BhS 
rajjubandhādikaraṇe dhvajasyārohaṇe kṛte 
bālālayaṃ na tatra syādvāstuśuddhiṃ samācaret  BhS 
prākṣayetpañcagavyaistu dhvajamantreṇa hūyate 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi niṣkṛtāvarcanakramam  BhS 
uktena vidhinā yatra naṣṭe duṣṭe 'pi vā dhvaje 
punasthsāpanaparyantaṃ kuryādveṇudhvajaṃ śubham  BhS 
atha vā kārayedvidvān suvarṇarajatādibhiḥ 
dhvajaṃ tālonnataṃ sthāpya garbhagehe tu pūjayet  BhS 
adhivāsādi tatsarvaṃ pratiṣṭhoktavadācaret 
acalo veṇudaṇḍaḥ syādgarbhagehe bhaveccalaḥ  BhS 
utsavādau tu sarvatra veṇudaṇḍaṃ samācaret 
caladaṇḍo veṇudaṇḍa iti syādutsavedvayam  BhS 
utsavādau pravṛtte tu uktadoṣe tvayaṃ vidhiḥ 
dhvajasthaṃ garuḍaṃ tasmādavamucya samāhitaḥ  BhS 
nītvātu yāgaśālāyāṃ saṃsthāpya tu samarcayet 
veṇudaṇḍaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sadyastasmin prayojayet  BhS 
mahāśāntiṃ tathā kuryātsahasrāhutimeva ca 
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇudaivatyaṃ gāruḍaṃ dhvājameva ca  BhS 
saudarśanaṃ ca kūśmāṇḍān śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ yajet 
tathaiva dīpadaṇḍasya bhavetsarvatra cakramaḥ  BhS 
dhvaje nāropayeddīpaṃ dīpadaṇḍaḥ pṛthagbhavet 
tatra dīpaṃ samāropya na labhetphalamavyayam  BhS 
dhvaje dīpaṃ samāropya vaiṣṇavaṃ śataśo yajet 
āpatkalpaṃ pravakṣyanti dhvaje dīpāvarohaṇam  BhS 
dīpayukte dhvaje naṣṭe pūrvavanniṣkṛtiṃ caret 
vīśapratiṣṭhāhīne tu dhvajasyārohaṇe kṛte  BhS 
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca nṛsūktaṃ dhvājameva ca 
gāruḍaṃ daśaśo hutvā pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret  BhS 
dhvajadevasya cakrasya śāntanandīśayos tathā 
hīner'cane vaiṣṇavaṃ ca taddaivatyasamanvitam  BhS 
hutvaiva punarabhyarcya paścātkāryaṃ samācaret 
bherītāḍanahīne ca raudraṃ ca vyāhṛtīstathā  BhS 
hutvā mahāvyāhṛtīśca bherītāḍanamācaret 
arcanādiṣu sarvatra yatra ghaṇṭāninādanam  BhS 
eṣa eva vidhiḥ proktaḥ prāyaścittaṃ samācaret 
āropite tu garuḍe hīne caiva nivedane  BhS 
vaiṣṇavaṃ dhvaṃmetrau ca hutvā gāruḍameva ca 
nivedayettudviguṇaṃ kṣama'svetyanumānayet  BhS 
mudgānne tu tathā hīne vaiṣṇavaṃ vāyudaivatam 
āgneyamīṅkārādīṃśca gāruḍaṃ dhvājameva ca  BhS 
hutvā yatnena bahuśo maudgikaṃ ca nivedayet 
varṣavātātapaissamyagupaghātādisaṃbhave  BhS 
viṣṭhādyupahate caiva pakṣiṇāmasakṛtsakṛt 
rajjvāditruṭane caiva pramādātpatane 'pi ca  BhS 
pātite buddhipūrvaṃ vā akāle 'pyavaropite 
śūdrādyairanulomairvā spṛṣṭe dhvajagate paṭe  BhS 
aśuciṃ śodhayitvānyatsamīkṛtyāsamīkṛtam 
utsavādhipadaivatyaṃ ṣaḍvāraṃ juhuyādguruḥ  BhS 
gāruḍaṃ dhvajamantraṃ ca sahastaṃ caiva hūyatām 
tataśśeṣaṃ samāpyeta viparītaṃ na kārayet  BhS 
pramādādbuddhipūrvaṃ vā paṭe dagdhe 'nyamāharet 
śāntiṃ pūrvoditāṃ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret  BhS 
avarohaṇamudvāsantaṃ ca mantreṇa kārayet 
avarohaṇahīne tu mantreṇodvāsanaṃ bhavet  BhS 
tataśśeṣaṃ prakūrvīta aśaktāvavarohaṇe 
apramāṇaṃ paṭaṃ gṛhya mahāśāntiṃ samācaret  BhS 
punaranyaṃ samādāya karmaśeṣaṃ samācaret 
hīne tu cotsavāraṃbhasnapane vaiṣṇavaṃ tathā  BhS 
viṣṇusūktaṃ nṛsūktaṃ ca vāruṇaṃ caiva hūyate 
śuddhodadair abhiṣākassyātprāyaścittavidhissmṛtaḥ  BhS 
hīne kautukabandhe tu vaiṣṇavaṃ śāntameva ca 
saudarśanaṃ ca hutvā tu kautukaṃ bandhayetpunaḥ  BhS 
yajñāgāre kuṃbhavedyāhīne vāpyadhike 'pi vā 
vaiṣṇavaṃ pāvakaṃ bhūmidaivatyaṃ ca hunedbudhaḥ  BhS 
toraṇānāmalābhe tu huneddauvārikānmanūn 
hīnāyāṃ darbhamālāyāmārṣaṃ hutvetarāṅkriyāt  BhS 
alaṅkāravihīne tu śrīdaivatyaṃ tadhā hunet 
prātarbaliṃ tu nirvāpya hīne nityotsave tathā  BhS 
vaiṣṇavaṃ śāntavīśau ca hutvā cotsavadaivatam 
sāyaṃ kuryādutsavaṃ tu dviguṇaṃ kārayetkramāt  BhS 
sāyaṃ hīnaṃ tu dviguṇaṃ prātarutsavamācaret 
ekakālotsavaścettu kṛtvā kāladvayaṃ balim  BhS 
sāyāhne cotsavaṃ kuryātkālātīte 'pyayaṃ vidhiḥ 
digdevatāssamāvāhya prathame 'hani pūjayet  BhS 
prācyādi balidānaṃ syādīśānāntaṃ pradakṣiṇam 
devāhvāne vyatyayassyādvyatīhāro 'tha vā bhavet  BhS 
pūrvoktāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ kṛtvā dviguṇaṃ tu baliṃ dadet 
brahmaṇaśca digīśānāṃ balidānaṃ tu naityikam  BhS 
adāne niṣkṛtiṃ kṛtvā pūrvoktaṃ ṣaḍguṇaṃ baliḥ 
catuṣpathādhidevānāṃ vṛkṣādīnāmathecchayā  BhS 
prathamāvāhanādarvāgvyatyaye pūrvaniṣkṛtiḥ 
prathamaṃ vāstuśuddhissyādya vai dīyate baliḥ  BhS 
antaṃ śuddhyanti rathyāstāśśurdhyanti samaye punaḥ 
akṛtāyāṃ vāstuśuddhau dadyādrathyāsu cedbalim  BhS 
śāntiṃ kṛtvātu pūrvoktāṃ vāstuśuddhiṃ panarbaliḥ 
antaśśace vāstuni tu na balibhramaṇaṃ caret  BhS 
śavamuddhṛtya paścāttu paryagni karaṇaṃ bhavet 
akāle balidānaṃ syādasuraprītivardhanam  BhS 
akāle tu baliṃ datvā kāle tu triguṇaṃ baliḥ 
balibhramaṇadeśassyāddevasya bhramaṇāya hi  BhS 
nānyatra caryā devasya laghuprokṣaṇa manyathā 
na hi śraddhotsave doṣamuśantyenaṃ sa hītaraḥ  BhS 
vāstuvṛddhau tathā hrāse grāmasīmānavīkṛtau 
anumānya ca deveśaṃ śatāṣṭakalaśāplavaḥ  BhS 
kṛtvā sīmāṃ viniścitya tataḥ kāryaṃ samācaret 
astarā cotsavaṃ kuryātsahasrakalaśāplavaḥ  BhS 
devatāvāhanaṃ kṛtvā tathaivotsava mācaret 
devādīnāṃ balaṃ yasmādvardhate sa balissmṛtaḥ  BhS 
śvasūkarādibhirduṣṭairnabhakṣyo balirucyate 
balibhugvāyasaḥ prokto gomukhyā medhyajantavaḥ  BhS 
viparīte mahān doṣastanmantrairhāvayecchatam 
baliśeṣaṃ na śūdro 'dyādarcako baliśeṣabhāk  BhS 
balāvamantrakaṃ kṣipte saṃkṣipte vidhivarjite 
bhakṣite cānulomādyaiḥpūrvoktāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ caret  BhS 
balau paryuṣite 'tyuṣṇe tathā caivānivedite 
nivedanātprāgarvāgvādṛṣṭe śūdrādibhirbalau  BhS 
pūrvoktāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ kṛtvā sarvatra dviguṇaṃ baliḥ 
devatāvāhanaṃ yatra deśeprāk kriyate tataḥ  BhS 
tatraiva balidānaṃ syādyāvadudvāsanaṃ bhavet 
maṇḍalaṃ ca jalaṃ kūrcamāhvānādhāra ucyate  BhS 
rathyāsu balidānāya pīṭhaṃ śailādibhirbhavet 
balidānaṃ tu guptaṃ syānna tatbaśyantyavaidikāḥ  BhS 
tatthsāvaṃ tu tiraskuryātkāle yavanikādibhiḥ 
balipradānahīne tu vaiṣṇavaṃ balirakṣakam  BhS 
hutvā tu niṣkṛtiṃ kuryādbalidānaṃ punastadā 
balidravye 'tha vā pātre patite bhūtale tathā  BhS 
bhinne naṣṭe ca pūrvoktaṃ hutvānyaṃ balimāharet 
balidānaṃ tu kṛtvaiva bhutapīṭhe kṣipettataḥ  BhS 
baliśeṣamanukte tu sthāne buddhyā tu nirvapet 
vaiṣṇavaṃ cākṣahamanuṃ vaiṣvakcenaṃ ca gāruḍam  BhS 
saudarśanaṃ ca hutvaiva bhūtapīṭhe bali kṣipet 
havirnivedane hīnehīne ca dviguṇārcane  BhS 
śāntiṃ ca vaiṣṇavaṃ hutvā tathābhyarcya nivedayet 
yathoktahome hīne tu vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam  BhS 
nṛsūktaṃ ca trayastriṃśatkṛtvo hutvā hunetpunaḥ 
cakravīśāmitānāṃ ca kuṃbhasthānāmathāpivā  BhS 
devānāmarcane hīne vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam 
nṛsūktaṃ sāntamantrau ca gāruḍaṃ cākrameva ca  BhS 
hutvā punassamabhyarcya viśeṣeṇa nivedayet 
devālaṅkaraṇe hīne śrīdaivatyaṃ ca vaiṣṇavam  BhS 
hudvālaṅkāramāsādya vidhīnā bhūṣayedguruḥ 
alaṅkāreṣu dravyeṣu niryāsaṃ candanaṃ sumam  BhS 
taddhitvānyatsamādāya dravyaṃ prakṣālyamantrataḥ 
pañcagavyaissamabhyukṣya tenālaṅkāra ucyate  BhS 
nṛtte geye 'tha vā hīne vaiṣṇavaṃ rudradaivatam 
stotrahīne tathā brāhmaṃ hutvā sārasvataṃ tataḥ  BhS 
bhaktabṛndaiḥ parivṛtau hīnāyāṃ vāruṇaṃ tathā 
vaiṣṇavaṃ śāntadaivatyaṃ hīne picchādike tathā  BhS 
vaiṣṇavaṃ juhuyāttadvaddhavirakṣamanuṃ tataḥ 
yānātkāle yāgaśālāṃ deve na pratigacchati  BhS 
bhavennityārcanaṃ tatra yatradevo 'dhivāsitaḥ 
dhruvārcanaṃ yathā pūrvaṃ na tatrāsti vyatikramaḥ  BhS 
devaṃ pratyāgataṃ dṛṣṭyā punaranyotsavaṃ caret 
dinavyapāye kuryācca tatkālaniyatotsavam  BhS 
atītamutsavaṃ cāpi tantreṇātra samācaret 
taddinepyapramādāccedbhūyātkālasya yāpanam  BhS 
na jahyā devakuryācca tatkālocitamutsavam 
atra pramādetu bhavetpūrvoktaiva hi niṣkṛtiḥ  BhS 
dīkṣito vastramālyādyaiḥ pañcāgārpitabhūṣaṇaiḥ 
carennityaṃ viśuddhātmā viparīte tu doṣakṛt  BhS 
dīkṣāṅgasya tu vastrasya tathā pratisarasya vā 
nāśe tatra mahān doṣastadānyatpunarāharet  BhS 
sahasraṃ viṣṇugāyatrīṃ hutvā śāntimathācaret 
yāvaddīkṣābhavettāvaddīkṣāṅgasya parigrahaḥ  BhS 
antetu tadgatāśaktissvayamevāvahīyate 
atha vā mocanaṃ kuryādite ke cidvadantihi  BhS 
tatra pūrṇāhutiṃ kālaṃ pravadanti vipaścitaḥ 
pratiṣṭhānte tu sā dīkṣā bhavedutsavasaṃgatā  BhS 
na tatra dīkṣāsāṃkaryaṃ dvayamekatra cedyadi 
anyonyaṃ kalahāyante yadyācāryādayaḥkratau  BhS 
mahānanarthastatra syātpratibhūrgururatra hi 
guruvākyaṃ ca rājājñāṃ samamāhurmaharṣayaḥ  BhS 
dīkṣite vartamāne tu nānyaṃ tatra praveśayet 
nahyekasmin bhavetkārya ācāryadvaya saṃgatiḥ  BhS 
pramādādbuddhipūrvaṃ vā kalahe kṣatajasrutiḥ 
kṣatāni vā bhaveyustaṃ visṛjyānyena kārayet  BhS 
na tasya tu bhaveddīkṣā mahāśāntiṃ tu kārayet 
sa dīkṣito bhavedeva pūrvasya pkaṇidhissa hi  BhS 
yāvadāśaucasaṃkrānti rāśaucetvaśucirbhavet 
punaranyaṃ samādāya śeṣaṃ pūrvavadāyaret  BhS 
ādau madhye tadhānte ca hīne brāhmaṇabhojane 
trivākaṃ tu mahāśāntiṃ hutvā brāhmaṇabhojanam  BhS 
dviguṇaṃ kārayeccaiva vaiṣṇavānāṃ tu pūjanam 
punāti pūjitassadyaḥ pāpmabhyo vaiṣṇapassakṛt  BhS 
avaiṣṇavaiśca pāṣaṇḍairūḍhe deve dvanarthakṛt 
taddoṣaśāntaye kuryātsahasrakalaśāplavam  BhS 
avaiṣṇavakṛtāpūjā hanti puṇyaṃ purātanam 
yānāttu patite deve śīghramuddhṛtya sādaram  BhS 
kṣama'svetyanumānyaiva śuddhodairabhiṣicyaca 
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca nṛsūktaṃ sahitaṃ kramāt  BhS 
dinādhipasya daivatyaṃ hutvā cotsavamācaret

śārīrāṇyanyasūtrāṇi tathā svargaphalāni ca  BhS 
vaiṣṇavaṃ sūtrametaddhi sarvasiddhikaraṃ param 
ādyatvātsarvasūtrāṇāṃ vaiṣṇavatvādviśeṣataḥ  BhS 
mayānuvartitaṃ tadvatkāśyapātrimarīcibhiḥ 
yasminneva tu saṃprokte sūtre vikhanasā purā  BhS 
vanasthānāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ vidhiśśrāmaṇakābhidhaḥ 
vānaprasthāstatassvarve yedvijāścānyasūtriṇaḥ  BhS 
tatsūtravidhyamaṣṭhānātsmṛtā vaikhānasā amī 
kiṃ bahūktena vidhinā sarvaṃ vaikhānasaṃ jagat  BhS 
parasmin vyomni yaccār'ke yattejastutrayīmayam 
tadvaikhānaḥ paraṃ brahma iti vedādadhīmahi  BhS 
śāstrametacca sūtraṃ ca sarveṣāmapi jīvanam 
ye vaikhānasasūtreṇa saṃskṛtāstu dvijātayaḥ  BhS 
te viṣṇusadṛśā jñeyāssarveṣāmuttamottamāḥ 
vaikhānasānāṃ sarveṣāṃ garbhavaiṣṇavajanmanām  BhS 
nārāyaṇassvayaṃ garbhemudrāṃ dhārayite nijām 
viprā vaikhānasākhyāye tebhaktāstattvamucyate  BhS 
ekāntinassusattvasthā dehāntaṃ nānyayājīnaḥ 
viṣṇoḥpriyatamā loke catvāraḥ parikīrtitāḥ  BhS 
aśvadthaḥkapilā gāvastulasī vaiṣṇavā dvijāḥ 
dvijeṣu brāhmāṇāśśreṣṭhā brāhmaṇeṣu ca caiṣṇavāḥ  BhS 
vaiṣṇaveṣu paraṃ śreṣṭhā ye vaikhānasasūtriṇaḥ 
vaiṣṇavīṃ pratimāṃ loke vipraṃ vaikhānasaṃ tathā  BhS 
gaṅgāṃ viṣṇupadīṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate mūlamasyāpi śāstrasya 
sārdhakoṭipramāṇataḥ upādiśatsa bhagavān asmabhyaṃ naimiśe vane  BhS 
iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ mahattvaṃ sūtraśāstrayoḥ 
tasmādvaikhānasā viprāssaṃpūjyā bhagavatpriyāḥ  BhS 
pūjānte snapanānte ca tathānte cotsavasya ca 
ācāryamarcakaṃ cāpi sarvān vaikhānasāṃstathā  BhS 
prathamaṃ pūjayitvaiva paścātkāryaṃ samācaret 
yaḥpūjakamanādṛtya vipraṃ vaikhānasaṃ haṭhāt  BhS 
tīrthaṃ gṛhītuṃ prathamcchetsa patati dhruvam yaḥ 
pūjakamanādṛtya vipraṃ vaikhānasaṃ punaḥ  BhS 
prasādaṃ devadevasya prathamaṃ tu jighṛkṣati 
brahmahatyāmavāpnoti tatbūjā niṣpalā bhavet  BhS 
yaḥ pūjakamanādṛtya vipraṃ vaikhānasaṃ punaḥ 
yādṛśīmapi devāgre vāñchatyapacitiṃ janaḥ  BhS 
caturvedyapi so viprassadyaścaṇḍālatāṃ vrajet 
tatpūjā niṣphalā ca syādrājarāṣṭraṃ vinaśyati  BhS 
ṣaṭkālaṃ vā trikālaṃ vā dvikālaṃ kālameva vā 
ālaye bhagavatpūjā saumyena vidhinā kṛtā  BhS 
sarvasaṃpatkarī sā syājjagatāmiti śāsanam 
tatrārcane tu śuddhātmā pūjakaḥ paritoṣitaḥ  BhS 
tena rājā ca rājyaṃ ca yajamānaśca nānvayaḥ 
sarvalokaśca saṃtuṣṭo vardhate brahmatejasā  BhS 
agraṃ vṛkṣasya rājānomūlaṃ vṛkṣasya pūjakāḥ 
tasmānmūlaṃ na hiṃsīyānmūlādagraṃ prarohati  BhS 
phalaṃ vṛkṣasya rājānaḥ puṣpaṃ vṛkṣasya pūjakāḥ 
tasmātpuṣpaṃ na hiṃsīyātpuṣpātsaṃjāyate phalam  BhS 
devasyaṃ brāhmaṇasvaṃ ca sanmānaṃ pūjakasya ca 
yastu na trāyate rājā tamāhurbrahmaghātukam  BhS 
durbalānāmanāthānāṃ bālavṛddhatapasvinām 
anyāyaiḥ paribhūtānāṃ sarveṣāṃ pārthivo gatiḥ  BhS 
rājā pitā ca mātā ca rājā ca paramo guruḥ 
rājā ca sarvabhūtānāṃ paritrātā gururmataḥ  BhS 
dāvāgnidavadagdhānāṃ rājā pūrṇamivāṃbhasā 
samudramiva tṛpyanti brāhmaṇā vedavādinaḥ  BhS 
dahatyagnistejasā ca sūryo dahati raśmibhiḥ 
rājā dahati diḍena vipro dahati manyuvā  BhS 
manyupraharaṇā viprāścakra praharaṇo hariḥ 
cakrāttīkṣṇataro manyustasmādviprānna kopayet  BhS 
agnidagdhaṃ praroheta sūryadagdhaṃ tathaiva ca 
daṇḍyastu saṃpraroheta brahmaśāpahato hataḥ  BhS 
āpadyapi ca kaṣṭāyāṃ nāvamānyo hi pūjakaḥ 
arcakena tu tuṣṭena yaduktaṃ devasannidhau  BhS 
tadvākyaṃ tu ha rervākyaṃ nāvamānyo hi pūjakaḥ 
arcakaṃ kopayedyastu sa hi devasya kopakṛt  BhS 
deveśaṃ toṣayedyastu sa hi pūjakatoṣakṛt 
gandhaṃ puṣpaṃ tathā mālyaṃ tāṃbūlaṃ cākṣatādikam  BhS 
prasādaṃ cāpi devasya prathamaṃ pūjakor'hati 
ṣaḍaṅgaviduṣāṃ caiva kratupravarayājinām  BhS 
vaikhānasaḥ punātyagre goṣṭhīṃ vipraśatasya tu 
phalābhisaṃdhirahitaṃ sarvaṃ karmākhilaṃ kṛtam  BhS 
brahmārpaṇadhiyā kuryātsa bhavedvaiṣṇavottamaḥ 
nānyaṃ devaṃ namaskuryānnānyaṃ devaṃ prapūjayet  BhS 
arcayetsatataṃ dhyāyennārāyaṇamanāyam 
kāyena manasā vācā sa tu vaiṣṇava ucyate  BhS 
tiryakpuṇḍradharaṃ caiva pāṣaṇḍinamavaiṣṇavam 
devāgre pūjaye 'nnaiva tadvaiṣṇavavimānanā  BhS 
abhyarcyā viṣṇubhaktā hi vaiṣṇavā bhagavatpriyāḥ 
avaiṣṇavasya pūjā tu teṣāmagre sudāruṇā  BhS 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena tyajeddūrādavaiṣṇavam 
yetu sāmānyabhāvena manyante puruṣottamam  BhS 
rudrādibhissahājñā nātte 'pi jñeyā avaiṣṇavāḥ 
nareṣu brāhmaṇāśśreṣṭhā brāhmaṇeṣu vipaścitaḥ  BhS 
vipaścitsu kṛtadhiyasteṣu kartāra eva ca 
kartṛṣu brahmaviduṣo ye hi bhaktājanākdane  BhS 
viṣṇubhakteṣu sarvatra śreṣṭhā vaikhānasāssmṛtāḥ 
tasmātsaṃpūjya sarvādau bhaktyā vaikhānasaṃ dvijam  BhS 
viṣṇubhaktaṃ tataḥ pūjya yathāvarṇānupūrvyaśaḥ 
goṣṭhīṃ samarcayetkāle bhojyāścānye dvijātayaḥ  BhS 
strīyaḥ pūjyā vidhānena vaiṣṇapyo vaiṣṇavāśrayāḥ 
na hi sādhāraṇi sṛṣyirvaiṣṇavīti vicintayet  BhS 
janmāntarasahasreṣu tapodhyānasamādhibhiḥ 
narāṇāṃ kṣīṇapāpānāṃ kṛṣṇe bhaktiḥ prajāyate  BhS 
na hyabhāgavatairviṣṇurjñrātuṃ stotuṃ ca tattvataḥ 
draṣṭuṃ vā śakyate mūḍhāḥ praveṣṭuṃ kuta eva hi  BhS 
tadbhaktibhāvitāḥ pūtā narāstadgatacetasaḥ 
bhavantivai bhāgavatāste viṣṇuṃ praviśanti ca  BhS 
aneka janmasaṃsāracite pāpasamuccaye 
vārṣiṇe jāyate puṃsāṃ govindābhimukhī matiḥ  BhS 
pradveṣaṃ yāti govinde dvijān vedāṃśca nindati 
yo narastaṃ vijānīyādāsurāṃśasamudbhavam  BhS 
pāṣaṇḍeṣu ratiḥ puṃsāṃ hetuvādānukūlatā 
jāyate viṣṇumāyātaḥ patitānāṃ durātmanām  BhS 
yadā pāpakṣayaḥ puṃsāṃ tadā devadvijātiṣu 
viṣṭau ca yajñapuruṣe śraddhā bhavati niścalā  BhS 
yathā svalpāna śeṣastu narāṇāṃ pāpasaṃcayaḥ 
bhavanti te bhāgavatā niśśreyaśaparā narāḥ  BhS 
bhrāmyatāmatra saṃsāre narāṇāṃ karmadurgame 
hastāvalaṃbano hyeko bhaktikrīto janārdanaḥ  BhS 
karmaṇā manasā vācā prāṇināṃ yo 'nasūyakaḥ 
bhāvasaktaśca govinde viṣṇau bhāgavato hi saḥ  BhS 
yo brāhmaṇāṃśca vedāṃśca nityameva namasyati 
na drogdhā paravittādeḥ sahi bhāgavataḥ smṛtaḥ  BhS 
sarvān devān hariṃ vetti sarvān lokāṃśca keśavam 
tebhyaśca nāsyamātmāvaṃ sa hi bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ  BhS 
devaṃ manuṣyamanyaṃ vā paśupakṣipipīlikāḥ 
tarupāṣāṇakāṣṭhādīn bhūmyaṃbhogaganaṃ diśaḥ  BhS 
ātmānaṃ cāpi deveśādvyatiriktaṃ janārdanāt 
yo na jānāti puṇyātmā sa hi bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ  BhS 
sarvaṃ bhagavato bhāgo yadbhūtaṃ bhavyasaṃsthitam 
iti yo vai vijānāti sa hi bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ  BhS 
bhavabhītiṃ haratyeṣa bhaktibhāvena bhāvitaḥ 
bhagavāniti yadbhāvassa tu bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ  BhS 
bhāvaṃ na kurute yastu sarvabhūteṣu pāpakam 
karmaṇā manasā vācā sa tu bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ  BhS 
bāhyārthanirapekṣo yo bhaktyā bhagavataḥ kriyām 
bhāvena niṣpādayati jñeyo bhāgavato hi saḥ  BhS 
nārayo yasya susnigdhā na codāsīnavṛttayaḥ 
paśyatassarvamevedaṃ viṣṇuṃ bhāgavatassa hi  BhS 
sutapteneha tapasā yajñairvā bahudakṣiṇaiḥ 
tāṃ gatiṃ na narāyānti yāṃ tu bhāgavatā narāḥ  BhS 
yogacyutairbhāgavataid devarājaśśatakratuḥ 
avāṅnirīkṣyate najrīkimu ye yogapāragāḥ  BhS 
yajñaniṣpattaye vedā devā yajñapateḥ kṛte 
tattoṣaṇāya yatate sa hi bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ  BhS 
yena sarvātmanā bhaktyā viṣṇau bhāvo niveśitaḥ 
yuktatvātkṛtakṛtyatvātsa hi bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ  BhS 
vratināṃ yajñapuruṣaḥ pūjyo viṣṇurasaṃśayaḥ 
strīyaśca svaṃ ca bhartāramṛte pūjyanna daivatam  BhS 
bharturgṛhasthasya sataḥ pūjyo yajñapatirhariḥ 
vaikhānasānāmārādhyastapobhirmadhusūdanaḥ  BhS 
dhyeyaḥ parivrājakānāṃ vāsudevo mahātmanām 
evamāśramiṇāṃ viṣṇussarveṣāṃ ca parāyaṇam  BhS 
na dānairnatapobhiśca prīyate bhagavān hariḥ 
varṇāśramācāravatā yathā sa parituṣyati  BhS 
varṇāśramācāravatā puruṣeṇa paraḥpumān 
viṣṇurārādhyate panthā nānyastattoṣakārakaḥ  BhS 
atrānukteṣu doṣeṣu prāyaścittaṃ pravakṣyate 
paiṇḍarīkāgnimāsādya pariṣicya ca pāvakam  BhS 
ṣaṭkṛtvo vaiṣṇavaṃ tadvaccatuṣkṛtvaśca vyāhṛtīḥ 
aṣṭākṣaraṃ cāṣṭakṛtvastathā ca dvādaśākṣaram  BhS 
hutvā dvādaśakṛtvastu viṣṇusūktaṃ ca pauruṣam 
ekākṣarādisūktaṃ ca śrībhūsūktadvayaṃ hunet  BhS 
devaṃ saṃsnāpya cābhyarcya havissamyaṅni vedayet 
anena vidhinā tatra śāntirbhavati śobhanā  BhS 
hādoṣeṣu ca punaruktahomaissahaiva tu 
pāramātmikamīṅkārādyaṣṭāśītiṃ viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
hutvā ca sarvadaivatyamaṣṭābhiśca śatairghaṭaiḥ 
devaṃ saṃsnāpya cābhyarcya havissamyaṅni vedayet  BhS 
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
athaika triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
saṃprokṣaṇatrayam
atha vakṣyāmi tatroktaprāyaścittasya saṃgraham 
jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caiva laghusaṃprokṣaṇaṃ tathā  BhS 
mahāsaṃprokṣaṇaṃ ceti prāyaścittaṃ tridhā smṛtam 
nimitte samanuprāpte jñātvā gauravalāghavam  BhS 
vakṣyamāṇakrāreṇa sadyassaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret 
saṃprokṣaṇavidhānasya na kālaniyamassmṛtaḥ  BhS 
na kuryānmāsanakṣatra tithivārādyavekṣaṇam 
tasmānnimitte saṃprāpte sadyassaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret  BhS 
deśakālādyavekṣāyā nimitte sati gauravam 
bahubereṣu caikasmin sthāvare jaṅgame 'tha vā  BhS 
arcanāyāṃ vihīnāyāṃ kālātīte viparyaye 
nirmālyapūjane caiva niveditanivedane  BhS 
ekāhe 'pyarcanāhīne nityasnāpanavarjane 
balihomādihīneca nityotsavavivarjane  BhS 
prākārābhyantare prāpte pramādādaśubhe sati 
aspṛśyāgamane tatra caṇḍālādyaiḥ praveśane  BhS 
śvakukkuṭa varāhoṣṭragardabhānāṃ praveśane 
udakyayā sūtikayā pāṣaṇḍādyairathāpi vā  BhS 
kuṇḍagolavratabhraṣṭaturuṣkādipraveśane 
anyasūtridvijaisspṛṣṭe mohādajñānato 'pivā  BhS 
mahāvātahate biṃbe saṃsikte varṣabindubhiḥ 
viṇmūtrarudhirasrāve bahujalpe ca maithune  BhS 
evamādinimitte tu jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret 
naivāsaṃprokṣite biṃbe harirvasati niścayaḥ  BhS 
tasmādbiṃbaviśuddhyarthaṃ saṃprokṣyaiva samarcayet 
doṣādhikye samutpanne laghusaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret  BhS 
rāṣṭrakṣobhe ca durbhikṣe tantrasaṃkaradūṣaṇe 
śūdrairvāthānulomairvāpāṣaṇḍairbhramitairapi  BhS 
udakyayā sūtikayā patitairvātha pātakaiḥ 
caṇḍālādyaiḥ praviṣṭe ca garbhāgāre viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
sūtairvā kuṇḍagolādyaistathā devalakādibhiḥ 
śvakukkuṭa varāhādyaiḥ praviṣṭe gārdabhādibhiḥ  BhS 
ulūkagṛdhrakākādyaiḥ praviṣṭe 'ntargṛhe tathā 
turuṣkādyaiḥpraviṣṭe vā śukraṇoṇitayorapi  BhS 
viṇmūtrādervisarge vā garbhāgārerdhamaṇḍape 
tṣahādūrdhvaṃ vihīne tu pūjane dīpavarjane  BhS 
eka rātramatikramya devegrāmāntarasthite 
āgnidāhe 'śanīpāte garbhāgārer'dhamaṇḍape  BhS 
anyasūtṣarcite biṃbespṛṣṭe vā buddhipūrvakam 
anyairanuktairdeṣaiśca laghusaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret  BhS 
mahānimitte saṃprāpte mahāsaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret 
dvādaśāhātsamārabhya vatsarāntaṃ vidhānataḥ  BhS 
hīnāyāmarcanāyāṃ ca nitye naimittike tathā 
kriyāhīne viparyāse hīne māsotsavādike  BhS 
nityasnapanahīne 'pi mātrādānavihīnake 
balihomādihīne ca saṃprāpte śāstrasaṃkare  BhS 
evamādiṣu hīneṣu vatsarāntaṃ pramādataḥ 
parṣadāṃ parivārāṇāmāśritālayasevinām  BhS 
dhvajārohaṇapūrvaṃ tu kṛte kālotsavādike 
viprādimaraṇe prāpte devāgāre viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
gardabhāśvalulāyoṣṭraśvasūkaramukhe mṛte 
gajādimṛganāśe ca devāgāre pramādataḥ  BhS 
caṇḍālādyantyajātīnāṃ maraṇe vā viśeṣataḥ 
śūdrairvāthānulomairvā pāṣaṇḍaiḥ patitādibhiḥ  BhS 
saṃspṛṣṭe vaiṣṇave biṃbe turuṣkādyairmalimlucaiḥ 
spṛṣṭe caṇḍālakādyairvā mahāpātakadūṣitaiḥ  BhS 
vimāne 'śanipāte vā maholkā patane 'pi vā 
lohito palavarṣe ca vāṃsuvarṣe viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
bhūkaṃpāccalite biṃbe valmīkasya samudbhave 
śithilibhavane vāpi cāṣṭabandhe viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
jīrṇe staṃbhādipatane devāgārena vīkṛte 
agnisparśe ca berasya manuṣyaprasave tathā  BhS 
suthākarmaṇi sarvatra garbhagehādike punaḥ 
biṃbeṣu garbhagehe vā kṛmikīṭādidarśane  BhS 
hasane rodane caiva bhāṣaṇe ca viśeṣataḥ 
svedaśoṇitayorvāpi darśane varṇasaṃkṣaye  BhS 
vimāne maṇḍape vātha yatra kutrāpi vā hareḥ 
devāgāre samutpanne doṣeṣveteṣu vā pṛthak  BhS 
durbhikṣe rāṣṭrasaṃkṣobhe durnimitteṣu caiva hi 
dussvapne bhūmikaṃpe vā pararājādyupadrave  BhS 
bhūgupte coddhṛte biṃbe ciramanyālaye sthite 
atikramya trirātraṃ tu deve grāmāntare sthite  BhS 
kuṇḍagolakasūtādyairdīkṣitairarcane kṛte 
anuktāni ca karvāṇi duritānyadbhutāni ca  BhS 
dṛṣṭvātu yajamānaśca ye tatparisare janāḥ 
grāmasthitā canāścaiva rājā rāṣṭraṃ ca yatnataḥ  BhS 
jñātvā śāstroktavidhinā doṣajaṃ bhaktitaḥ phalam 
mahāsaṃprokṣaṇaṃ kuryānmahādoṣāpanuttaye  BhS 
mahadoṣeṣu sarvatra mahāśāntirvithīyate 
pūrvaṃ sthāpitabiṃbasya na sādhāraṇahetunā  BhS 
syātpunasthsāpanaṃ tasmānmahāsaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret 
mahāsaṃprokṣaṇavidhernūtanasthāpanasya ca  BhS 
svalpo bheda iti proktamṛṣibhiḥ kāśyapādibhiḥ 
jalasaṃprokṣaṇavidhiṃ pravakṣyāmi tapodhanāḥ  BhS 
yajamānābhyanujñāto gurussnātvā vidhānataḥ 
ālayābhimukhe vāpi dakṣiṇe vā manorame  BhS 
sthaṇḍile saikate śuddhe puṇyāhāgnimukhātvaram 
vāstuhomāvasāne ca doṣaduṣṭaṃ tu yat sthalam  BhS 
paryagnipañcagavyābhyāṃ saṃskratya vidhinā budhaḥ 
biṃbaṃ puruṣasūktena kalaśairabhiṣicya ca  BhS 
ṣaṭdroṇadhānya rāśau tu pañcakuṃbhānnidhāya ca 
vastrayugnena saṃveṣṭya pratimāsteṣu nikṣipet  BhS 
nālikerāmrapatrādyairalaṅkṛtya pṛthak ghaṭān 
pañcasūktaṃ japitvaiva pañcaśāntibhireva ca  BhS 
pañcamūrtibhirāvāhya samabhyarcyāṣṭavigrahaiḥ
