sa vā eṣa puruṣaḥ pañcadhā pañcātmeti ca śrutiḥ 
tathā popūyamānaḥ pañcabhissvaguṇairiti  BhS 
ādimūrtistu pañcānāṃ viṣṇurbhedāśca tasyatu 
catasraḥ puruṣādyāssyurmūrtayo bhinnalakṣaṇāḥ  BhS 
tadviṣṇośśramāpanudāya caturguṇā''yeti caśrutiḥ 
tasmādbrahma catuṣpādityucyate vedavedibhiḥ  BhS 
pādādardhāttripādācca kevalācchaktibhedataḥ 
krameṇa dharmajñānaiśvaryavairāgyākhyairguṇairyutāḥ  BhS 
bhavantimūrtayastasmāccatasro viṣayairnijaiḥ 
cāturātmyādādimūrteścatasrastatramūrtayaḥ  BhS 
viṣṇuścaiva mahāviṣṇussadāviṣṇuriti kramāt 
vyāpī nārāyaṇa iti tannāmāni tataḥkramāt  BhS 
viṣṇoraṃśastu puruṣo mahāviṣṇostu satyakaḥ 
sadāviṣṇoracyutassyādyyāpino 'ṃśo 'niruddhakaḥ  BhS 
dharmādibhirbrahmaguṇaiścaturdhābheda īritaḥ 
tṛtīyaṃ vibhavākhyantaṃ viśvamantaramadhyamam  BhS 
nānākārakriyākartṛ rūpaṃ vakṣye mahātmanaḥ 
vibhavā matsyakūrmādyā hayagrīvādayo matāḥ  BhS 
antaryāmisvarūpaṃ tu turīyamidamucyate 
nīvāraśūkavattanvī pītābhā syāttanūpamā  BhS 
tasyāśśikhāyā madhye paramātmā vyavasthitaḥ 
ityuktaśśrutyabhihito hṛdayāṃbujamadhyame  BhS 
jvalanmahāgnau viśvārcirjvālānte viśvato mukhe 
āpādatalacūḍāgraṃ santāpayati santatam  BhS 
śikhā tatra ca pītābhā tanvī nīvāraśūkavat 
madhye śikhāyāstasyāśca jyotiḥ prajvalitaṃ mahat  BhS 
svasaṃkalpaviśeṣeṇa taptajāṃbūnadaprabhaḥ 
pītāṃbaradharassaumyassuprasannaśśucismitaḥ  BhS 
padmākṣo raktanetrāsyapāṇipādaścaturbhujaḥ 
cakraśaṅkhābhayadharaḥ kaṭinyastānyahastakaḥ  BhS 
śrīvatsāṃko mahābāhussarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ 
hṛdi tiṣṭhati sarvātmā śrībhūmibhyāṃ ca pārṣadaiḥ  BhS 
bhrāmayan sarvabhūtāni yantrārūḍhāni māyayā 
antaryāmīti vijñeyassarvakāraṇakāraṇaḥ  BhS 
anyadarcāsvarūpaṃ tu sarvottaraphalapradam 
nityamuktopabhogyatvātparavyūhātmanohareḥ  BhS 
tatkālasannikṛṣṭaikalakṣyatvādvibhavātmanaḥ 
viśuddhairyogasaṃsiddhaiścintyatvādantarātmanaḥ  BhS 
arcātmanyeva sarveṣāmadhikāro niraṅkuśaḥ 
viśeṣabhaktihetutvātpratimārādhanaṃ param  BhS 
arcāvatārassarveṣāṃ bāndhavo bhaktavatsalaḥ 
arcāvatāraviṣaye mayāpyuddeśatastathā  BhS 
uktā guṇā na śakyante vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi 
vicitrā dehasaṃpattirīśvarāya niveditum  BhS 
kalpitā brahmaṇā pūrvaṃ hastapādādisaṃyutā 
mudhaiva jihvā kṛṣṇeti keśaveti na vakṣyati  BhS 
mudhā cittaṃ natadgāmi yadanyatkimito 'dhikam 
sā jihvā yā hariṃ stauti taccittaṃ keśavārpitam  BhS 
tatkarmacārcanaṃ tasya tadanyattu nirarthakam 
sattāmātraṃ paraṃ brahma viṣṇvākhyamaviśeṣaṇam  BhS 
durvicintyaṃ yataḥpūrvaṃ tatprāptyarthamihocyate 
vātormicañcalaṃ cittamanālaṃbanamasthiram  BhS 
sūkṣmatvādbrahmaṇo 'jasya nigrāhyaṃ grāhmadharmaṇaḥ 
samyagabhyasyato 'jasramupabṛṃhitaśaktimat  BhS 
janmāntaraśatasyāpi brahmagrāhyeva jāyate 
yadyastarāyadoṣeṇa nāpakarṣo vicintyate  BhS 
yogino yogarūḍhasya tālāgrātpatanaṃ yathā 
tadāpnoti paraṃ brahmakleśena mahatāpi ca  BhS 
janmāntarābhyāsoddhena vijñānena samādhinā 
viṣṇvākhyaṃ brahmaduṣprāpaṃ viṣayākrāntacetasā  BhS 
manuṣyeṇālpasāreṇa tatprāptau sādhanaṃ tvidam 
surūpāṃ pratimāṃ viṣṇoḥ prasannavadanekṣaṇām  BhS 
kṛtvātmanaḥ prītikarīṃ suvarṇarajatādibhiḥ 
tāmarcayettāṃ vraṇamettāṃ namettāṃ vicintayet  BhS 
viśatyapāstadoṣastu tāmeva brahmarūpiṇīm  BhS 
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ sahitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre trayastriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
atha catustriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
svayaṃvyaktādi sthānapañcakam
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi sthalapañcakakalpanam 
devadevo mahābāhurharirnārāyaṇassvayam  BhS 
yena yena prakāreṇa āvirāstedharātale 
arcāvatārarūpeṇa bhaktasaulabhyahetave  BhS 
svayaṃvyaktaṃ ca divyaṃ ca saiddhaṃ paurāṇameva ca 
pauruṣaṃ ceti kathitaṃ sthalānāṃ pañcakaṃ budhaiḥ  BhS 
svayaṃvyaktaṃ tu tatproktaṃ yatrāsau harivyayaḥ 
svecchayā lokarakṣāye bhūmyāmāvirbhavetsvayam  BhS 
na tatra devadevasya pratiṣṭhā vidhisammatā 
na cāpi karṣaṇaṃ nāpi biṃbaśuddhyādikāḥ kriyāḥ  BhS 
biṃbena saha deveśassannidhatte yatassvayam 
yānadicchā vasedbhūmau tāvatkālaṃ samarcitaḥ  BhS 
svayaṃvyaktasthale pūjā sarvalokaśubhapradā 
svayaṃvyaktasthalānyatra catvāryāsata bhūtale  BhS 
yatra vaikhānasaṃ śāstramāśritya paramaṃ śubham 
arcayāmo jagadyonimahamanye ca te trayaḥ  BhS 
marīcirmandhare viṣṇumarcayāmāsa keśavam 
sarvadevottamaṃ devaṃ śrīnivāse 'trirarcayat  BhS 
kāśyapo viṣṇvadhiṣṭhāne śubhakṣetre 'pyahaṃ bhṛguḥ 
yādṛśīvartate pūjā yā biṃbānāṃ ca saṃsthitiḥ  BhS 
na kiṃ cittāmatikramya pūrvoktāṃ tu samācaret 
svayamāvirabhūddevo yatra bhaktānukaṃpayā  BhS 
kartavyamakhilaṃ tatra tannideśena kalpyate 
na vāpyucchāstrakaraṇaṃ pravartayati mādhavam  BhS 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena pūrvairācaritaṃ caret 
anyathā cettu kurvāṇo devāyaivāparādhyati  BhS 
yanmāyāmohitaṃ sarvaṃ yasyāntaṃ ke 'pi no viduḥ 
tasya devasya māhātmyaṃ vaktuṃ śaknoti ko bhuvi  BhS 
yadyadā caritaṃ tatra tatsarvaṃ śāstrameva hi 
tatrāpi ca viśeṣo 'sti prāyaścittādidarśane  BhS 
sarvaṃ prāmādikaṃ kuryāttatra śāstraṃ pravartakam 
śrutismṛtī ubhetasya paramājñāṃ vadanti hī  BhS 
svayaṃvyaktasthale pūjā sarvalokaśūbhāvahā 
svayaṃ vyakto jagannāthastādātmyena śilādiṣu  BhS 
svayaṃ bhaktajanābhīṣṭān vicāryaiva prayacchati 
na hyatra sādhanāpekṣā svayaṃnyaktastato varaḥ  BhS 
devaiḥ pratiṣṭhito yatra harirāvirbabhūva hi 
taddidyasthalamuddiṣṭaṃ devo divya udīryate  BhS 
smṛtā devāstrayastriṃśattāvatkoṭīmitā api 
sarve te phalakāmāssyurve prapadyante yathā harim  BhS 
tāṃstathā bhajate devo yato 'sau karuṇānidhiḥ 
phalārthino yadā devāḥ pratiṣṭhyāpya hariṃ kramāt  BhS 
samabhyarcya ca saṃprāpya vāṃbhitaṃ tadanantaram 
lokānugrahahetor vai tādṛśaṃ devamandiram  BhS 
cirasthāyi ca saṃkalpya yathārhaṃ samapūjayan 
divyasthalasthadevo hi devānāṃ sannidhāpanāt  BhS 
atyantaṃ puṣṭivaḥ proktassarvaśāntikarassṛtaḥ 
divyasthalasthapūjā tu śatayojanavistṛtam  BhS 
punāti parito deśaṃ nātra saṃdeha iṣyate 
divyasthalāni kathitānyasaṃkhyeyāni bhūtale  BhS 
na hi devāssvayaṃ bhūmāvavatīrya kalau kvacit 
pratiṣṭhāṃ devadevasya kurvanti kuhiciddhruvam  BhS 
divyasthalāni bhūbhāge kalau tu viralāni vai 
bhaviṣyanti bahūnyatra luptabūjāni sattamāḥ  BhS 
divyasthalakṛtā pūjā śāstrasiddhā na saṃśayaḥ 
nocchāstraṃ tu pratiṣṭhādi kurvantidivi devatāḥ  BhS 
devāśca devaloke 'pi kṛtvā vaiṣṇavamandiram 
ārādhya ca jagannāthaṃ prāpnuvanti phalaṃ bahu  BhS 
yā tu bhūmitale pūjā tādṛśī divijā na vai 
karmabhūmistu saṃproktā bhūmirdyairna hi tatsamā  BhS 
saṃcintya puṇyaṃ pāpaṃ vā bhūmau lokāntarenarāḥ 
gamiṣyantitato jyāyān bhūbhāgassarvakarmasu  BhS 
tato devāḥ pratiṣṭhāpya cārcayitvā ramāpatim 
arcāvatārarūpeṇa svayaṃ tīrṇāḥ punaḥ punaḥ  BhS 
bhūmisthānakhilān jantūn tāryayiṣyantyanugrahāt 
ato viprāssadā yajñairdānaiśca tapasā muhuḥ  BhS 
toṣayiṣyanti devānvai teṣāmānṛṇyahetave 
devā nisargaripavo manuṣyeṣu bhavantyapi  BhS 
ārādhanena devasya copakurvanti mānavān 
idameva hareḥ pūjābalaṃ saṃpāditaṃ phalam  BhS 
sarve 'pi sāttvikā yānti tuṣyanti svārjitaiḥ phalaiḥ 
na dviṣyanti ripūnvāpi tatro dāharaṇaṃ surāḥ  BhS 
yathā cyavanadharmā syātsvargassvargāśrito 'tha vā 
tathādinyasthalāniha na syuśśāśvatikāni tu  BhS 
divyasthaleṣu sarvatra divyenaivāgamena tu 
vaikhānasena pūjāsītsāhi śrautī ca sammatā  BhS 
prāyaścittocitānyatra nimittāni yadātadā 
śāstroktaṃ kārayedeva nānyathā kārayedvidhiḥ  BhS 
ye tu pūrvārjitaireva tapobhiḥ paramātmani 
raktātmānastapassiddhāssaṃkalpya svatapaḥphalam  BhS 
devadevaṃ jagannāthaṃ nārāyaṇamanāyam 
pratiṣṭhāpya kvacidbiṃbe samabhyarcya viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
ujjīvanāya lākānāṃ pradāsyantīha pūjanam 
sa deśassaiddha ityuktassaiddhā tatrārcanocyate  BhS 
na hi siddhāstapassiddhiṃ kurvanti vibhalāṃ kvacit 
yasyānugrahamicchantastapasyantīha sādhavaḥ  BhS 
yaṃ prasādayituṃ viprā yajñadānādi kurvate 
tasyaivārādhanaṃ hitvā kiṃ siddhāssaṃprakurvate  BhS 
te siddhāste mahātmānaste santa nte tapasvinaḥ 
ye svakarmaphalaṃ devaṃ viditvā śrīpatiṃ harim  BhS 
pratiṣṭhāpya tu tadrūpamarcayanti nirantaram 
na hyanyaḥ prāpaṇe heturarcanānmuktihetave  BhS 
saiddhasthale tu yā pūjā sarvaśāntikarī smṛtā 
pañcāśadyojanaṃ tasya paritaḥ pāvayenmahīm  BhS 
siddhapratiṣṭhitā deśā bahavo viditāḥ purā 
utpadyante bhaviṣyanti santisiddhā dharātale  BhS 
saiddhasthalāni bhūyāṃsi bhaviṣyanti ca santi ca 
siddhā vaikhānasaṃ śāstramāśrityaiva svanirmitam  BhS 
devaṃ saṃpūjayantīha tatprāyaḥ pracalatyapi 
na hi siddhāḥ prakurvantikiñciducchāstramāpadi  BhS 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena sarvaṃ siddhāśritasthale 
kuryādvaikhānasaṃ śāstramāśritya sakalāḥ kriyāḥ  BhS 
siddhā jānanti śāstrārthān siddhā jānanti cāgamān 
siddhāssamarcayantyeva vaikhānasavidhānataḥ  BhS 
yadi siddhāśrito deśaḥpūjyate 'nyaiḥ pramādataḥ 
rājā taṃ tu vicāryaiva punarvaikhānasaiḥkramāt  BhS 
satvaraṃ yājayetkṛtvā prāyaścittaṃ yathāvidhi 
saiddhameke sthalaṃ prāhurārṣametacca sammatam  BhS 
atha paurāṇiko deśaḥ kathyate yatra yatra vai 
gādhā paurāṇikī bhūyāttatpurāṇasthalaṃ matam  BhS 
ajñātakartṛkāṇyatra smaryante prāyaśo bahu 
sthalānīmānitattāni
purāṇāni pracakṣate  BhS 
purāṇāni tvanantāni sthalāni pṛthivītale 
bhavantyatha kalau prāpte lupyante tānyanekaśaḥ  BhS 
daśayojanaparyantāṃ bhūmiṃ tu paritassakṛt 
punāti deśaḥ paurāṇastatra kiṃ cinna hīyate  BhS 
svayaṃvyaktādayassarve paurāṇāḥ kīrtitā api 
svayaṃvyaktādibhedena vyavahārasya darśanāt  BhS 
purāṇatvaṃ ca teṣāṃ syādanyat paurāṇamucyate 
purāṇasthaladevasya pratiṣṭhā vidhisammatā  BhS 
pratiṣṭhite tvavidhinā sthare naiva rameddhariḥ 
na hi vṛddhāssamarcanti biṃbamucchāstranirmitam  BhS 
na hi paurāṇike deśe yajamānasya gauravam 
arthasya gauravaṃ cāpi darśanīyaṃ mahātmabhiḥ  BhS 
yadi paśyedvisūḍhātmā rauravaṃ narakaṃvrajet 
eṣa eva viśeṣassyādanyatsaiddhavadācaret  BhS 
purāṇasthalapūjā tu śāstradṛṣṭena vartmanā 
pramādetu samīkāryāna tena syādvyatikramaḥ  BhS 
mānuṣaṃ pañcamaṃ proktaṃ sthalaṃ yatra viśeṣataḥ 
grāme vā nagare vāpi śāstrokte sumanorame  BhS 
pratiṣṭāpyārcake viṣṇussarvadeveśvareśvaraḥ 
brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyairvaiśyaiśśūdrairvānyairnarottamaiḥ  BhS 
vaikhānasena śāstreṇa pañcarātreṇa vā punaḥ 
mānuṣasthalapūjā tu yojanaṃ paritasthsalam  BhS 
pāpayettasya tu proktāśaktiranyātu tāvatī 
manuṣyāḥ puṇyakarmāṇastatra tatra dine dine  BhS 
preritā bhagavadbhaktyādhanino nirdhanā api 
nirmāya bhagavadgehaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya śriyaḥpatim  BhS 
arcayanti viśeṣeṇa vaikhānasavidhānataḥ 
viśālaḥ pṛthivībhāgaḥ kālo 'nādirantakaḥ  BhS 
śāstraṃ cāpyatigaṃbhīraṃ bhaktāśca bahavo harau 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena sarvasyāpyanuśāsanam  BhS 
proktaṃ vikhanasā pūrvaṃ bhagavacchāstramuttamam 
anenaiva prakāreṇa sarvatrārādhayeddharim  BhS 
bhaktāśca bahudhā śāstraṃ praśaṃsantīdameva hī 
taduktenaiva vidhinā kalpayedālayādikam  BhS 
yathā mānādhikaraṇe mayā proktassa vistaraḥ 
yatra vā dṛśyate bhedo bhagavacchāstraśilpayoḥ  BhS 
śilpaśāstraṃ parityajya bhagavacchāstrataścaret 
pradhānametacchāstraṃ syādbhagavadgehakalpane  BhS 
na tacchāstramanādṛtya kāryaṃ kiṃ citsamācaret 
lobhānmohādathājñānācchāstre 'sminna dhṛtaṃ caret  BhS 
atikramyāpi śāstraṃ tatpūjā niṣbhalā bhavet 
yajamāno vipadyeta tasmādatroktamācaret  BhS 
tenaiva tu vidhānena pratiṣṭhādikamācaret 
aihikāmuṣmikaṃ yasmātphaladvayamavāpyate  BhS 
grāme viṣṇvarcanāhīne viṣṇvarcāhīnaveśmani 
tīrthapānaṃ surāpānamannaṃ gomāṃsabhakṣaṇam  BhS 
devadhāmavihīnaṃ tu śmaśānaṃ grāma ucyate 
gṛhaṃ ca cititulyaṃ syādyatra nārādhyate hariḥ  BhS 
yo mohādatha vālasyādakṛtvā devatārcanam 
bhuṅkte sa yāti narakān sūkareṣvasi jāyate  BhS 
keśavārcāgṛhe yasya na tiṣṭhati śūbhapradā 
tasyānnaṃ naiva bhoktavyamabhakṣyeṇa samaṃ hi tat  BhS 
biṃbaśuddhyādikaṃ kṛtvā śāstroktavidhinā punaḥ 
kalānyāsādikaṃ sarvaṃ vidhāya parameśvaraḥ  BhS 
pratiṣṭhāpyārcyate yatra parito yojanāvadhi 
pūyate 'nugrahādviṣṇoḥ sa deśo 'prākṛtassmṛtaḥ  BhS 
tatra pārṣadasaṃyuktaśśriyā lakṣmyā samanvitaḥ 
yathā ca parame vyomni sannidhatte tathā hariḥ  BhS 
tatra devāstrayastriṃśatpitaraḥ pannagāśca ye 
sādhyā vidyādharā yakṣāssarvā vai devayonayaḥ  BhS 
sarvasaṃvatsamṛddhissyātparjanyo varṣuko bhavet 
vāyurvāti sukhaṃ tatra sūryastapati tejasā  BhS 
candramāśśītalairdeśaṃ sevate kiraṇaistathā 
bhūmissasyavatī ca syātprasannaṃ ca nabho bhavet  BhS 
nakṣatragrahatārāśca prasādābhimukhāssame 
rājanvatī prajā ca syātpaśuputrasamanvitā  BhS 
na vyādhijaṃ bhayaṃ kiṃ cinnāpi jvarakṛtaṃ tathā 
na vyālajaṃ bhayaṃ vāpi bhavedatrana saṃśayaḥ  BhS 
nopaplavo nṛpāṇāṃ vā mṛgāṇāṃ vāpyapāṃ bhavet 
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāśśūdrāstatra nivāsinaḥ  BhS 
sve sve karmaṇyabhiratā bhaveyussukhajīvinaḥ 
āgnihotrāśca hūyante tapyante 'tra tapāṃsi ca  BhS 
dīyante bhūridānāni yatra devo harispvayam 
aprākṛtamimaṃ deśaṃ sannidhānācchriyaḥ pateḥ  BhS 
prākṛtaṃ yo vadenmūḍhassa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam 
aprākṛtamimaṃ devaṃ naro yaścāpanihnute  BhS 
caṇḍālassa tu vijñeyo niṣkṛtirnāsya dṛśyate 
mahāpātakīnāṃ tadvaddṛṣṭaṃ pātakināmapi  BhS 
upapātakināṃ cāpi prāyaścittaṃ viśeṣataḥ 
śāstrāpalāpināṃ naiva prāyaścittaṃ pradṛśyate  BhS 
yastu sāmānyabhāvena manyate sthalamīdṛśam 
brahmahatyāmavāpnoti bhrūṇahatyāṃ tathaiva ca  BhS 
svarṇasteye ca yatpāpaṃ surāpāne ca yadbhavet 
gurutalpasya gamane yaccapāpamudīritam  BhS 
vṛṣalīgamane yacca pāpaṃ sarvaṃ tadaśnute 
nāsti śāstrātparaṃ jñānaṃ nasyāttasmātpravartakam  BhS 
tasmāttasyāvamānena sadyaḥ patati dūṣakaḥ 
tasmin deśe viśeṣeṇa sarvebhāgavatā harau  BhS 
devapādodakādīni pītvā yāsyantisadgatim 
na hi sarvo 'pi sarvatra svayaṃvyaktasthalādikam  BhS 
gatvaivārādhayedviṣṇuṃ sadā taccāpyasaṃbhavi 
ata eva kṛpāsiṃdhurbhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ  BhS 
arcāvatārarūpeṇa grāme grāme gṛhe gṛhe 
avatīrya mahābāhurbhaktasaulabhyahetave  BhS 
arcyate śāstravidhinā tatra kāryona saṃśayaḥ 
tasmādaprākṛtaṃ deśaṃ na brūyātprākṛtaṃ naraḥ  BhS 
na ca sāmānyabhāvena taṃ paśyedyadi paśyati 
naśyatyeva na saṃdeha iti śāstraviniścayaḥ  BhS 
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ sahitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre catustriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
atha pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
phalaśrutiḥ
atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa kriyāyogaśritaṃ phalam 
yastu devālayaṃ dāruśilālohavilekhanaiḥ  BhS 
kārayenmṛṇmayaṃ vāpi tasyānantaphalaṃ smṛtam 
ahanyahani yajñena yajato yanmahatphalam  BhS 
prāpnoti tatphalaṃ viṣṇoryaḥ kārayati mandiram 
kulānāṃ śatamāgāmi samatītaṃ tathā śatam  BhS 
tārayedbhagavadgehamiti buddhiṃ karoti yaḥ 
saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpamalpaṃ vā yadi vā bahu  BhS 
viṣṇorālayavinyāsaprāraṃbhādeva naśyati 
saptalokamayo viṣṇustasya yaḥkurute gṛham  BhS 
pratiṣṭhāṃ samapāpnoti sa narassāptalaukikīm 
praśastadeśe bhūbhāge yo naro bhavanaṃ hareḥ  BhS 
kārayatyakṣayān lokān sa varaḥ pratipadyate 
iṣṭakācayavinyāso yāvadvarṣāṇi tiṣṭhati  BhS 
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi tatkartādivi modate 
pratimāṃ lakṣaṇavatīṃ yaḥ kārayati mānavaḥ  BhS 
kesavasya sa tallokamakṣayaṃ pratipadyate 
ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi sa mogate  BhS 
svargaukasāṃ nivāseṣu pratyekamarisūdanaḥ 
tataḥ prayāti vaikuṇṭhaṃ nissamābhyadhikaṃ mahaḥ  BhS 
pratīṣṭhāpya harerarcāṃ supraśaste niveśane 
puruṣaḥ kṛtakṛtyatvānnainaṃ śvo maraṇaṃ tapet  BhS 
ye bhaviṣyanti ye 'tītā ākalpāḥ puruṣāḥ kule 
tāṃstārayati saṃsthāpya devasya pratiyāṃ hareḥ  BhS 
berapūjā tviyaṃ proktā pūjānāmuttamottamā 
atīte yajamāne 'pi ciramasyā avasthite  BhS 
anuśastāḥ kila purā yameva yamakiṅkarāḥ 
pāśadhaṇḍadharāḥ krūrāḥ prajāsaṃyamanodyatāḥ  BhS 
viharadhvaṃ yathānyāyyaṃ niyogo me 'nupālyatām 
nājñābhaṅgaṃ kariṣyanti bhavatāṃ jantavaḥ kvacit  BhS 
kevalaṃ ye jagannāthamanastaṃ samupāśritāḥ 
bhavadbhiḥ parihartavyāsteṣāṃ nāstyatra saṃsthitiḥ  BhS 
ye tu bhāgavatā loke taccittāstatparāyaṇāḥ 
pūjayanti sadā viṣṇuṃ te vastyājyāḥ sudūrataḥ  BhS 
yastiṣṭhan yassvapan bhuñjan uttiṣṭhan skhaliteṣu ca 
saṃkīrtayati govindaṃ sa vastyājyassudūrataḥ  BhS 
nityanaimittikairdevaṃ ye yajante janārdanam 
nāvalokyā bhavadbhiste tattejo hanti vau gatim  BhS 
ye dhūpapuṣpavāsobhirbhūṣaṇaiścāpi durlabhaiḥ 
arcayanti na te grāhyānarāḥ kṛṣṇāśrayoddhatāḥ  BhS 
upalepanakartārassammārjanakarāśca ye 
kṛṣṇālaye parityājyāsteṣāṃ tripūruṣaṃ kulam  BhS 
yena cāyatanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kāritaṃ tatkulodbhavam 
puṃsāṃ kulaṃ nāvalokyaṃ bhavadbhirduṣṭacakṣuṣā  BhS 
yenārcā bhagavadbhaktyā vāsudevasya kāritā 
narāyutaṃ tatkulajaṃ bhavatāṃ śāsanātigam  BhS 
bhavatāṃ bhramatāmatra viṣṇusaṃśrayamudrayā 
vinājñābhaṅgakṛnnaiva bhaviṣyati naraḥkvacit  BhS 
yajñā narāṇāṃ pāpaughakṣālanāḥ sarvakāmadāḥ 
tathaivejyā jagaddhātussarvayajñamayo hariḥ  BhS 
sthāpitaṃ pratimā viṣṇossamyak saṃpūjya mānavaḥ 
yaṃ yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ taṃ tamāpnotyasaṃśayam  BhS 
yathā hi jvalano vahnistamohānintadarthinām 
śītahānintadanyeṣāṃ svedaṃ svedābhilāṣiṇām  BhS 
karoti kṣudhitānāṃ ca bhojyāṃ pākakriyāṃ śikhī 
tathaiva kāmān bhūteśassadadāti yathepsitam  BhS 
kalpadrumādivahareryadiṣṭaṃ tadavāpyate 
yassadāyatane viṣṇoḥ kurute mārjanakriyām  BhS 
sapāṃsubhumyair
dehasya sarvaṃ pāpaṃ vyapohāti 
yāvantaḥ pāṃsukaṇikā mārjyante keśavālaye  BhS 
varṣāṇi divi tāvante vasatyastamalo naraḥ 
ahanyahani yatpāpaṃ kurute viṣayī naraḥ  BhS 
yo bāhyābhyantaraṃ veśma mārjayetkeśavālaye 
sabāhyābhyantaraṃ tasya kāyo niṣkalmaṣo bhavet  BhS 
gocarmamātraṃ sammṛjya hanti tatkeśavālaye 
sabāhyābhyantaraṃ yacca mārjayedacyutālaye  BhS 
sabāhyābhyantaraṃ tasya kāyaṃ niṣkalmaṣaṃ viduḥ 
udakābhyukṣaṇaṃ viṣṇoryaḥ karoti satā gṛhe  BhS 
so 'pigacchati yatrāste bhagavān yādasāṃ patiḥ 
mṛdā dhātuvikārairvā varṇakairgomayena vā  BhS 
viṣṇorāyatane nityaṃ yaḥ karotyanu lepanam 
pravāte vāti guṇavadvarṣāsvatimanoharam  BhS 
svanuliptaṃ śūbhākāraṃ svakṛhaṃ labhate naraḥ 
pūrṇadhānyahiraṇyādimaṇimuktāphalojjvalam  BhS 
pratyāsannajalopetaṃ gṛhaṃ prāpnoti śobhanam 
sāmantasvajanānāṃ ca sarveṣāmuttamottamam  BhS 
tadāpnoti gṛhaṃ ramyamupalepanakṛnnaraḥ 
yenānulipte tiṣṭanti viṣṇvāyatanabhūtale  BhS 
brāhmaṇāḥkṣatriyā vaiśyāśśūdrassādhvyastriyastathā 
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ vaktuṃ nālaṃ devāssahānugāḥ  BhS 
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇaṃ muktāhālaśatojjvalam 
śreṣṭhaṃ sarvavimānānāṃ svargadhiṣṇyamavāpnuyāt  BhS 
yāvanta stithayo liptā divyābdāṃstāvato naraḥ 
tasminvimāne sa narastsrī vā tiṣṭhati śobhane  BhS 
sraggandhavastrasaṃyuktaḥ sarvabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ 
gandharvāpsarasāṃ saṃghaiḥ pūjyamānassa tiṣṭhati  BhS 
liptā ca yāvatā hastā viṣṇorāyatane mahī 
tāvadyojanavistīrṇasvargasthānādhipo bhavet  BhS 
pūjyamānassuragaṇaiśśītoṣṇādivivarjitaḥ 
manojñagātro viprendraistiṣṭhatyābhūtasaṃplavam  BhS 
tat kṣayādiha cāgatya viśiṣṭe jāyate kule 
atyutkṛṣṭagṛhaṃ prāpya martyaloke 'bhivāñchitam  BhS 
natatra tāvaddāridṣaṃ nopasargona vākaliḥ 
na tāvanmṛtaniṣkrāntiryāvajjīvanti sākṣiṇaḥ  BhS 
viṣṇussamastabhūtāni sasarjaitāni yāni vai 
teṣāṃ madhye jagaddhāturatīveṣṭā vasuṃdharā  BhS 
kṛte sammārjane tasyāstathā caivānulepane 
prayāti paramaṃ toṣaṃ viṣṇurbhūrvaiṣṇavīyataḥ  BhS 
upoṣito naro nārī yaḥkarotyanulepanam 
na tasyajāyate bhaṅgo gārhasthye tu kadā ca na  BhS 
yā ca nārī karotyevaṃ yathāvadanulepanam 
nāpnoti sāpi vaidhavyaṃ gṛhabhaṅgaṃ kadā ca na  BhS 
sarvābharaṇasaṃpūrṇassarvopaskaradhānyavān 
gomahiṣyādisaṃbhāgaṃ gṛhamāpnoti mānava  BhS 
tasmādabhīpsatā samyaggārhasthyaṃ tadakhaṇḍitam 
viṣṇorāyatane kāryaṃ sahasai vopalepanam  BhS 
yaścānulepanaṃ kuryādviṣṇorāyatane naraḥ 
so 'pi lokaṃ samāsādya modatevai śatakratoḥ  BhS 
puṣpaprakīrṇamatyarthaṃ sugandhaṃ keśavālaye 
upalipte naro datvā na durgatimavāpnuyāt  BhS 
snānapānāṃbhasāṃ viṣṇoḥ pradānāttatsalokabhāk 
snānīyadravyadānena nīrogaḥ prītya modate  BhS 
kṣaumādidānādāpnoti paraloke mahatsukham 
ālepanadravyadānātkāmānāpnoti śāśvatān  BhS 
elākarpūratāṃbūlītailādi sparśanātpukhī 
paratreha ca loke syāddīrghakālamasaṃśayaḥ  BhS 
sarvayajñamayo viṣṇurgavyānāṃ paramassmṛtaḥ 
jāyate yeṣu lokeṣu pulakassaṃgamomahān  BhS 
yeṣu kṣīravahā nadyo hradāḥ pāyasakardamāḥ 
tān lokān puruṣā yāntikṣīrasnānakarā hareḥ  BhS 
āhgādaṃ nirvṛtiṃ svāsthyamārogyaṃ cārurūpatā 
saptajanmānyavāpnoti kṣīrasnānakaro hareḥ  BhS 
dadhyādīnāṃ vikārāṇāṃ kṣīratassaṃbhavo yathā 
tathaivāśeṣakāmānāṃ kṣīrasnāpanato hareḥ  BhS 
yathā ca vimalaṃ kṣīraṃ yathā nirvṛtikārakam 
tathāsya nirmalaṃ jñānaṃ bhavatyatiphalapradam  BhS 
grahānukūlatāṃ puṣṭiṃ priyaṃ cāpyakhile jane 
karoti bhagavān viṣṇuḥkṣīrasnāpanatoṣitaḥ  BhS 
sarvo 'syasnigdhatāmeti dṛṣṭimātprātprasīdati 
yassnāpayati devasya ghṛtena pratimāṃ hareḥ  BhS 
indraprasthe dvijāgṣāṇāṃ sa dadāti gavāṃ śatam 
gavāṃ śatasya viprāṇāṃ na dattasya bhavetphalam  BhS 
ghṛtaprasthena tadviṣṇorlabhetsnānopayoginām 
purā rājarṣibhiḥ prāptā saptadvīpā vasundharā  BhS 
ghṛtāḍhakena govinda pratimāsnāpanātkila 
pratimāsaṃ sitāṣṭamyāṃ ghṛtena jagataḥ patim  BhS 
snāpayitvā samastebhyaḥ pāpebhyo 'pi pramucyate 
dvādaśyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ ca gavyena haviṣā hareḥ  BhS 
snāpanaṃ devadevasya mahāpātakanāśanam 
jñānato 'jñānato vāpi yatpāpaṃ kurute naraḥ  BhS 
tatkṣālayati saṃdhyāyāṃ ghṛtena snāpayan harim 
ghṛtakṣīreṇa deveśe snāpite madhusūdane  BhS 
sa gatvāvaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma modate saha sūribhiḥ 
srajaṃ baddhvā sumanasāṃ yaḥ prayacchati viṣṇave  BhS 
sa bhuktvā vipulān bhogānnākapṛṣṭhe virājate 
cāmaravyajana chatradānātsvārājyamaśnu te  BhS 
dānādābharaṇādīnāṃ tejasvī divimodate 
dānācca navaratnāvāṃ devasālokyamaśnute  BhS 
ādarśanapradānena dṛśyassarvairbhaviṣyati 
gandhadravya pradānena sugandhirdāyate bhṛvet  BhS 
dhūpadravyapradānena svasthānaṃ svargiṇāṃ bhavet 
upānahau pāduke ca vāhanaṃ yānameva ca  BhS 
dadāti yo saṃdayitvā
maṇikāñcanacitritam 
sa vimānaṃ tu dutprāpaṃ prāpno tyeva na saṃśayaḥ  BhS 
alaṅkṛtaṃ bhadrapīṭhaṃ prayacchan sarvakāmabhāk 
vinatānandanasthānaṃ dhvajamutpādya darśayan  BhS 
sāmīpyaṃ sahasā viṣṇoryāti sadyo sa saṃśayaḥ 
dhvajaṃ ca vādyamutpādya viṣṇusātkurute tu yaḥ  BhS 
sa divyadundubhi prāyaṃsthānaṃ prāpya virājate 
dāsīdāsaṃ tathātmāna mātmīyaṃ ca prayacchali  BhS 
vāsudevāya dāsyena muktiḥ karatalesthitā 
nṛttabhedairgītabhedais tathā vādyairanekathā  BhS 
śrotavyairapi dṛśyaiśca devadevasya sannidhau 
āsīnamupacāraistairye samārādhayantite  BhS 
pretya divyeṣu lokeṣu pūjyantetairna saṃśayaḥ 
dīpaṃ prayacchati naro viṣṇorāyatane hi yaḥ  BhS 
sadakṣiṇasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnotyasaṃśayaḥ 
āhorātramanirvāṇaṃ dīpamāropayennaraḥ  BhS 
sarvapāpa viśuddhātmā viṣṇuloke mahīyate 
dinedine japannāma keśaveti samāhitaḥ  BhS 
sakṛddadātiyovipraḥpradīpaṃ keśavālaye 
jātismaratvaṃ prajñāṃ ca prākāśyaṃ sarvavantuṣu  BhS 
avyāhatendriyatvaṃ ca samāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ 
sarvakālaṃ ca cakṣuṣmān medhāvī dīpado naraḥ  BhS 
jāyate narakaṃ cāpi tamassaṃjñaṃ na paśyati 
suvarṇamaṇimuktāḍhyaṃ manojñamatiśobhanam  BhS 
dīpamālākulaṃ divyaṃ vimānamadhirohati 
tasmādāyatane viṣṇordadyāddīpaṃ prayatnataḥ  BhS 
tāṃś cadatvānnahīnaste
na ca tailaviyojanam 
kurvīta dīpahartāca mūkū'ndho jāyate jaḍaḥ  BhS 
andhetamasi duṣpāre narake patitān kila 
vikrośamānānmanujān vakṣyanti yamakiṅkarāḥ  BhS 
vilāpairala matrevaṃ kiṃvo vilapite phalam 
tathā pramādibhiḥ pūrvamātmātyantamupekṣitaḥ  BhS 
purvamālocitaṃ naitatkathamante bhaviṣyati 
idānīṃ yātanā bhaugāḥkiṃ vilāpaḥ kariṣyati  BhS 
dehoditāni svalpāni viṣayāścātikarṣakāḥ 
etatkona vijānāti yena yūyaṃ pramādinaḥ  BhS 
janturjanmasahasrebhyo hyekasmin mānuṣo yadi 
tatrāpyativimāḍhatvātkiṃbhogānabhidhāvati  BhS 
ko 'tibhāro harernāmni jihvayā parikīrtite 
varṇite tulyamūletu yadagnirlabhyate sukham  BhS 
ato 'dhikarolābhaḥ kovaścitai'bhavattathā 
yenāyateṣu hasteṣu svātantṣesati dīpakaḥ  BhS 
mahāphalo viṣṇugṛhe na datto narakāpahāḥ 
na vo vilapite kiṃ cididānīṃ dṛśyate phalam  BhS 
asvātantṣe vilapatāṃ svātantṣe tu pramādinām 
avaśyaṃpātinaḥ prāṇā bhoktājīvopyaharniśam  BhS 
dattaṃ calabhate bhoktuṃ kāmayanviṣayāṃstadā 
etatsvātantṣavadbhirvo yuktamāsītparīkṣitum  BhS 
idānīṃ kiṃ vilāpena sahadhvaṃ yadupāgatam 
yadyetadanabhīṣṭaṃ vo yadduḥkhaṃ samupasthitam  BhS 
yadbhūyo 'pi matiḥ pāpe na kartavyā kathaṃ ca na 
pāpakarmaṇinirvṛtte 'pyajñānādaghanāśanam  BhS 
kartavyamapyavicchinnaṃ smaradbhirmadhusūdanam 
vimānamatividyoti sarvaratnamayaṃ divi  BhS 
samāpnoti naro datvā pradīpaṃ keśavālaye 
haviṣāṃ pāyasādīnāṃ haraye ca nivedanāt  BhS 
sukhaikarasapūrṇatmā rājate viṣṇusannidhau 
bhakṣyapānīyabhojyānāmanyeṣāmapi dānataḥ  BhS 
śvetadvīpe tatsamīpe vasanti sukhinassadā 
bahunātra kimuktena vāsudevārthamādarāt  BhS 
dadāti vastudānaṃ
yasthsānaṃ prāpnoti cepsitam 
karmaṇāṃ mārjanādīnāṃ phalabhogādanantaram  BhS 
karmaśeṣaiḥ punarjanma karmānuguṇayoniṣu 
utkṛṣṭāsvena bhoktāro labhante sukhinassadā  BhS 
ārāmāṇāṃ taṭākānāṃ prapāṇāṃ ca pravartanāt 
viṣṇorālayasāmīpye tatphalaṃ kena varṇyate  BhS 
supradarśā balavatī citrā dhātuvibhūṣitā 
upetā sarvabhūtaiśca śreṣṭhā bhūmirihocyate  BhS 
tasyāḥ kṣetraviśeṣāśca taṭākānāṃ ca bandhanam 
audakāni ca sarvāṇi pravakṣyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ  BhS 
taṭākānāṃ ca vakṣyāmi kṛtānāṃ cāpi ye guṇāḥ 
triṣu lokeṣu sarvatra pūjanīyaḥ pratāpavān  BhS 
atha vā mitrasadanaṃ maitraṃ mitravivardhanam 
kīrtisaṃjananaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ taṭākānāṃ niveśanam  BhS 
dharmasyārthasya kāmasya phalamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ 
taṭākaṃ sukṛtaṃ deśekṣetramekaṃ mahāśrayam  BhS 
caturvidhānāṃ bhūtānāṃ taṭākamupalakṣayet 
taṭākāni ca sarvāṇi diśanti śriyamuttamām  BhS 
devā manuṣyā gandharvāḥ pitaro yakṣarākṣasāḥ 
sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni saṃśrayanti jalāśayam  BhS 
tasmāttāṃstu pravakṣyāmi taṭāke ye guṇāssmṛtāḥ 
yā ca tatra phalāvāptirṛṣibhissamudāhṛtā  BhS 
varṣākāle taṭāke tu salilaṃ yasya tiṣṭhati 
agnihotraphalaṃ tasya phalamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ  BhS 
śaratkā le tu salilaṃ taṭāke yasya tiṣṭhati 
gosahasrasya saṃpretya labhate phalamuttamam  BhS 
hemantakāle salilaṃ taṭāke yasya tiṣṭhati 
sa vai bahusuvarṇasya yajñasya labhate phalam  BhS 
yasya vai śaiśire kāle taṭāke salilaṃ bhavet 
tasyāgniṣṭomayajñasya bhalamūhurmanīṣiṇaḥ  BhS 
taṭākaṃ sukṛtaṃ yasya vasantetaṃ mahāśrayam 
atirātrasya yajñasya phalaṃ sa samupāśnute  BhS 
nidāghakāle pānīyaṃ taṭāke yasya tiṣṭhati 
vājimedhapalaṃ tasya phalaṃ vai munayo viduḥ  BhS 
sa kulaṃ tārayetsarvaṃ yasya khāte jalāśaye 
gāvaḥ pibanti salilaṃ sādhavaśca narāssadā  BhS 
taṭāke yasya gāvastu pibanti tṛṣitā jalam 
mṛgapakṣimanuṣyāśya so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  BhS 
yatpibanti jalaṃ tatra styāyante viśramantica 
taṭākadasya tatsarvaṃ pretyānantyāya kalpate  BhS 
durlabhaṃ salilaṃ ceha viśeṣeṇa paratra vai 
pānīyasya pradānena prītirbhavati śāśvatī  BhS 
taṭāke yasya pānīyaṃ pānīyāya jagatpateḥ 
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ vaktuṃ nālaṃ devāssahānu gāḥ  BhS 
taṭāke yasya pānīye sāyaṃ prātardvijātayaḥ 
snātvā kurvanti karmāṇi tasya nākesthitirbhavet  BhS 
taṭāke yasya devasya snāpanaṃ cādhivāsanam 
tasya lokā bhavantyeva pāvanāḥ kṣativarjitāḥ  BhS 
sarvadānairgurutaraṃ sarvadānairviśiṣyate 
pānīyāvāsadānaṃ tu devasyāgre praśasyate  BhS 
atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa vṛkṣāṇāmavaropaṇam 
sthānarāṇāṃ ca bhūtānāṃ jātayaṣṣaṭ prakīrtitāḥ  BhS 
vṛkṣagulpala tāvallyastvakcārāstṛṇajātayaḥ 
etā jātyastu vṛkṣāṇāṃ teṣāṃ rope guṇāstvime  BhS 
kīrtiśca mānave loke pretya caiva phalaṃ śubham 
labhate nāma loke ca pitṛbhiśca mahīyate  BhS 
devalokagatasyāpi nāmatasya na naśyati 
atīte 'nāgate cobhepitṛvaṃ śe 'nyatastathā  BhS 
tārayedvṛkṣarūpī ca tasmādvṛkṣāṃśca ropayet 
tasya putrā bhavantyete pādapā nātra saṃśayaḥ  BhS 
paralokagatassvargaṃ lokāṃścāpnoti so 'vyayān 
puṣpaissuragaṇān vṛkṣāḥ phalaiścāpi tathā pitṛn  BhS

phalodakasnāpanena śubhānīyātphalāni tu  BhS 
snāpanāttu kuśodena brahmavarcasamāpnuyāt 
ratnodakasnāpanena maṇiratnādi vardhayet  BhS

bhavantyoṣadhayassarvāssarvauṣadhyudakāplavāt  BhS

dhātubhiścāpyalaṅkārāddhātuvṛddhirbhaviṣyati

upatiṣṭhejjagadyoniṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti vistṛtam

yathoktānīha labdhvaivaphalāni suciraṃ bhuvi 
ante vimāsamāruhya haimaṃ devaiḥ parīvṛtaḥ  BhS 
kinnarairapsarobhiśca nṛttairgeyaiśca tarpitaḥ 
yakṣairvṛto 'tha gandharvaistsūyāmāno mudānvitaḥ  BhS

yaḥ kuryādvaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma bhaktiśraddhāsamanvitaḥ  BhS

pramādātpatite biṃbe sphuṭate dūṣite 'tha vā

navīkṛtyār'payedyastu tasya pāpaṃ praṇaśyati

prāyaścittanimittāni saṃbhūtānitu dhāmani

tasya tuṣyati deveśaḥ pra hṛṣṭassaṃprasīdati 
prāyaścittānyaśeṣāṇi pāpaughadhvaṃsanāya vai  BhS

na kaścinnācaretkarma śāstroktaṃ sakalaṃ kramāt

tasya puṇyaphalaṃ vaktuṃ na śakyaṃ tridaśairapi

adityamaṇḍalaṃ bhitvā gatvā śubhrāṃśumaṇḍalam  BhS

tathāśeṣaviśeṣaṃ ca nityānandaṃ nirañjanam

śāśvataṃ tatparañjyotiḥ praviśennātra saṃśayaḥ 
atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa kriyālope ca yatphalam  BhS 
nirmātumālayaṃ yastu saṃkalpya matimānnaraḥ

nirmātumicchayā dhāma devasya madhuvidviṣaḥ  BhS 
svayaṃ nivartate yastu tasya syānmahatī vipat

tasya saṃpadvināśassyāt kruddho bhavati cāvyayaḥ  BhS 
pravṛttāyāṃ pratiṣṭhāyāṃ yena kenāpi hetunā

yena vighnastadā bhūyāttaṃ hatvāpi na doṣabhāk 
yastu śāstroditaṃ karma kurvantaṃ ca padārthinam  BhS 
śilpinaṃ vivadenmūḍhastasya nāstiphalaṃ kvacit

adhvare vartamāne tu saṃbhārān śāstracoditān  BhS

arcakaṃ vṛṇuyānno cedyajamāno vinaśyati

kālāvadhiṃ viniścitya yaḥ karmasu niyojayet

ācāryamarcakaṃ kuryāt svasthānādyo 'varopitam

āpadyapi ca kaṣṭhāyāṃ na kadāpyanyamarcakam

taṭākānāṃ sahasreṇa hayamedhaśatena ca  BhS 
gavāṃ koṭipradānena bhūmihartāna śuddhyati

gurumitradhanaṃ caiva svargasthamapi pātayet

ācchettācānumantā ca tānyena narake vaset  BhS

śūdrāhṛtaiḥ krayakrītair arcanaṃ niṣphalaṃ sumaiḥ

pūtigandhograndhāni hyugragandhāni varjayet  BhS

pitarastanna gṛhṇanti bhasmībhavati kāṣṭhavat

tebhyaḥkruddho 'kṣayaṃ duḥkhaṃ krodhādviṣṇuḥ prayacchati

janmadvayaṃ tu vai mūḍhaśśūdratāṃ yāti mānavaḥ 
asūtragrathitaṃ puṣpamasnehāktaṃ tathodanam  BhS 
avālukāyutaṃ toyaṃ sarvaṃ paryuṣitaṃ bhavet

ādarśanavihīne tu kāmilā ca bhaviṣyati

mātrādānavihīne tu sarvanāśo bhaviṣyati 
rakṣānīrājane hīne rāṅgasair

apacārāḥ

paradārāṃśca gacchanti lubdhāssnigdhena cakṣuṣā  BhS 
guroḥkurvanti bhrukuṭīṃ krūranetrāścaye narāḥ 
sūcībhiragnivarṇābhisteṣāṃ cakṣuḥ pravidhyate  BhS 
kṣārādyaiśca kramātsarvairdehe sarvāśca yātanāḥ 
sparśalobhena ye mūḍhāssaṃspṛśanti parastriyaḥ  BhS 
teṣāṃ taptāgnivarṇābhissūcībhirvidhyate karaḥ 
tataḥ kṣārādikaissarvaṃ śarīramanulipyate  BhS 
yātanāśca mahākaṣṭāssarveṣu narakeṣu ca 
pareṣvajanti cātyugraṃ pradīptaṃ lohaśālmalim  BhS 
hanyante pṛṣṭhadeśeṣu punarbhīmairmahābalaiḥ 
dantureṇātikuṇṭhena krakacena balīyasā  BhS 
śilaḥpṛbhṛti pāṭyanteghoraiḥ karmabhirātmajaiḥ 
tenatenaiva rūpeṇa hanyante pāradārikāḥ  BhS 
gāḍhamāliṅgyate nārī jvalantīlohanirmitā 
pūrvākālaṃ jvalantaṃ taṃ pūruṣaṃ lohanirmitam  BhS 
duścāriṇyaḥstrīyo gāḍhamāliṅgantivadanti ca 
kiṃ pradhāvasi vegena na te moho 'sti saṃprati  BhS 
laṅghitaste yathā bhartā pāpaṃ bhuṅkṣva tadādhunā 
lohakuṃbhe vinikṣiptāḥ sāpidhāne śanaiśśanaiḥ  BhS 
mṛdvagninā prapacyante svapāpairiva mānavāḥ 
ulūkhalādyaiḥ kṣodyante prapīḍyante śilāsu ca  BhS 
kṣipyante cāndhakūpeṣu daśyante bhramarairbhṛśam 
kṛmibhirbhinna sarvāṅgāśśataśo jarjarīkṛtāḥ  BhS 
sutīkṣṇakṣurakūpeṣu kṣipyante tadanantaram 
mahajvāle ca narake pāpāḥ pacyanti sarvataḥ  BhS 
itastataśca dhāvanti dahyamānāstadarciṣā 
pṛṣṭhenānīya jaṅghe dve vinyaste srandhayojite  BhS 
tayormadhyena cākṛṣya bāhupṛṣṭhena gāḍhataḥ 
baddhvā parasparaṃ sarvaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ pāparajjubhiḥ  BhS 
piṇḍabaddhaṃ daśantyenaṃ bhramārāstīkṣṇalohajāḥ 
mānināṃ krodhināṃ caiva taskarāṇāṃ ca dāruṇāḥ  BhS 
piṇḍabaddhāssmṛtā yāmyamahājvāle ca yātanāḥ 
rijjubhirveṣṭitāṃgāśca praliptāḥ kardamena ca  BhS 
karīṣavatprapacyante mriyante tena tetathā 
sutīkṣṇakṣāratoyena karmaśānu śilāsu ca  BhS 
apāpasaṃkṣayātpāpā ghṛṣyante candanaṃ yathā 
śarīrābhyantaragataissantataṃ kṛmibhirnarāḥ  BhS 
bhakṣyante tīvravadanairādeha prakṣayādbhṛśam 
kṛmīṇāṃ nicaye kṣiptāḥ pūtimāṃsasya rāśiṣu  BhS 
tiṣṭhantyudvignahṛdayāḥ parvatābhyantarārditāḥ 
sutaptavajralepena śarīramupalipyate  BhS 
adhomukhordhvapādāśca vṛtā stapyanti vahninā 
vadanāntaḥ pravinyastaṃ suprataptamayoguḍam  BhS 
te khādanti parādhīnā hanyamānāśca mudgaraiḥ 
ye devārāmapuṣpāṇi lobhātsaṃsṛhya pāṇinā  BhS 
jighranti mūḍhamanaso śirasā dhārayanti ca 
āropyate śirasteṣāṃ sutaptairlohaśaṅkubhiḥ  BhS 
tataḥ kṣāreṇa dīptena tailatāmrādibhiḥ kramāt 
śarīre ca mahāghorāścitrā narakayātanāḥ  BhS

saṃdaṃśena sutaptena prapīḍyorasi pādataḥ  BhS

nirbhartsayantiye krūrā mātaraṃ pitaraṃ gurum 
teṣāṃ vajrajalūkābhirmukhamādaśyate yataḥ  BhS 
tataḥkṣāreṇa tāmreṇa trapuṇā sicyate punaḥ 
drutair āpūryate 'tyarthaṃ taptalohaiśca tanmukham  BhS 
itastataḥ punardhāvan baddhyate yamakiṅkaraiḥ 
ye nindanti mahātmānamācāryaṃ dharmadeśikam  BhS 
viṣṇubhaktāṃśca sammūḍhāstaddharmaṃ caiha śāśvatam 
teṣāmurasi kanthe ca jihmāyāṃ dantasandhiṣu  BhS 
tālunyoṣṭhe ca nāsāyāṃ mūrdhni sarvāṃgasandhiṣu 
agnivarṇāssutaptāśca triśikhā lohaśaṅkavaḥ  BhS 
āropyante subahuśaḥ sthāneṣveteṣu mudgaraiḥ 
tataḥ kṣāreṇa taptena tāmreṇa trapuṇā punaḥ  BhS 
taptalohādibhissarvairāpūryante samantataḥ 
yātanāśca mahācitrāśśarīrasyāpi sarvataḥ  BhS 
niśśeṣanarakeṣvevaṃ bhramanti kramaśaḥ punaḥ 
ye gṛhṇanti paradravyaṃ padbhyāṃ vipraṃ spṛśanti ca  BhS 
devopakaraṇāṃgaṃ ca jñānaṃ ca likhitaṃ kvacit 
hastapādāghanaiste ṣāmāpūryante samantataḥ  BhS 
kṣāratāmrādibhirdhīptairdahyante kramaśaḥ punaḥ 
narakeṣu ca sarveṣu vicitrā dehayātanāḥ  BhS 
bhavanti bahuśaḥ kaṣṭāḥ pāṇipādasamudbhavāḥ 
pradattāṃ devadevasya tannāmnā pūjakasya vā  BhS 
padārdhināmathānyeṣāṃ haṭhādvṛttiṃ harantiye 
te vai narakakūpeṣu pacyamānāssvakarmabhiḥ  BhS 
vrajantiyātanā bhūyo nātiyantiyāmāṅgaṇam 
ye devāyatanārāmavāpīkūpamaṭhāṅgaṇam  BhS 
upadravanti pāpiṣṭhā nṛpāstatra vasanti ca 
vyāyāmodvartanābhyaṅgasnānapānānnabhojanam  BhS 
krīḍanaṃ maithunaṃ dyūtamaśaucādyācaranti ca 
te nadhairvividhairghorairikṣu yantrādipīḍanaiḥ  BhS 
nirayāgniṣu pacyante yāvadācandratārakam 
devāyatanaparyante devārāme ca kutracit  BhS 
samutsṛjanti ye mūḍhāḥpurīṣaṃ mūtrameva vā 
teṣāṃ śiśnaṃ savṛṣaṇaṃ hanyate lohamudgaraiḥ  BhS 
sūcībhīrnetraparyantair agnivarṇaissakaṇṭakaiḥ 
aropyante gude teṣāṃ yāvanmūrdhni vinirgataiḥ  BhS 
tataḥ kṣāreṇa mahatā tāmreṇa trapuṇā punaḥ 
drutenāpūryate gāḍhaṃ gudaṃ śiśnaṃ ca dehinām  BhS 
manassarvendriyāṇāṃ ca yasmāduktaṃ pravartanam 
tasmādindriyaduḥkhena jāyate tatsuduḥkhitam  BhS 
anna pānamadattaṃ yairmūḍhairnāpyanumoditam 
dhane satyapi ye dānaṃ na ca yacchanti tṛṣṇayā  BhS 
atithiṃ cāvamanyante kālaprāptaṃ gṛhāśrame 
tejohīnā raṇe baddhā hastapādānadhāritāḥ  BhS 
vistāritāṃgāśśuṣyanti tiṣṭhantyabdaśataṃ narāḥ 
hastapādalalāṭeṣu kīlitā lohaśaṅkubhiḥ  BhS 
nityaṃ ca vikṛtaṃ vakraṃ kīlakadvayaghāṭitam 
kṛmibhiḥprāṇibhiścograirlohatuṇḍaiśca vāyasaiḥ  BhS 
upadravairbahuvidhairmukhamantaḥ prapīḍyate

tiṣṭanti laṃbamānāśca lohākārāssuvartulāḥ 
tataḥ svamāṃsamutkṛṣya tilamātrapramāṇataḥ  BhS 
khādituṃ dīyate teṣāṃ sūcyagreṇa ca śoṇitam 
yathā nirmāṃsatāṃ prāptāḥ kālena bahudhā punaḥ  BhS 
tataḥ kṣāreṇa dīptena taccharīraṃ pralipyate 
bhidyante varṣa dhārābhiśśuṣyante vāyunā punaḥ  BhS 
punastailena sicyante sutaptena samantataḥ 
iti citravidhairghorairmadhyamānāssvakarmajaiḥ  BhS 
mriyante naiva pāpiṣṭhā yāvatpāpasya saṃkṣayaḥ 
tasmātpāpaṃ na kurvīta cañcale jīvite sati  BhS 
evaṃ kliṣṭā viśiṣṭāśca sāvaśeṣeṇa karmaṇā 
tataḥ kṣitiṃ samāsādya jāyante dehinaḥ punaḥ  BhS 
sthāvarā vividhāḥ krūrāstṛṇa gulmādibheditaḥ 
tatrānubhūya duḥkhāni jāyante kīṭayoniṣu  BhS 
niṣkrāntāḥ kīṭayonibhyojāyante pakṣiṇaḥ kramāt 
saṃkliṣṭāḥ pakṣibhevena bhavanti mṛgajātiṣu  BhS 
mārgaṃ duḥghamatikramya jāyante paśuyoniṣu 
kramādgoyonimāsādya jāyante mānuṣe punaḥ  BhS 
vyutkrameṇāpi mānuṣyaṃ prāpyate puṇyagauravāt 
tato manuṣyatāṃ prāpya tattatpāpānusārataḥ  BhS 
saṃyutāṃ pāpacihneśca vartante prāṇinastataḥ 
devābhigamanam
snāto dhṛtordhvapuṇḍraśca prayataśśāntamānasaḥ  BhS 
avyagraścānyakāryeṣu gṛhītvā śaktitassvayam 
phalādīnyupahārāṇi gandhān sumanasastathā  BhS

upahārādibhissamyagabhisacchejjagadgurum  BhS 
patraiḥ puṣpaiḥphalair vāpi yathāśakti samarpitaiḥ 
ayatnasulabhenāpi toyenāpi sa tuṣyati  BhS 
pādacāryeva gacchettu devālayamatandritaḥ 
aśakto 'pyatha vāśakta āḍhyo vā durvidho 'dha vā  BhS 
ādhirājye jagaddhāturadhikārī samassmṛtaḥ 
na hi saṃharate jyotsnāṃ candraścaṇḍālaveśmani  BhS 
na vā saudheṣu samrājāṃ sudhādhārāḥ pravarṣati 
bhogāyataname teṣā mekākāraṃ kaleparam  BhS 
anugṛhṇāti dātā tasya noccānaco vidhiḥ viṣṇupāramyam 
devateha parañjyotireka eva paraḥ pumān  BhS 
sa eva bahudhā loke māyayā bhidyate svayā 
viṣṇvākhyassa svayaṃ māyaṃ prakṛtiṃ vyajya sa dvidhā  BhS 
sthitastridhā ca sattvādiguṇabhedātpratīyate

viṣṇvādyā mūrtayastasya dharmajñānādibhedataḥ 
catasra eva vijñeyā vedavarṇa yugāśrayāḥ  BhS 
viṣṇuśca puruṣassatyo hyacyutaśchāniruddhakaḥ 
pañcadhopaniṣadbhedānmahābhūtatvamāgataḥ  BhS 
manaśśrotrādibhiṣṣaḍbhiraṅgaiśca hṛdayādibhiḥ 
ṣaḍakṣarātmako nityamṛṣibhiścaiṣa bhidyate  BhS 
saptavyāhṛtibhirlo kaiśchandobhiḥ kratubhistathā

aṣṭaprakṛtibhiścāsāvaṣṭamūrtibhireva ca

nārāyaṇo nṛsiṃhaśca varāho vāmanastathā

vāyussomastatheśāno brahmānantaścate daśa  BhS 
ekādaśendriyairbhinnas tathā dvādaśamānapaiḥ 
sa trayodaśadhā caiva viśvedevādibhiḥ sthitaḥ  BhS 
sa caturdaśadhā bhinno manubhiścākṣuṣādibhiḥ 
tithibhiḥ pañcadaśadhā bhinno jñeyassu vai prabhuḥ  BhS 
svaraiṣṣoḍaśadhā bhinnodikkoṇāvāntaraistathā 
mūrtyantaraiśca vijñeyo bahudhā tasya vistaraḥ  BhS

dvyādayo viśvataḥpāṇerbhujabhedastathā smṛtāḥ 
vividhābharaṇā dīrghā vividhāyudhadhāriṇaḥ  BhS 
mūrdhānaścaiva tasyoktā lasanmukuṭakuṇḍalāḥ 
haimordhvapuḍralāvaṇyaprabhavā vakrakuntalāḥ  BhS 
smerāruṇādharāssaumyāḥ prasādāmṛtavarṣiṇaḥ

hiraṇyagarbho 'nekātmā vimalaśśyāma eva ca

candrasūryausmṛtau tasya nayane vāmadakṣiṇe

bhruvormadhye tathā rudraṃ bhṛguṃ manasi saṃsthitam

nakṣatragrahatārāśca dantāssyurmaruto 'pi ca

vāyuḥprāṇeṣu vijñeyassādhyāścāṃgulayaḥsmṛtāḥ 
ṛṣayo romakūpeṣu sāgarā vastigocarāḥ  BhS

jānusthāvaśvinau devau parvatāścorusaṃsthitāḥ  BhS

nakhāgreṣu ca vijñeyā divyā oṣadhayas tathā  BhS 
nāsikāyāḥ puṭau jñeyāvayane dakṣiṇottare

lalāṭāgre tathā siddhā bhruvormeghāssavidyutaḥ 
yakṣakinnaragandharvā daiteyā dānavāstathā  BhS

pitaraḥ pretakūśmāṇḍa vetālapramathāstathā  BhS

pārśvayostasya vijñeyāḥkriyā vedairabhiṣṭutāḥ  BhS

nāmnāṃ śataṃ sahasraṃ vā tathānantaṃ paṭhantiyat 
anantānantarūpasya yathāyogaṃ samanvitam  BhS 
mūrtayaścāsya sarvāstāssaṃkhyātītāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
devādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ mūrtayastatra saṃśritāḥ  BhS 
tasmādanantansaṃproktaḥ puṃsūkte tadudīritam 
sahasraśīrṣā puruṣassahasrākṣassahasrapāt''  BhS 
brāhmaṇā mukhate yasya kṣatriyā yasya bāhutaḥ 
ūruto yasya vai jātā vaiśyāśceti narā bhuvi  BhS 
candramā manaso jātaścakṣuṣormihiras tathā 
mūkhādindras tathāgniśca prāṇādvāyurajāyata  BhS 
nābhyāyasyāntarikṣaṃ ca śiraso dyaurajāyata

tamīdṛśaṃ mahāviṣṇumaprameyamanāmayam 
tatprasādādṛte jñātuṃ vaktuṃ vā naiva śakyate  BhS 
sarvadevamayo viṣṇuḥ sarve devāstadātmakāḥ 
aśeṣaṃ vāṅmayaṃ cedaṃ lokālokaṃ carācaram  BhS 
vaiṣṇavyā vyāpyate śaktyā vāyunevadiśo 'ntaram

ādhārādheyabhāvena dvedhāsa vyāpya tiṣṭhati 
sarvabhūtahitāyaiva niṣkalassakalaḥsthitaḥ  BhS 
niṣkalassakalaścaivaṃ jñeyo viṣṇussanātanaḥ 
sarvataḥpāṇipādaṃ tatsarvato 'kṣiśiromukham  BhS 
sarvataśśrutimalloke sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati 
sarvendriyaguṇābhāsaṃ sarvendriyavivarjatam  BhS 
asaktaṃ sarvabhṛccaiva nirguṇaṃ guṇabhoktṛ ca

bhūtabhartṛca tad jñeyaṃ grasiṣṇu prabhaviṣṇu ca

jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ jñānagamyaṃ hṛdi sarvasya viṣṭhitam

sthūlasūkṣmaparatvena tridhā ca bhagavān sthitaḥ  BhS 
prabhaviṣṇurmahāviṣṇussadāviṣṇuḥ smṛtaśca saḥ

viṣṇureva paro devassarva bhūteṣvavasthitaḥ

varāho bhārgavassiṃho rāmaśrīdharavāmanāḥ

purusaṃjñeśarīre 'smin śayanātpuruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ

acyuto 'cyavanādeva sa hariḥ samadīritaḥ 
aniruddhastathā proktassarvasmādanirodhanāt  BhS 
vasanāstarvabhūteṣu vāsudevatvamīyivān 
ādimūrtessamākṛṣṭaḥ smṛtassaṃkarṣaṇaḥ prabhuḥ  BhS 
pradyumno dyumna pṛṣṭhatvāttridhāmā dhāmabhistribhiḥ 
vaikuṇṭhāmalavarṇatvādvaikuṇṭhaśṭāyamucyate  BhS 
līyete pralaye tvasmin keśāvityeṣa keśavaḥ 
naranārīprakartṛtvānnarāṇāṃ cāyanādayam  BhS 
nārāyaṇo naroddhānāmayanatvādapāñca saḥ 
mādhavo madhuṣūtpattyā dhavatvādvā śriyaḥsmṛtaḥ  BhS 
govindatīti govindo gāvo vindanti yaṃ tathā 
asuraṃ madhunāmānaṃ hantīti madhusūdana  BhS 
tribhiḥsvairvikramairvyāpto jagadeṣa trivikramaḥ 
vāmano vrāsvatāyogācchrīdharo vahanācchriyaḥ  BhS

padmaṃ nābherabhūdyapya padmanābhastatasmmataḥ  BhS 
udarālambi dāmāsyetyukto dāmodaro hariḥ 
uttamaḥ puruṣoyasmāduktassa puruṣottamaḥ  BhS 
vilomendriyagamyatvātprocyate sa tvadhokṣajaḥ 
ardhamardhaṃ larassiṃho narasiṃhā udāhṛtaḥ  BhS

indrasyāvarajo bhūta upendraḥ procyate hariḥ  BhS 
haraṇātsarvapāpānāṃ harirnāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ 
karṣaṇātpāparāśīnāṃ kṛṣṇassarvātmako hariḥ  BhS 
rudro rodayate tasmāt brahmā bṛṃhaṇakarmaṇā 
indraśca paramaiśvaryādvahanādvahnirucyate  BhS 
yamassaṃyamanātpuṃsāṃ varaṇādvaruṇastathā

tasyeśvarasya caiśvaryātsarvametatpravartate  BhS

tanmayatvena govinde nyastasarvabharā narāḥ  BhS 
tadyājīno mahābhāgāstaranti bhavavāridhim 
taṃ prasādhayituṃ yatnaḥ kāryassarātmanā naraiḥ  BhS 
bhaktinamrassadā gacchetsarvo 'pi jagataḥ patim 
taddevasya priyaṃ bhūyādyatassammānanaṃ tu tat  BhS 
tasya sannihito devo yasya citte janārdanaḥ 
dānena tapasā nānyaistyasya tuṣṭobhaveddhariḥ  BhS 
āruhya śakaṭaṃ gacchedyo viṣṇormandiraṃ naraḥ 
nārī vā bālako vātha vṛddha ātura eva vā  BhS 
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ nāsti pretya yugyaśca jāyate 
ye vāhayanti tānmartyānnarā vā prāṇinaśca ye  BhS

ye vāhayanti jantūṃstān ste 'pimūḍhāḥ patanti vai  BhS 
yastodayati tāneva gamane mūḍhacetanaḥ 
sa yāmīryātanāḥ prāpya todyate yamakiṅkaraiḥ  BhS 
punaḥ paśutvamāpannastodyate paśubhirnaraiḥ 
yo vā bhṛtakadānena vāhanena tu mānavaḥ  BhS 
vāhayatyatha voheta so 'pi yāsyati durgatim 
apāre durgasaṃsāre karmabaddhe viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
svīyaṃ karma samutsṛjya patanti narake 'śucau

praṇāmaṃ haraye kuryātta sya dūrataro hariḥ  BhS 
devadarṇanamuddiśya naivedaṃ vidha āvrajet

caṇḍālayoni māpnoti janmāni daśa pañca ca

tasyātiriktaṃ no kiñcidviśeṣastatra vakṣyate  BhS

ābrahmastaṃbaparyantaṃ jagadantarvyavasthitāḥ  BhS

narājjātāni tattvāni nārāṇīti pracakṣate

nārāyaṇaḥ paraṃ brahma tattvaṃ nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ

saṃjñābhedairmahātmānassadaivārādhayantitam

tadbhavedanyadevārcā tasmātparimitaṃ phalam

atha śāstravidhirbhinno yatra nāpyupalabhyate 
tatrānyatvaṃ vijānīyānna cecchecchāstrasaṃkaram  BhS

yadanyaṃ sedate vīthyāṃ tatkāle vāhanasthitam  BhS 
so 'pi pāpamavāpnoti viṣṇudhyānena śuddhyati

parvatāgre mahānadyāstīre durgāṭavīṣuvā 
tatra gacchennaro bhaktyā sevetotsavamādarāt  BhS 
saha puttressahāmātyaissarvaiḥ parijanairvṛtaḥ 
vaiṣṇavaṃ kratudeśantu gatvā seveta mānavaḥ  BhS 
yathār'hamupayuñjīta svaśaktiṃ tatkriyāsu ca 
śrutvā devotsavāraṃbhaṃ paṅgūbhāvena yo naraḥ  BhS 
tiṣṭhetsa janmasāhasraṃ paṅgureva bhaviṣyati 
tadbhavedviphalaṃ janma bhūbhārastasya jīvitam  BhS 
deveśasyotsave samyagvartamāne mahāphale 
yo 'nyatra vyāpṛtastatra na gaccheddurmanā naraḥ  BhS 
na tasya niṣkṛtiḥ proktā sa pāpī narakaṃ vrajet 
anāhūto 'dhvaraṃ gacchettathā gurukulaṃ vrajet  BhS 
yo 'dhvaraṃ gantukāmo 'tra pratīkṣetārṅgaṇādikam 
tanya pūrvārjitaṃ puṇyaṃ tat kṣaṇādeva naśyati  BhS 
devotsavaṃ tu yo martyo yatamānaṃ tu sevitum

viṣṇupañcadine vāpi puṇyāheṣvitareṣvapi  BhS

khaṭvāmāsthāya yaśśete vartamāne tadutsave

pratyudthānābhivādābhyāṃ punastān pratipādayet  BhS 
sarveṣāṃ prāṇabhūto 'sau bhagavān hariravyayaḥ 
prāṇinaścetanāssarve prāṇyekaḥ prāṇado 'paraḥ  BhS 
anyathā cenmahādoṣaḥ saṃkṣuphyante ca mānavāḥ 
ekahastapraṇāmena yatpāpaṃ na tadanyataḥ  BhS

aśaknu vānāssvātantṣahatāḥ pāpahatā hatāḥ

ātmanā sa bhavedvāpassa druhyedātmane budhaḥ 
purastāddevabiṃbe tu devyamaṅgalavigrahe  BhS

tathā nirlekhayejjihvāṃ sa pāpī naśyati dhruvam  BhS

ārādhitumathecchedvāsa gacchennarāyutam

mandiraṃ na praveṣṭavyaṃ praviṣṭastu praṇaśyati  BhS

bhuktvāśrāddhaṃ paragṛhe yāyādviṣṇugṛhantu yaḥ 
arcayedvā viśeṣeṇa caṭako jāyate khalaḥ  BhS

tiṣsetsa kānane śūnye kaṇṭakair bahubhirvṛtaḥ 
phalapuhpādihīnaśca śmaśāne

yajña sūtramadhaḥkṛtya karṇe kṛtvā viśeṣataḥ 
apasavyaṃ ca dhṛtvaiva dhṛtvā caiva nivītavat  BhS 
na gaccheddevatāgāraṃ na vā muktaśikho naraḥ 
akacchaḥ pucchakacchaśca nagnaḥ kaupīnamātṛdhṛk  BhS 
riktahastaśśūnyaphālastyaktasaṃvyāna eva ca

ācāralakṣaṇo dharmaḥ santaścāritralakṣaṇāḥ  BhS 
sādhūnāṃ ca yathāvṛttametadācāralakṣaṇam

adharmajñā durācārāste bhavantigatāyuṣaḥ

tatra nācamanaṃ kuryāttadvatsome dvijottamaḥ 
anyadevārthasandiṣṭhaiḥ pūjayeyuśca ye harim  BhS

anarhassarvakarmabhyo sa neyāddevatā gṛham

gacchedanyatra vā prāsyātsopi mūḍho vipadyate

durgandhī jāyate martyojāyate janmapañcakam  BhS

yaḥstriyā sahito mūḍhaśśayīta bhagavadgṛhe

yogibhiryogasiddhyarthamabhyasyante viśeṣataḥ 
āsanāni tvasaṃkhyāni devāgāre na cācaret  BhS 
mantrayogaparaistadvallayayogaparāyaṇaiḥ 
haṭhayogibhiretāni kriyante rājayogibhiḥ  BhS 
svastikaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ siddhaṃ siṃhāsanaṃ tathā 
savyaṃ khūlaṃ sukhaṃ caiva gomukhaṃ garuḍaṃ tathā  BhS 
mayūraṃ matsyamatsyendraṃ maṇḍūkaṃ mudgaraṃ mṛgam

sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ na daivaṃ tasya mṛṣyati  BhS 
tathā strīṇāṃ viśeṣaṇa tyājyā syādatisaṃgatiḥ 
devatāmandiraṃ prāpya kāleṣvanyeṣu vā tathā  BhS 
āyuryaśastapohāniḥ puṃsāṃ strīṣvatisaṃginām 
puruṣeṣvatisaktānāṃ tulyā sā yoṣitāmapi  BhS 
kulīnā rūpavatyaśca nāthavatyaśca yoṣitaḥ 
maryādāsu sa tiṣṭhanti sa doṣaḥ strīṣu garhitaḥ  BhS 
na strībhyaḥ paramanyadvai pāpīyastaramasti vai 
striyo hi mūlaṃ doṣāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ  BhS 
samājñātānṛddhimataḥ pratirūpān va śesthitān 
patīnantaramāsādya nālaṃ nāryaḥ parīkṣitum  BhS 
asaddharmastvayaṃ strīṇāṃ prāyeṇa hi bhavedbhuvi 
pāpīyaso narān yadvai tyaktalajjā bhajantitāḥ  BhS 
strīyaṃ hi yaḥ prārthayate sannikarṣaṃ ca gacchatir 
iṣacca kurute sevāṃ tamevecchanti yoṣitaḥ  BhS 
anarthitvānmanuṣyāṇāṃ bhayātparijanasya ca 
maryādāyāmamaryādāḥ strīyastiṣṭhanti bhartṛṣu  BhS 
nāsāṃ kaścidagamyo 'stināsāṃ vayasi saṃsthitiḥ 
rūpavantaṃ virūpaṃ vā pumānityeva bhuñjate  BhS 
na bhayānnāpyanukrośnānnār'thahetoḥ kathaṃ ca na 
na jñātikulasaṃbandhāt tsriyastiṣṭhanti bhartṛṣu  BhS 
yauvane vartamānānāṃ mṛṣṭābharaṇavāsasām 
nārīṇāṃ svairavṛttīnāṃ spṛhayanti kulastrīyaḥ  BhS 
yāśca śasvadbahumatā rakṣyante dayitāḥstrīyaḥ 
api tāḥ saṃprasajjante kubjāndhajūvāmanaiḥ  BhS 
paṅguṣvanyeṣu kuṣṭheṣu ye cānye kutsitā narāḥ 
strīṇāmagamyo loke 'sminnāsti kaśchidihodyate  BhS 
yadi puṃsāṃ gatistatra kathaṃ cinnopapadyate 
apyanyonyaṃ pravartantena hi tiṣṭhanti bhartṛṣu  BhS 
duṣṭhācārāḥ pāparatā asatyā māyayā vṛtāḥ 
adṛṣṭabuddhibahulāḥ prāyeṇetyavadhāryate  BhS 
alābhātpuruṣāṇāṃ hi bhayātparijanasya ca 
vadhabandhabhayāccāpi svayaṃ guptā bhavanti tāḥ  BhS 
calasvabhāvā dussevyā durgrāhyā bhāvatastathā 
prājasya puruṣasyeva yathā bhāvās tathā strīyaḥ  BhS 
nāgnistṛpyati kāṣṭhānāṃ nāpagānāṃ mahodadhiḥ 
nāntakassarvabhūtānāṃ na puṃsāṃ vāmalocanāḥ  BhS 
rahasyamidamanyacca vijñeyaṃ sarvayoṣitām 
dṛṣṭvaiva puruṣaṃ hyanyaṃ yoniḥ praklidyate striyāḥ  BhS 
kāmānāmapi dātāraṃ kartāraṃ mānasāntvayoḥ 
rakṣitāraṃ na mṛṣyanti svabhartāramasat striyaḥ  BhS 
na kāmabhogān vipulān nālaṅkārārtha saṃcayān 
tathaiva bahumanyante yathā ratyāmanugraham  BhS 
antakaḥ śamano mṛtyuḥ pātālaṃ baḍabāmukham 
kṣuradhārā viṣaḥ sarpo vahnirityekataḥ striyaḥ  BhS 
etā hi svīyamāyābhirvañcayantīha mānavān 
na cāsāṃ mucyate kaścitpuruṣo hastamāgataḥ  BhS 
gāvo navatṛṇānīva gṛhṇantyetā navaṃ navam 
śaṃbarasya ca yā māyā yā māyā namucerapi  BhS 
baleḥ kuṃbhīnaseścaiva tāssarvāyoṣito viduḥ 
hasantaṃ prahasantyetā rudantaṃ prarudanti ca  BhS 
apriyaṃ priyavākyaiśca gṛhṇate kālayogataḥ 
yadi jihmā sahasraṃ syājjīvecca śaradāṃ śatam  BhS 
ananyakarmā strīdoṣānanuktvā nidhanaṃ vrajet 
uśanā veda yacchāstraṃ yacca veda bṛhaspatiḥ  BhS 
strībuddhyā na viśiṣyeta surakṣyā na bhavantitāḥ 
anṛtaṃ satyamityāhussatyaṃ cāpi tathānṛtam  BhS 
iti yāstāḥ kathaṃ rakṣyāḥ puruṣairdurbharāḥ striyaḥ 
saṃpūjyamānāḥ puruṣairvikurvanti mano nṛṣu  BhS 
apāstāśca tathā sadyo vikurvanti manaḥ striyaḥ 
na ca strīṇāṃ kriyāḥ kāściditi dharmo vyavasthitaḥ  BhS 
nirindriyā hyaśāstrāśca strīyo 'nṛtamiti śrutiḥ 
śayyāsanamalaṅkāramanna pānamanāryatām  BhS 
durvāgarbhavaṃ ratiṃ caiva dadau strībhyaḥ prajāpatiḥ 
na tāsāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ śakyaṃ kartuṃ puṃsāṃ kathaṃ cana  BhS 
api viśvakṛtā caiva kutastu puruṣairiha 
vācā ca vadhabandhairvā kleśairvā vividhaistathā  BhS 
na śakyā rakṣitāṃ nāryastā hi nityamasaṃyatāḥ 
avidvāṃsamalaṃloke vidvāṃsamapi vā punaḥ  BhS 
pramadāhyutpathaṃ netuṃ kāmakrodhavaśānugam 
nātaḥ paraṃ hi nārīṇāṃ vidyate ca kadā cana  BhS 
yathā puruṣa saṃsargaḥ parametatphalaṃ viduḥ 
ātmacchandena vartante nāryo manmathacoditāḥ  BhS 
na ca dahyanti gacchantyaḥ sutaptairapi pāṃsubhiḥ 
nānilo 'gnirna varuṇo na cānye tridaśāntathā  BhS 
priyāḥ strīṇāṃ yathā kāmo ratiśīlā hi yoṣitaḥ 
sahasrekila nārīṇāṃ prāpyetaikā kadā cana  BhS 
tathā śatasahasreṣu yadi kācitpativratā 
naitā jānanti pitaraṃ na kulaṃ na ca mātaram  BhS 
na bhrātṝnna ca bhartāraṃ na ca putrān na devarān 
līlāyantyaḥ kulaṃ ghnanti kūlānīva saridvarāḥ  BhS 
strīṣvāyāsasametasya ye puṃsaśśakrabindavaḥ 
na te sukhāya mantavyāḥ svedajā iva bindavaḥ  BhS 
kṛmibhistudyamānasya kuṣṭhinaḥ pāmanasya vā 
kaṇḍūyanāgnitāpābhyāṃ yatsukhaṃ strīṣu tadviduḥ  BhS 
yādṛśaṃ vidyate saukhyaṃ kaṇḍūpūyavinirgame 
tādṛśaṃ strīṣu vijñeyaṃ nādhikaṃ tāsu vidyate  BhS 
granthestu vedanā yadvat sphuṭitasya nivartane 
tadvat strīṣvapi vijñeyaṃ na saukhyaṃ paramārthataḥ  BhS 
varcomūtravisargāttu sukhaṃ bhavati yādṛśam 
tādṛśaṃ strīṣu vijñeyaṃ nādhikaṃ tāsu vidyate  BhS 
na cāṇumātramapyeve sukhamasti vicārataḥ 
tathā devotsavādīnāṃ sevā tāsāṃ niṣidhyate  BhS 
na hi svatantrato yoṣijjātu gacchet sthalāntaram 
na hi nirmimate vṛddhā līlayā devamandirān  BhS 
kāmukānāṃ vilāsārthaṃ tasmādyuktataro bhavet 
anugacchetpitā bhrātā bhartā putro 'tha vā yadi  BhS 
tadā devagṛhaṃ yāyānnānyathā jātu kāminī 
dhyāyato viṣayān puṃsassaṃgasteṣūpajāyate  BhS 
saṃgātsaṃjāyate kāmaḥ kāmātkrodho 'bhijāyate 
krodhādbhavati sammohassammohātsmṛtivibhramaḥ  BhS 
smṛtibhraṃśādbuddhināśo buddhināśātpraṇaśyati 
balavānindriyagrāmo vidvāṃsamapikarṣati  BhS 
tasmāt strīyā bhavedvidvānnātisaktaḥ kathaṃ cana 
tasmāt strīṣu na kartavyaḥ prasaṃgo devatākṛhe  BhS 
tathaiva paradārebhyo manaḥ prahiṇuyānna ca 
paradārā na gantavyā narairṛddhimabhīpsubhiḥ  BhS 
na hīdṛśamanāyuṣyaṃ loke kiṃ cana vidyate 
yādṛśaṃ puruṣasyeha paradāraniṣevanam  BhS 
tādṛśaṃ vidyate kiñci danāyuṣyaṃ nṛṇāmiha 
yāvanto romakūpāḥ syuḥ strīṇāṃ gātreṣu nirmitāḥ  BhS 
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi narakaṃ paryupāsate 
atisaṃgaṃ tyajettasmādyoṣitāṃ devamandire  BhS 
yairasabhyaḥ padairarthaḥ padenaikena vā tathā 
gamyate kathanaṃ tādṛgaślīlaṃ parivarjayet  BhS 
aślīlakathanāccaiva bhavedudvejanaṃ nṛṇām 
bhaktānāṃ bhagavadgehe bhaveccittamathāvilam  BhS 
nivarteta manastatra niviṣṭaṃ paramātmani 
tasmādaślīlamābhāṣṭa naraḥ pāpaparo bhavet  BhS 
sa tu caṇḍālatāṃ prāpya jāyate janmanāṃ śatam 
artona praviśedgehaṃ devasya paramātmanaḥ  BhS 
vāyubhūte śarīre 'smin vāyusaṃcārakarmaṇi 
malavāyuvisargastu devagehe viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
pātayetpuruṣaṃ satyamapi vedāntapāragam 
tasmādapānagandhasya visargaṃ naiva cācaret  BhS 
atha vāyunirodhetu vyādhikopo bhaviṣyati 
tasmādvāyuvisargaṃ tu kuryādevāvicārayan  BhS 
iti devagṛhaṃ gantuṃ vyādhito naiva cārhati 
tathā kuṣṭhī viśeṣeṇa pāparogārditāssame  BhS 
udvīkṣituṃ ca deveśaṃ mandire madhusūdanam 
arcituṃ sevituṃ cāpi dātuṃ dravyacayaṃ tathā  BhS 
nārhantiyasmāttatsaktaṃ pāpaṃ sāṃkrāmikaṃ bhavet 
yadyanyathā bhavetsadyassa pāpī saṃprajāyate  BhS 
janmāni nava pañcāpi jāyate malabhuk kṛmiḥ 
yadā viśedgṛhaṃ viṣṇossevārdhaṃ madhuvidviṣaḥ  BhS 
kṛtvopavītavatsamyaguttarīyaṃ manoharam 
seveta devadevaśamupavītaḥ sadā śuciḥ  BhS 
kañcukenāvṛtāṅgastu na gaccheddharimandiram 
naivābhivādanaṃ kuryānnābhivādyaḥ sa uccate  BhS 
uṣṇīṣī na ca seveta naiva pāṇau dhṛtāyudhaḥ 
vastreṇācchādya dehantukambalenetareṇa vā  BhS 
yogacchedvaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma yo vāpi praṇameddharim 
śvitrī saṃjāyate mūḍho navajanmāni pañca ca  BhS 
kṣaumādibhirvā saṃvīto yo naraḥpraṇameddharim 
caṇḍālayonitāṃ yāti nava janmāni pañca ca  BhS 
na jātu tvamitabrūyādāpannopi mahattaram 
tvaṅkāro vā vadho veti vidvatsu na niśiṣyate  BhS 
paranindā parasyaiva puṃso nindā bhaviṣyati 
paranindā ca śāstrasya parasya tu vinindanam  BhS 
paranindā bhavetkrodhātkrodhātsadyo vinaśyati 
nindayā vai pareṣāṃ tu ninditāste punassmṛtāḥ  BhS 
tasmānnidāṃ pareṣāṃ tudevāgre parivarjayet 
tathā parastutiṃ caiva vidhinā saṃtyajennaraḥ  BhS 
paraḥ parātmā puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ procyate tu yaḥ 
tadagre 'nyasya devasya na stutiṃ stāvayennaraḥ  BhS 
yastu sarveśvarādanyamadhikaṃ tasya cāgrataḥ 
pūjayedyadi manyeta pūjārhaṃ vāsa naśyati  BhS 
sarvaṃ jagacca tasyaiva svarūpaṃ paramātmanaḥ 
tathāpi tattadrūṣeṇa tāratamyajuṣā punaḥ  BhS 
pūjyate bhagavān bhaktaistatra śāstroditā gatiḥ 
tasmāddeveśvarādanyadyatkiñcitthsāṇu jaṅgamam  BhS 
pūjārhaṃ vidyate vastu taddhāmani viśeṣataḥ 
tasmātpūjāṃ stutiṃ cānyāmitareṣāmasaṃśayam  BhS 
tyajeddevagṛhe yastu sukhaṃ manyeta jīvitum 
śaktau satyāṃ viśeṣeṇa yastulobhādinā naraḥ  BhS 
gauṇairarcayate viṣṇamupacārairudīritaiḥ 
na tasya vidyate puṇyaṃ sa tūcchāstraṃ vravartate  BhS 
yāvatā kīrtyateśāstre phalamāḍhyadaridrayoḥ 
tattacchaktyarpitaireva yathārhaṃ ca dhanādikaiḥ  BhS 
yathā tuṣyatideveśo muktāhāreṇa bhūbhujām 
tathaiva tulasīdāmnā durvidhasyāpi tuṣyati  BhS 
tasmātkurvīta yatnena śaktilobhaṃ na jātu cit 
anyathā yadi kurvāṇaḥ phalaṃ naiva prapadyate  BhS 
pretya mārjāratāṃ prāpya jāyate janmapañcakam 
viṣaṃ prāśnāti sammūḍho yassvasmai pacate naraḥ  BhS 
yo 'dyādannaṃ kaṇaṃ vāpi yadviṣṇoraniveditam 
sa bhavedbrahmahābhūyaḥ sa bhuṅktepūyaśoṇitam  BhS 
yatpibecca yadaśnīyāt yaccajighrecca dhārayet 
anuliṃpecca yattattannivedyāgre madhudviṣe  BhS 
tanniveditaśeṣaṃ tu bhuñjīyādvopayojayet 
viṣṇorniveditaṃ yastu na bhuṅkte manujādhamaḥ  BhS 
kalpakoṭiśatenāpi niṣkṛtirnāsya vidyate 
niveditaṃ tu yadviṣṇorbhaktebhyastasya dāpanāt  BhS 
prīyat bhagavān devastatparastu bhavennaraḥ 
niveditaṃ yadi brūyāducchiṣṭamiti mandadhīḥ  BhS 
sa tu durgatimāsādya vindate yamayātanāḥ 
vibhūtiṃ samupāśritya yasyānantasya śāśvatam  BhS 
samṛddhā dharaṇī seyaṃ saśailavanakānanā 
yā ca bhūyāṃsi loke 'sminnutpādayati santatam  BhS 
oṣadhīrnikhilā stadvatpuṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca 
tasyānṛṇyasyahetorvaiya teta vidhinā naraḥ  BhS 
yastu nār'payate viṣṇostattatkālodbhavāni tu 
sasyāni cauṣadhīstadvatphalāni kusumāni ca  BhS 
saṃbhṛtāni yathāśakti sabhavedbrahmah naraḥ 
navāni kāle jātāni sasyādīni viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
dhyāyanti devadeveśamabhigantuṃ yatanti ca 
kadarthayantoye mūḍhāsteṣāmabhyarthanaṃ param  BhS 
audāsīnyena tiṣṭhanti svayaṃ vāpyupayuñjate 
teyāntinarakān ghorān kṛtaghnā yāntiyān bahūn  BhS 
śapantyauṣadhayassarvāstasmādbhaktyā viśeṣataḥ 
navaṃ sasyaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ dadhikṣīraṃ ghṛtaṃ madhu  BhS 
yadarhamarpaṇe sarvamagre tasmai samarpayet 
lobhānmohādathājñānādya ucchiṣṭaṃ nivedayet  BhS 
deveśāya viśeṣeṇa sa bhavetpātakī naraḥ 
ucchiṣṭa manyadevasya yo devāya nivedayet  BhS 
so 'pi caṇḍālatāṃ prāpya naśyedeva na saṃśayaḥ 
niveditaṃ tu devasya ya ucchiṣṭena yojayet  BhS 
devānāmita reṣāṃ vā manuṣyāṇāmathāpi vā 
sa pāpī janmasāhasraṃ śvānayoniṣu jāyate  BhS 
na hi devagṛhaṃ gatvā pṛṣṭī kṛtyāsanaṃ caret 
devābhimukha eva syādbhaktassarvātmanānaraḥ  BhS 
na pṛṣṭhaṃ darśayejjātu devāgre hitacintakaḥ 
pārśvatastu caranneva nivartetālayaṃ prati  BhS 
naivānyaṃ praṇamejjātu praviśya harimandiram 
sa hi sarveśvara śśeṣī yastatrāste ramādhavaḥ  BhS 
pūjārhaśca praṇāmārhaḥ pūjārhastatra netaraḥ 
yastathā praṇamenmūḍhassa yāti narakāyutam  BhS 
caṇḍālayonimāsādya bhajate yātanā muhuḥ 
yastu devagṛhaṃ prāptān vaiṣṇavān bhagavatpriyān  BhS 
ācāryamṛtvijaścātha pūjakān paricārakān 
nār'cayenmaunamāsthāya sa vinaśyati sānvayaḥ  BhS 
yadiṣṭaṃ yājakebhyassyātpūraṇāyeva tasyatu 
bhaktāḥ paricareyuśca viśeṣādgrāmavāsinaḥ  BhS 
anyathā cenmadoṣassarveṣāṃ ca vipacadbhavet 
atmānaṃ yo viśeṣeṇastautyahaṅkāra bhāvidaḥ  BhS 
anādṛtya gurūn daivamanibaddhaṃ ca saṃpadet 
avalīptona jānāti doṣamātmani saṃgatam  BhS 
kulavidyātapassampatpramukhairgarvite naraḥ 
na sukhaṃ na ca saubhāgyaṃ yenātmāntūyate svayam  BhS 
tasmādātmastutiṃ kṛtvā naraḥ patati niścayam 
tato janmaśataṃ prāpya mṛgayonau viśeṣataḥ  BhS 
jāyate mriyate 'bhīkṣṇaṃ tasya pāpaṃ mahadbhavet 
yasdevagṛhaṃ gatvā vāñchatyapacitiṃ janaḥ  BhS 
sa tu tit tiritāṃ yāti navajanmāni pañca ca 
deveśasyatu sevārthaṃ varṇānāmānupūrvyaśaḥ  BhS 
adhikāraḥ samākhyātastatkramaṃ na vimānayet 
viśanti garbhagehetu ye vaikhānasasūtriṇaḥ  BhS 
garbhāgāre praveṣṭavyo na hyavaikhānasaḥ kvacit 
antarāle tathā yeṣāṃ sthānaṃ tattu pravakṣyate  BhS 
anye dvijāśca tiṣṭhanti yathā syādāśramakramaḥ 
te dvijāstat strīyaścāpi sevante tatra saṃgatāḥ  BhS 
kṣatrajātā viśeṣaṇa sthitvā caivār'dhamaṇḍape 
deveśamabhisevante tadīyā yāśca yoṣitaḥ  BhS 
saṃgatāśśūdrajātāśca pratilomabhavāścaye 
mahāmaṇḍapamāsthāya sevante puruṣottamam  BhS 
anulomabhuvaścaivaye cānye mlecchajātayaḥ 
gopurādbāhyataḥ sthitvā sevante mandiraṃ hareḥ  BhS 
tāratamyamidaṃ jñātvā seveta satataṃ harim 
devatānindanaṃ kuryādyassa pāpīna mucyate  BhS 
anyadevasamaṃ yastu manyate puruṣottamam 
caṇḍālayonitāmeti nava janmāni pañca ca  BhS 
apahnutya punardevāṃ staddravyādi harettu yaḥ 
sa bhaveddevahā satyaṃ jāyate śvādiyoniṣu  BhS 
tiraskṛtya tathā devān bhagavacchāstrameva ca 
karmāṇi svecchayā kuryātso 'pi syāddevahā naraḥ  BhS 
kathāyāṃ kathyamānāyāṃ devasya madhuvidviṣaḥ 
anādṛtya ca ye yānti te narāḥ pāpakāriṇaḥ  BhS 
toyahīne 'tiraudre ca vane vai śūnyavṛkṣatām 
jāyante saptajanmāni tataścaṇḍālatāṃ yayuḥ  BhS 
deveṣu goṣu vipreṣu devāgāreṣu caiva hi 
vahennaivādhipatyaṃ yannāsāvṛddhimavāpnuyāt  BhS 
doṣāśca bahulā stasminnādhipatye smṛtā budhaiḥ 
kāmato 'kāmataścāpi sarvaṃ tasya viceṣṭitam  BhS 
pāpāyaiva bhavettasmādbhūtikāmastu taṃ tyajet 
sevārthināṃ sakāśāttu balātkāreṇa yaḥ prabhuḥ  BhS 
gṛhṇīyāttukaraṃ sadyaḥ patetsa saha tena ca 
devasya sannidhau bhaktairbhaktyāyattu samarpyate  BhS 
patraṃ phalaṃ vā mūlaṃ vā svarṇaṃ vāsāṃsi cetarat 
dāyādyamarcakānāṃ tu yo mohādapanihnute  BhS 
svayaṃ vāpyupayuñjīta sa pāpī narakaṃ vrajet 
viśrāṇayanti haraye yadbhaktā bhaktibhāvitāḥ  BhS 
tannāmnā pūjakāneva jānanti phalabhāginaḥ 
sthirajaṅgamayoḥ pūjā yatassampāditā bhavet  BhS 
tasmādbhagavato nāmnā dattaṃ yaddevamandire 
vihāyābharaṇādīni vāsāṃsyanyatparicchadam  BhS 
devālaṅkārayogyāni mūlyavanti viśeṣataḥ 
arcakā eva gṛhṇīyuḥ pratibadhnīta netaraḥ  BhS 
yastvadhīkāragarveṇa devāgāramupāśritaḥ 
akāle sevituṃ cecchetso 'pi yāsyati durgatim  BhS 
atha vā sevituṃ cecchetkāraṇenāpi kena cit 
ukteṣveva tu kāleṣu seveta matimānnaraḥ  BhS 
antyārcanāvasāne yat kavāṭo badhyate tataḥ 
punarudghāṭanaṃ yāvatpratyūṣe ca bhaviṣyati  BhS 
tāvannaiva hariṃ sevedakālassa viśeṣataḥ 
pratyūṣādyantyakālāntapūjane 'pi tu mantrataḥ  BhS 
tattatkāle kavāṭasya bandhane vihite 'pi ca 
na tadā tāvatī hāniravabaddhe 'pyamantrakam  BhS 
athār'canārhakālepi bhaktānāṃ sevanāya tu 
akālā bahavaḥ proktāstathā yavasikoditā  BhS 
tasmādakālasevāṃ tu vidhinā parivarjayet 
viṣayākrāntacittānāṃ viṣṇvarcanamakurvatām  BhS 
karmabhūmau nṛṇāṃ janma karmāpi vibhalaṃ dhruvam 
yo gurau mānuṣaṃ bhāvaṃ śilābhāvaṃ ca daivate  BhS 
mantreṣu jīvikābhāvaṃ hiṃsābhāvaṃ makheṣu ca 
pūjakeṣu ca pūjāyāṃ nīrasaṃ bhāvameti saḥ  BhS 
sarvadhā ninditavyo hi jīvitaṃ tasya niṣphalam 
kṣamāmantraḥ
atha vakṣye viśeṣaṇa kṣamāmantravidhiṃ param  BhS 
apacāreṣu sarveṣu yaṃ japtvā mucyate naraḥ 
aparādhaḥ kṛto yena jānatā svavaśena saḥ  BhS 
kṣamāmantrasahasrasya jāpenāpi na mucyate 
kṣamāmantrastvaśeṣāghadhvaṃsanakṣama ucyate  BhS 
nārāyaṇa namaste 'stu namo bhaktaparāyaṇa 
namo namo namaste 'stu namaste 'stu namo namaḥ  BhS 
ajñānādarthalobhādvā rāgāddveṣātpramādataḥ 
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama  BhS 
saṃdhyayośca divā rātrau jāgratsvapnasuṣuptiṣu 
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama  BhS 
kāyena manasā vācā sarvairvāpi samuccitaiḥ 
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama  BhS 
tiṣṭhatā prajatā caiva śayyāsanagatena ca 
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama  BhS 
snāsyatā japatā vāpi yajatā juhvatā mayā 
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama  BhS 
bhujatā dhyāyatā nūnaṃ viṣayānupasevatā 
aparādhāḥ kṛtā ye tān kṣamasva puruṣottama  BhS 
mayā vā majjanairvāpi mama bandhubhirevavā 
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama  BhS 
rājñā vā tadamātyairvā rājabhṛtyairathāpivā 
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama  BhS 
ācāryeṇār'cakenāpi bhaktairvāparicārakaiḥ 
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama  BhS 
gāyakairnartakairvātha vāditrāṇāṃ ca vādakaiḥ 
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama  BhS 
praṇavādivisargāntaṃ kriyāsu vidhipūrvakam 
amantramarcane doṣaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama  BhS 
uddhānācchayanā ntantu kriyāsu vividhāsu ca 
śraddhālopakṛtaṃ doṣaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama  BhS 
kaśśaknotyarcituṃ devaṃ tvāmanādyantamavyayam 
tasmādajñānacaritaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama  BhS 
prārthaye devadevaṃ tvāṃ prasīda bhagavanmayi 
prasīdatu ram mahyaṃ tava vakṣaḥsthalālayā  BhS 
iśānā jagato devī mātā nityānapāyinī 
prasīdantu surāḥ sarve prasādādyuvayormayi  BhS 
svastyastu kṛpayāsmākaṃ yuvayoḥ suprasannayoḥ 
upacārāpadeśena kṛtānaharaharmayā  BhS 
apacārānimān tsarvān kṣamasva puruṣottama 
iti vijñāpayedbhūyo bhaktisādhvasabhāvitaḥ  BhS 
tadarthanātparaṃ prītaḥ prasīdati khagadhvajaḥ 
kṣamāmantramimaṃ deyānna cāśuśrūṣave kvacit  BhS 
guhyādguhyatamo gopyassarvadā gurubhiḥ sadā iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ sihitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre ṣaṭtriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
atha saptatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
triyugadharma prapañcaḥ
atha vakṣye laghūktena yugadharmāṃstataḥ param 
kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaśca kaliśceti caturyugam  BhS 
kṛtameva ca kartavyaṃ tasmin kāle yadīpsitam 
na tatradharmāḥsīdanti na ca kṣīyantivai prajāḥ  BhS 
tataḥ kṛtayugaṃ proktamanvarthena guṇena vai 
na tasmin yugasaṃsargevyavāyo nendriyakṣayaḥ  BhS 
nānūyā nāpi ruditaṃ na darpo na ca paiśunam 
na vigraho na vidveṣona mithyā nāpi vañcanam  BhS 
na bhayaṃ na ca santāpo na lobho na ca mānitā 
tadā jyotiḥparaṃ brahma vaikhānasamanāmayam  BhS 
yā gatir yogināmekā hyapunarbhavakāṅkṣiṇām 
viṣṇussarvātmako devaḥ śuklo nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhS 
antaryāmiṇi tasmiṃstu sarvalokamaye harau 
svayaṃ śuklatvamāpanne sarvamacchaṃ bhaviṣyati  BhS 
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāśśūdrāśca bhagavatparāḥ 
svakarmaniratāssarvebhavanti manujāḥ kṛte  BhS 
samāśramaṃ samācāraṃ satyabhūtaṃ taporatam 
vijñānabharitaṃ sarvaṃ jagadbhavati santatam  BhS 
eka vedasamāyuktā ekadharmavidhikriyāḥ 
pṛthagdharmāstveka vedā dharmamekamanuvratāḥ  BhS 
caturāśramayustena karmaṇā kālayoginā 
akāmabhalasaṃyogāḥ prāpnuvanti parāṃ gatim  BhS 
kṛte yuge catuṣpādaścāturvarṇyasya śāśvataḥ 
etatkṛtayugaṃ nāma traiguṇyaguṇavarjitam  BhS 
tatastretāyugaṃ nāma yatra dharmastrī pādbhavet 
raktatāṃ tu samabhyeti harirnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ  BhS 
satyapravṛttāśca narāḥ dānadharmaparāyaṇāḥ 
yajante vividhairyajñairnārāyaṇamanāmayam  BhS 
brāhmaṇādyāssvadharmeṣu pravartante nirantaram 
yato dharmapade vṛddhā dvāparaṃ pratipedare  BhS 
yugaṃ saṃśīnadharmatvāddvāparaṃ paricakṣate 
viṣṇuḥ pītatvamabhyeti vedaścāpi vibhajyate  BhS 
dvipādbhavati vaidharmo dvāpare samupasthite 
dvivedāścaikavedāśca nirvedāśca tathā pare  BhS 
vibhinnaśāstraniṣṭhāśca bhavanti vividhakriyāḥ 
prajā dānaparā bhūtvā dānaṃ śaṃsanti santatam  BhS 
rājasaṃ bhāvamāśritya rājasī bhavati prajā 
sattvātpracyavamānānāṃ vyādhayo bhṛśadāruṇāḥ  BhS 
atyāhitāni cānyāni bhaveṣyantyadharottaram 
kālasya hrasvatāyogāccaturthaṃ syādyugaṃ kaliḥ  BhS 
pratyakṣarūpadhṛgdevo na kalau dṛśyate yataḥ 
kṛtādiṣviva tenaiva triyugaḥ kalirucyate  BhS 
padenaikena vai dharmaḥ pravarteta kalau yuge 
tasmiṃstu samanuprāpte na dharmassaṃpravartate  BhS 
tāmasaṃ yugamāsādya hariḥ kṛṣṇatvameti ca 
yaḥ kaścidatra dharmātmā kriyoyogarato bhavet  BhS 
naraṃ dharmaparaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve 'sūyāṃ prakurvate 
varṇāśramāśritācārāḥ praṇaśyantina saṃśayaḥ  BhS 
vratācārāḥ praṇaśyanti dhyānayajñādayastathā 
upadravā janiṣyanti hyadharmasya pravartanāt  BhS 
asūyāniratāssarve daṃbhācāraparāyaṇāḥ 
prajāścālpāyuṣassarve bhaviṣyantikalau yuge  BhS 
sarvedharmāḥ praṇaśyanti kṛṣṇe kṛṣmatvamāgate 
yasmātkalirmahāghorassarvapāpasya sādhakaḥ  BhS 
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāśśūdrā dharmaparāṅmukhāḥ 
ghore kaliyuge prāpte dvijā vedaparāṅmukhāḥ  BhS 
vyājadharmaparāssarve vṛdhāhaṅkāra dūṣitāḥ 
sarvamākṣipyate nityaṃ naraiḥ paṇḍitamānibhiḥ  BhS 
ahamevādhika iti sarvo vivadate janaḥ 
adharmalolupāssarve tathā caiva dvijātayaḥ  BhS 
atastvalpāyuṣassarve bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge 
alpāyuṣṭvānmanuṣyāṇāṃ na vidyāgrahaṇaṃ bhavet  BhS 
vidyāgrahaṇaśūnyatvādadharmassaṃpravartate 
vyutkrameṇa prajāssarvā mriyante pāpatarparāḥ  BhS 
brāhmaṇādyāstathā varṇāssaṃkīryante parasbaram 
kāmakrodhaparā mūḍhā vṛdhāhaṃ kārapūritāḥ  BhS 
baddhavairā bhaviṣyanti parasparavadhepsavaḥ 
janāssarve dayāhīnā dākṣiṇya parivarjitā  BhS 
śūdratulyā bhaviṣyanti tapassatyavivarjitāḥ 
uttamā nīcatāṃ yānti nīcāścottamatāṃ tathā  BhS 
rājāno dravyaniratā lobhamohaparāyaṇāḥ 
dharmakañcukasaṃvītā dharmavidhvaṃsakāriṇaḥ  BhS 
yo yo 'śvarathanāgāḍhyassa sa rājā bhaviṣyati 
kiṅkarāśca bhaviṣyanti śūdrāṇāṃ cadvijātayaḥ  BhS 
mlecchāśca yunādyāśca pālayanti vasuṃdharām 
anāvṛṣṭibhayātprāyo gaganādattacakṣuṣaḥ  BhS 
bhaviṣyanti narāssarve sadā kṣudbhayakātarāḥ 
kalau narābhaviṣyanti svalpabhāgyā bahuprajāḥ  BhS 
pativākyamanādṛtya sadānyagṛhatatparāḥ 
duśśīlā duṣṭaśīleṣu kariṣyanti spṛhāṃ striyaḥ  BhS 
paruṣānṛtabhāṣiṇyo dehasaṃskāra varjitāḥ 
vācālāśca bhaviṣyantikalau prāpte sadā striyaḥ  BhS 
nagareṣu ca grāmeṣu prākārāṭṭādikān janāḥ 
corādibhayabhītāśca kāṣṭhayantrāṇi kurvate  BhS 
durbhikṣakarapīḍābhiratīvopadrutā janāḥ 
godhūmānnayavānnāḍhyān deśān prāpsyanti duḥkhitāḥ  BhS 
svakāryasiddhiparyantaṃ snihyantyanyeṣu mānavāḥ 
bhikṣavaścāpi mitrādisnehasaṃbandhayantritāḥ  BhS 
annopādhinimittena śiṣyān gṛhṇanti sarvataḥ 
ubhābhyāmapi hastābhyāṃ śiraḥkaṇḍūyanaṃ striyaḥ  BhS 
kurvantyo bhartṛmukhyānāmājñāṃ bhetsyantyānādṛtāḥ 
pāṣaṇḍālāpaniratāḥ pāṣaṇḍijanasaṃginaḥ  BhS 
bhaviṣyanti yadā viprā stadā vṛddhimiyātkaliḥ 
alpodakāstathā meghā alpasasyā vasuṃdharā  BhS 
alpakṣīrāstathā gāvaḥ kṣīrātsarpirna jāyate 
ekavarṇā bhaviṣyanti varṇāścatvāra eva ca  BhS 
nāsti varṇāntaraṃ tatralayaṃ yāsyanti mānavāḥ 
santassīdantyasantaśca vilasantisamantataḥ  BhS 
maitrī parajane bhūyādvairaṃ ca svajane bhavet 
putrāḥ pitṛṣu jīvatsu mriyante ca tadagrataḥ  BhS 
kalau kākiṇike 'pyarthe vigṛhya tyaktasauhṛdāḥ 
tyakṣyantihi priyān prāṇān haniṣyanti svabāndhavān  BhS 
pāṣaṇḍapracuredharme dasyuprāyeṣu rājasu 
cauryānṛtavṛdhāhiṃsānānāvṛttiṣu vai nṛṣu  BhS 
śūdraprāyeṣu varṇeṣu chāgaprāyeṣu goṣu ca 
kariṣyanti tathā śūdrāḥ pravrajyāliṅginau'dhamāḥ  BhS 
kāṣāyaparinītāśca jaṭilā bhakmadhūsarāḥ 
aśaucāvakramatayaḥ parapākānnajīvinaḥ  BhS 
devadvijanivāseṣu pūjāmicchanti pāpinaḥ 
bhaviṣyanti durātmānaḥ śūdrāḥ pravrajitās tathā  BhS 
utkoca jīvinastatra mahāpāparatāstathā 
bhaviṣyantyatha pāṣaṇḍāḥ kāpālā bhikṣavodhamāḥ  BhS 
dharmavidhvaṃsaśīlānāṃ dvijanāṃ rājavallabhāḥ 
śūdrā dharmān pravakṣyanti pravrajyāliṅgino 'dhamāḥ  BhS 
gītavādyaparā viprā vedavādaparāṅmukhāḥ 
bhaviṣyanti kalau prāpte śūdramārga pravartinaḥ  BhS 
hartāro na ca dātārobhaviṣyanti kalau yuge 
viśvāsahīnāḥ piśunā vedadevadvijātiṣu  BhS 
asaṃskṛto ktivaktāro rāgadveṣaparāstathā 
paramāyuścateṣāṃ syāttadā varṣāṇi ṣoḍaśa  BhS 
pañcame vāthaḥvaṣṭhe vā varṣekanyā prasūyate 
sartpavarṣāṣṭavarṣāśca prasūyante tathā narāḥ  BhS 
svakarmatyāginassarve kṛtaghnā bhinnavṛttayaḥ 
yācakāḥ piśunāścaiva bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge  BhS 
parāvamānaniratā ātmastutiparāyaṇāḥ 
parasvaharaṇopāyacintakāḥ sarvadā narāḥ  BhS 
nindāṃ kurvanti satataṃ pitṛmātṛkuleṣu tu 
vadanti vācā dharmāṃśca cetasā pāpalolupāḥ  BhS 
chādayanti prayatnena svadoṣaṃ pāpakarmajam 
apāpe duṣkṛtaṃ samyagvivṛṇvanti narādhamāḥ  BhS 
dharmamārgapravaktāraṃ tiraskurvanti pāpinaḥ 
bhaviṣyanti kalau prāpti rājāno mlecchajātayaḥ  BhS 
dvijāśca kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāścānyāśca jātayaḥ 
atyantakāminassarve saṃkīryante parasparam  BhS 
na śiṣyo na guruḥ kaścinna putro na tathā pitā 
na bhāryā na patistatra bhavitā sarvasaṃkaraḥ  BhS 
kalau ca te bhaviṣyanti dhanāḍhyā api yācakāḥ 
rasavikrayiṇaścāpi bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge  BhS 
dharmapatnīṣu yacchanti patayo jāralakṣaṇam 
dviṣyanti pitaraṃ putrā guruṃ śiṣyādviṣanti ca  BhS 
patiṃ ca vanitā dveṣṭi kalau prāptena saṃśayaḥ 
lobhābhibhūtamanasassarve duṣkarmaśālinaḥ  BhS 
parānnalolupā nityaṃ bhaviṣyanti dvijātayaḥ 
parastrīniratāssarve paradravyaparāyaṇāḥ  BhS 
martyāmiṣeṇa jīvanti duhantaścāpyajāvikān 
sarittīreṣu kuddālairopayiṣyanti cauṣadhīḥ  BhS 
atyalpāni phalānyāsāṃ bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge 
veśyālāvaṇyaśīleṣu spṛhāṃ kurvanti yoṣitaḥ  BhS 
dharmavighnā bhaviṣyanti striyaśca puruṣeṣu ca 
na kanyāṃ yācate kaścinna ca kanyāprado naraḥ  BhS 
kanyā varāṃśca chandena grahīṣṭanti parasparam 
prāyaśaḥ kṛpaṇānāṃ ca bandhūnāṃ ca tadhā dvijāḥ  BhS 
sādhūnāṃ vividhānāṃ ca vittānyapaharanti ca 
na yakṣyanti na hoṣyantina tapasyanti vai janāḥ  BhS 
naiva dāsyanti dānādi nār'cayiṣyanti vā harim 
na dharme niviśiṣyanti hetuvādakathāśrayāḥ  BhS 
apātreṣveva dānāni kurvanti ca tathā narāḥ 
kṣīropādhinimittena goṣu prītiṃ prakurvate  BhS 
na kurvanti tathā viprāḥ snānaśaucādikāḥ kriyāḥ 
akālakarmaniratāḥ kūṭayuktiviśāradāḥ  BhS 
devanindāparāścaiva vipranindāparāstathā 
tyaktapuṇḍraśikhāsūtrāścariṣyantidvijātayaḥ  BhS 
viṣṇubhaktiparaṃ na syānmanaḥ kasyāpi jātu cit 
devapūjāparaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve parihasanti ca  BhS 
śāstroditāśca ye devāḥparivārā madhudviṣaḥ 
tān parityajya mohena narāḥ kālabalātkṛtāḥ  BhS 
hetuvādaparān devān kariṣyantyaparāṃ stadā 
nirbadhnanti dvijāneva karārthaṃ rājakiṅkarāḥ  BhS 
nādriyante dvijānanye kalau pāpasamākule 
dānayajña japādīnāṃ vikrīṇante phalaṃ dvijāḥ  BhS 
pratigrahaṃ ca kurvante caṇḍālāderapi dvijāḥ 
śūdrastrīmaṅganiratā vidhavāsaṃgalolupāḥ  BhS 
rajassvalānāṃ voḍhāro bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge 
śūdrānna pānaniratāḥ śūdraprāyā bhavanti ca  BhS 
aṭṭaśūlājanapadāḥ śivaśūlāścatuṣpathāḥ 
pramadāḥ keśaśūlinyo bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge  BhS 
kuhakāśca janāstatra hetuvādaviśāradāḥ 
pāṣaṇḍino bhaviṣyanti tiṣṭantyāśramanindakāḥ  BhS 
na ca dvijātiśuśrūṣāṃ sarvadharmanivartinīm 
gṛhaprāyeṣvāśrameṣu yogiprāyeṣu bandhuṣu  BhS 
tataśchānudinaṃ dharmassatyaṃ śaucaṃ dayā kṣamā 
kālena balinā sarvaṃ naśyatyāyurbalaṃ smṛtiḥ  BhS 
vīttameva kalau nṝṇāṃ janmācāraguṇodayam 
dāṃpatye 'bhirucirheturmāyaiva vyavahārake  BhS 
dharmanyāyavyavasthānāṃ kāraṇaṃ balameva hi 
strītvamevopabhoge svādvipratve sūtrameva hi  BhS 
liṅgamevāśramakhyātāvanyāyo vṛttikāraṇam 
avṛttau cāpi daurbalyaṃ pāṇḍitye cāphalaṃ vacaḥ  BhS 
svīkāra eva codvāhe snānamevāśucau smṛtam 
udaraṃbharitā svārthesatyatve dhārṣṭyameva hi  BhS 
dākṣye kuṭuṃbabharaṇe yaśorthe dharmasevanam 
itthaṃ kaliyuge prāpte dharmassarvo 'pi jīryate  BhS 
yadā māyānṛtaṃ tandrā nidrā hiṃsā viṣāyanam 
śoko moho bhayaṃ dainyaṃ sa kalistāmasaḥsmṛtaḥ  BhS 
yadāyadā satāṃ hānirvaidikānāṃ dvijanmanām 
tadā tadā kaliṃprāptamavabuddhyeta paṇḍitaḥ  BhS 
aho duḥkhamahoduḥkhamahoduḥkhamaho mahat 
svarūpamatibhīmasya saṃsārasya sudurbharam  BhS 
viṇmūtrapūyakalite garbhavāse nipīḍanāt 
aśucāvatibhībhatse duḥkhamatyantadussaham  BhS 
duḥkhaṃ ca jāyamānānāṃ gātrabhaṅgādipīḍane 
vātena preryamāṇānāṃ mūrchanāyātibhītidam  BhS 
bālake nirvivekānāṃ bhūtadaivātmasaṃbhavam 
yauvane vārdhake caiva maraṇe cāti dāruṇe  BhS 
ekauttaraṃ mṛtyuśataṃ dehe jñeyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam 
tatraikaḥ kālasaṃjñaḥ syāccheṣāstvāgantukāḥsmṛtāḥ  BhS 
ye cātrāgantukāḥ proktāste tu śāmyanti bheṣajaiḥ
